	I2-Sai3-A (23)
[1]	Tng Ou-se-a, Iok-than2, A-hap-su, Hi-se-ka, choe3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 e5 si5, A-mou5-su e5 kiaN2, I2-sai3-a sou2 tit-tioh8 lun7 Iu5-tai7 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 bek8-si7.
	2). ThiN ah, tioh8 thiaN, toe7 ah, tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 kong2, Goa2 bat iuN2-chhi7 kiaN2-ji5, poe5-iong2 in toa7-han3, in keng2-jian5 poe7-gek8 Goa2.  3). Gu5 bat i e5 chu2-lang5, lu5 bat i e5 chu2-lang5 e5 cho5; chong2-si7 I2-sek-liat8 m7-bat, Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 boe7 hiau2 siuN7.  4). Hai7 ah, hoan7-choe7 e5 kok, pe7-choe7 e5 peh-siN3, kiaN5-phaiN2 e5 cheng2-lui7, pai7-hoai7 e5 kiaN2-ji5; in li7-khui Ia5-ho5-hoa, khoaN3-khin I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5, kap I chhiN-sou, oat8-to3-tng2 khi3.  5). Lin2 tauh8-tauh8 poe7-gek8, si7 ai3 koh siu7 phah mah? Moa2 thau5-khak i2-keng thang3-thiaN3, moa2-sim soe-jiok8.  6). Tui3 kha-chioh-toe2 kau3 thau5-khak-teng2, bo5 chit8-te3 ho2-bah; long2 si7 siong-chhui3, ou-chhiN-cheng2, kap sin-phah e5 siong; long2 be7 u7 siu-chhui3, be7 u7 pau-bat8, ia7 bo5 eng7 iu5 lun7-tek8.  7). Lin2 e5 toe7 i2-keng pha-hng; lin2 e5 siaN5 siu7 he2 sio-hui2; lin2 e5 chhan5-hng5 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 hou7 goa7-pang lang5 sou2 chhim-thun; i2-keng pha-hng, chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 goa7-pang lang5 sou2 pai7-hoai7-e5.  8). Chi2-u7 lau5 Sek-an siaN5, chhin-chhiuN7 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 chhau2-liau5, koe-a2-chhan5 e5 chhau2-chhu3, siu7 ui5-khun3 e5 siaN5.  9). Na7 m7-si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 lan2 lau5 tam7-poh8 chhun e5 peh-siN3, lan2 chiu7 i2-keng chhin-chhiuN7 Sou2-to-ma2, chhin-chhiuN7 Go5-mou5-lah8 chit8-iuN7.
	10). Lin2 Sou2-to-ma2 e5 koaN-tiuN2 ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7; lin2 Go5-mou5-lah8 e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 ka3-si7.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 hian3 hiah-choe7 che3-mih8 hou7 Goa2 u7 sim2-mih8 li7-ek? kang mi5-iuN5 e5 sio-che3 kap pui5 e5 cheng-siN e5 iu5, Goa2 i2-keng pa2-ia3 lah; gu5-kang2 e5 huih, iuN5-a2 e5 huih, soaN-iuN5-kang2 e5 huih, Goa2 long2 bo5 hoaN-hi2.  12). Lin2 lai5 tiau5-kiN3 Goa2, chi7-chui7 tui3 lin2 tho2 chit-e5, lai5 thun2-tah8 Goa2 e5 iN7 ah?  13). Boh8-tit koh hian3 khang-khang e5 le2-mih8; hiuN-liau7 si7 Goa2 sou2 iam3-ouN3--e5; geh8 e5 chhoe-it, an-hioh-jit8, tiau3-chip8 e5 chu7-hoe7, si7 kiaN5-phaiN2; siu2 giam5-siok-hoe7 Goa2 lun2-boe7-tiau5.  14). Lin2 tak8-geh8 e5 chhoe-it kap choeh-ki5, Goa2 e5 sim oan3-hun7, khoaN3 i choe3 tang7-taN3, hou7 Goa2 taN-boe7-khi2.  15). Lin2 kiah8-khi2 chhiu2, Goa2 beh ng bak8-chiu m7-khoaN3 lin2; lin2 choe7-choe7 ki5-to2, Goa2 ia7 m7-thiaN; lin2 e5 chhiu2 moa2-moa2 thai5 lang5 e5 huih.  16). Lin2 tioh8 soe2 lai5 ka-ki7 chheng-khi3; tui3 Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 tu5--khi3 lin2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2; soah lin2 e5 choe3-phaiN2;  17). hak8-sip8 kiaN5-ho2, chhe7 kong-peng5, chin2-kiu3 siu7 ap-che3-e5, ka7 bo5-pe7 e5 kiaN2 sin-oan, ui7 chiu2-koaN2-lang5 pian7-hou7.
	18). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 lai5, lan2 saN-kap pian7-lun7; lin2 e5 choe7 sui-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 chu-ang5, beh pian3-peh8 chhin-chhiuN7 seh; sui-jian5 ang5 chhin-chhiuN7 ian-chi, beh peh8 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-mng5.  19). Lin2 na7 kam-sim thiaN-than3, beh tit-tioh8 chiah8 toe7-chiuN7 e5 ho2-mih8.  20). Na7 m7 thiaN-than3, hoan2-tng2 poe7-gek8, beh siu7 to-kiam3 thun-biat8; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhin-chhui3 kong2 i.
	21). Hai7 ah, tiong-sin3 e5 siaN5 piN3-choe3 chhiong-ki; chiong5-cheng5 chhiong-moa2 kong-peng5, kong-gi7 tiam3 hit lai7-bin7; hian7-kim si7 hiong-siu2 khia7-khi2.  22). Li2 e5 gun5 piN3-choe3 che-tai2; li2 e5 chiu2 thau3-chui2.  23). Li2 e5 koaN-tiuN2 hoan7-hoat, kap chhat8 tau3-phoaN7; tak8-e5 ai3 siu7 pou3-lou7, siau3-siuN7 sia7-le2; in bo5 ui7-tioh8 bo5-pe7 e5 kiaN2 sin-oan, chiu2-koaN2 lang5 e5 an3-kiaN7 boe7 tit-tioh8 kau3 i e5 bin7-cheng5.
	24). In-ui7 an2-ni, Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 eng-hiong5--e5 kong2, Houh, Goa2 beh tu5 Goa2 e5 kiu5-siu5, hou7 ka-ki7 khah-oe7 an-tit; beh tui3 Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 lai5 po3-siu5.  25). Goa2 beh koh he7-chhiu2 ti7 li2 e5 sin-chiuN7, it-chin7 thoan3-lian7 li2 e5 che-tai2, tu5-chheng li2 e5 chap8-chit.  26). Goa2 beh koh siat-lip8 li2 e5 sim2-phoaN3-koaN chhin-chhiuN7 khi2-thau5, siat-lip8 li2 e5 bou5-su7 chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-jit8; jian5-au7 li2 beh chheng-choe3 kong-gi7 e5 siaN5, tiong-sin3 e5 siaN5.  27). Sek-an beh in-ui7 kong-peng5 tit-tioh8 kiu3-siok8; in to3-tng2-lai5 e5 lang5 beh in-ui7 kong-gi7 tit-tioh8 kiu3-siok8.  28). Poe7-gek8--e5 kap hoan7-choe7--e5 beh choe3 chit8-e7 pai7-hoai7; pang3-sak Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5, tek-khak siau-biat8.  29). Hiah e5 lang5 beh in-ui7 lin2 sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 siong7-chhiu7 lai5 lau3-khui3; lin2 beh in-ui7 sou2 keng2 e5 hng5 lai5 kian3-siau3.  30). In-ui7 lin2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 hioh8 ta--khi3 e5 siong7-chhiu7; beh chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 chui2 e5 hng5.  31). U7 koan5-se3-e5 beh chhin-chhiuN7 moa5-sut, i e5 sou2-choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 he2-chhiN; long2 choe3 chit8-e7 toh8, bo5 lang5 phah-hoa.

[2]	A-mou5-su e5 kiaN2 I2-sai3-a sou2 tit-tioh8 lun7 Iu5-tai7 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 bek8-si7.
	2). Kau3 hiah e5 jit8 e5 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa tian7 e5 soaN beh kian3-lip8 ti7 chiah e5 soaN e5 teng2-bin7, poaN5-ke3 long2-chong2 e5 soaN-nia2; ban7-kok long2 beh lai5 kui i.  3). U7 choe7-choe7 kok e5 peh-siN3 beh khi3, kong2, Lai5 ah, lan2 chiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 soaN, kau3 Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 e5 tian7; I beh eng7 I e5 to7-lou7 ka3-si7 lan2, lan2 iah8 beh kiaN5 I e5 lou7; in-ui7 lut8-hoat beh tui3 Sek-an chhut, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 beh tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 thoan5-pou3.  4). I beh ti7 liat8-kok-tiong lai5 sim2-phoaN3, ui7-tioh8 choe7-choe7 peh-siN3 lai5 kai2-koat; in beh chiong in e5 to phah-choe3 loe5-thau5, chiong in e5 chhiuN phah-choe3 liam5-a2; chit-kok bo5 kiah8-to kong-kek hit-kok, in iah8 bo5 koh hak8-sip8 kau-chian3.
	5). Nga2-kok e5 ke ah, tioh8 lai5, lan2 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 kng-beng5-tiong lai5 kiaN5.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa, Li2 u7 pang3-sak Li2 e5 peh-siN3, Nga2-kok e5 ke, in-ui7 in chhiong-moa2 tang-hng e5 hong-siok8, kiaN5 sia5-sut8 e5, chhin-chhiuN7 Hui-li7-su7 lang5; ia7 kap goa7-pang lang5 kiat-iok.  7). I e5 toe7 u7 kim-gun5 moa2-moa2, i e5 chai5-po2 boe7-sng3--tit; i e5 toe7 u7 be2 moa2-moa2, i e5 chhia ia7 boe7-sng3--tit.  8). I e5 toe7 u7 ngou2-siong7 moa2-moa2, in kui7-pai3 ka-ki7 chhiu2 sou2-cho7--e5, chiu7-si7 ka-ki7 e5 chng2-thau5-a2 sou2-choe3-e5.  9). Pi-chian7--e5 khut-loh8, chun-kui3--e5 kang3-ke7; Li2 boh8-tit sia3-bian2 i.  10). Li2 tioh8 jip8 chioh8-tong7, bih ti7 thou5--nih, siam2-pi7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hian2-hek kap I ui-giam5 e5 eng5-kng.  11). Kau3 hit-jit8, bak8-thau5 koaiN5 e5 lang5 beh kang3 choe3 ke7, kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 beh siu7 khut-loh8, tok8-tok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa chi3-chun bu5-tui3.
	12). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 chit8-jit8 beh kong-kek it-chhe3 kiau-ngou7 chu7-ko--e5, kap it-chhe3 seng-koaiN5--e5, long2 kang3 choe3-ke7;  13). koh kong-kek Li7-pa-lun3 it-chhe3 koaiN5-toa7 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7, kap Pa-san it-chhe3 e5 siong7-chhiu7;  14). koh kong-kek it-chhe3 e5 koaiN5-soaN, kap it-chhe3 toa7 e5 soaN-nia2.  15). Koh kong-kek it-chhe3 e5 koaiN5-tai5, kap it-chhe3 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5;  16). koh kong-kek Tha-si it-chhe3 e5 chun5-chiah, kap it-chhe3 thang i3-ai3 sui2 e5 mih8.  17). Kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 beh siu7 khut-loh8, chu7-ko e5 lang5 beh kang3 choe3-ke7; ti7 hit-jit8 tok8-tok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa chi3-chun bu5-tui3.  18). Ngou2-siong7 beh choe3 chit8-e7 bo5--khi3.  19). Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2--lai5, hou7 toe7 toa7 tin2-tang7 e5 si5, lang5 chiu7 jip8 chioh8-tong7, jip8 thou5-khang, siam2-pi7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hian2-hek, kap I ui-giam5 e5 eng5-kng.  20). Kau3 hit-jit8 lang5 beh chiong sou2-cho7 lai5 pai3 gun5 e5 ngou2-siong7, kim e5 ngou2-siong7, hiat hou7 chhan5-chhu2 kap bit8-po5.  21). Kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2-lai5, hou7 toe7 toa7 tin2-tang7 e5 si5, lang5 beh jip8 chioh8-poaN5-phang7 kap soaN-tong7, siam2-pi7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hian2-hek, kap I ui-giam5 e5 eng5-kng.  22). Lin2 boh8-tit oa2-kho3 se3-kan lang5, put-ko3 u7 chit8-tiau5 khui3 ti7 phiN7-khang; thang sng3-choe3 sim2-mih8 ah?

[3]	KhoaN3 ah, in-ui7 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kap Iu5-tai7 tu5--khi3 in sou2 oa2-kho3 e5, sou2 i-oa2 e5, chiu7-si7 sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 bi2-niu5, sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 chui2;  2). tu5--khi3 iong2-su7, kap chian3-su7, sim2-phoaN3-koaN kap sian-ti, chiam-pok--e5 kap tiuN2-lo2;  3). ngou2-sip8-hu-tiong2 kap chun-kui3 e5 lang5, bou5-su7 kap khiau2 e5 sai-hu7, i2-kip8 gau5 kiaN5 hoat-sut8 e5.  4). Goa2 beh hou7 gin2-na2 choe3 in e5 leng2-siu3, hou7 eN-a2 koan2-hat in.  5). Peh-siN3 beh tai7-ke saN ap-che3, tak8-lang5 siu7 chhu3-piN e5 ap-che3; siau3-lian5 lang5 beh bu2-ban7 lau7-lang5, pi-chian7 e5 lang5 beh bu2-ban7 chun-kui3 e5 lang5.  6). Lang5 beh ti7 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, khiu2 i e5 hiaN-ti7, kong2, Li2 u7 i-hok8, tioh8 choe3 goan2 e5 koaN-tiuN2; chit-e5 to2-hoai7 e5 keng2-hong2, thang kui li2 e5 chhiu2 liau7-li2.  7). Hit-si5 i beh toa7-siaN kong2, Goa2 bo5 beh choe3 i-ti7 lin2 e5; in-ui7 goa2 e5 ke bo5 bi2-niu5, ia7 bo5 i-hok8; lin2 m7-thang siat-lip8 goa2 choe3 peh-siN3 e5 koaN-tiuN2.  8). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 soe-pai7, Iu5-tai7 to2-hoai7; in-ui7 in e5 chhui3-chih8 i2-kip8 kiaN5-choe3 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan2-tui3, jia2--tioh8 I eng5-kng e5 bak8-chiu.  9). In e5 bin7-sek kan-cheng3 ka-ki7 e5 bo5 cheng3-tit8; in kong2-khi2 ka-ki7 e5 choe7-ok, peng7-bo5 un2-moa5, chhin-chhiuN7 Sou2-to-ma2 chit8-iuN7.  In u7 chai-e7 ah, in-ui7 in ka-ki7 chhu2 chai-hai7.  10). Lun7 gi7-lang5 lin2 tioh8 kong2, I u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 beh chiah8 ka-ki7 kiaN5-choe3 sou2 kiat e5 ke2-chi2.  11). PhaiN2-lang5 u7 chai-e7 ah, i beh tu2-tioh8 chai-lan7; in-ui7 beh chiau3 i sou2-kiaN5-e5 siu7 po3-eng3.  12). Lun7-kau3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, gin2-na2 ap-che3 in, hu7-jin5-lang5 koan2-hat in.  Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, in2-chhoa7 li2--e5 hou7 li2 kiaN5 chha-chhok, koh hui2-hoai7 li2 sou2-kiaN5 e5 to7-lou7.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2-lai5 cheng-pian7, khia7-teh sim2-phoaN3 hiah e5 peh-siN3.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh sim2-mng7 I peh-siN3-tiong e5 tiuN2-lo2, kap in e5 leng2-siu3, kong2, chiah8-liau2 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 ke2-chi2-e5 chiu7-si7 lin2; tui3 song3-hiong lang5 sou2-chhiuN2-e5 long2 ti7 lin2 e5 ke.  15). Lin2 siaN2-su7 ap-che3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, sau3 song3-hiong lang5 e5 bin7-phe5? che si7 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kong2 e5.
	16). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh kong2, In-ui7 Sek-an hiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kiau-ngou7, kiaN5-lou7 am7-kun2 chhun tng5-tng5, khoaN3 lang5 sai2 bak8-be2, liam-kha kiaN5, kha-khoan5 khin-khiang hau2;  17). sou2-i2 Chu2 beh hou7 Sek-an hiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chhau3-thau5 kian-phi2; Ia5-ho5-hoa koh hou7 in chhiah-sin lou7-the2.  18). Kau3 hit-jit8, Chu2 beh tu5--khi3 in sui2 e5 kha-khoan5, thau5-mng5 bang7, geh8-chiam;  19). hi7-khoan5, chhiu2-soh8, ta3-bin7 e5 phe3;  20). hoe-bo7, kha-lian7, hoe-toa3, hiuN-ah8, hu5-te7;  21). chhiu2-chi2, phiN7-khoan5;  22). le2-hok8, goa7-tho3, phi-kian, ho5-pau;  23). chhiu2-kiaN3, iu3-toe7 saN, pau-thau5 e5 kun, jia seng-khu e5 phe3.  24). Beh u7 chhau3-khi3 lai5 thoe3 phang-bi7; soh-a2 lai5 thoe3 io-toa3; thau5-khak kng-kho7-kho7 lai5 thoe3 sui2 e5 thau5-mng5; moa5-pou3 ha5-io lai5 thoe3 sui2 e5 i-hok8; eng7 he2 e5 ku3-siong lai5 thoe3 i sui2 e5 bin7-mau7.  25). Li2 e5 ta-pou-teng beh to2 ti7 to-e7; li2 e5 iong2-su7 beh si2 ti7 chian3-tin7.  26). I e5 siaN5-mng5 beh pi-siong ai-kio3; i beh leng2-cheng7 che7 ti7 thou5-kha.

[4]	Ti7 hit-jit8 chhit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 beh khiN5 chit8 e5 ta-pou-lang5, kong2, Goan2 chiah8 ka-ki7 e5 bi2-niu5, chheng7 ka-ki7 e5 i-chiuN5; tok8-tok8 kiu5 li2 chun2 goan2 kui ti7 li2 e5 mia5, lai5 tu5--khi3 goan2 e5 kian3-siau3.
	2). Kau3 hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoat-siN e5 iN2 beh sui2 koh eng5-kng; thou2-toe7 e5 chhut-san2 beh choe3 I2-sek-liat8 to5-thoat e5 lang5 e5 eng5-kng the2-bian7.  3). Hoan7-na7 lau5 ti7 Sek-an, chun5 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ki3-chai3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 eng-kai tit-tioh8 oah8 e5 lang5 long2 beh chheng-choe3 seng3;  4). chiu7-si7 ti7 Chu2 eng7 sim2-phoaN3 e5 sin5, sio-hui2 e5 sin5, soe2-tu5 Sek-an cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 u3-oe3, chheng-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 tiong thai5-lang5 lau5-huih e5 si5.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ti7 Sek-an soaN pian3-toe7 kap i hiah e5 hoe7 e5 teng2-bin7, jit8--si5 khi2 hun5 kap ian, mi5--si5 u7 he2-iam7 e5 kng; in-ui7 ti7 long2-chong2 eng5-kng e5 teng2-bin7, tek-khak u7 jia-kham3.  6). Beh u7 teng5-a2, jit8--si5 thang choe3 im3-ng2 lai5 siam2-pi7 joah8, ia7 thang choe3 to5-siam2 bih sin e5 sou2-chai7, siam2-pi7 kong5-hong toa7-hou7.

[5]	Goa2 beh ui7-tioh8 goa2 sou2 chhin-thiaN3--e5 chhiuN3-koa, si7 goa2 sou2-thiaN3--e5 e5 koa, lun7 i e5 phu5-to5-hng5.  Goa2 sou2 chhin-thiaN3-e5 u7 phu5-to5-hng5; ti7 chin pui5 e5 soaN-thau5.  2). I khai-khun2 hit e5 hng5, tu5-khi3 chioh8-thau5, chai siong7-teng2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7, ti7 hng5-lai7 khi2 chit8 cho7 lau5, koh kut8 chiu2-khut ti7-hia, ng3-bang7 kiat ho2 e5 phu5-to5, bo5 phah-sng3 kiat ia2 phu5-to5.  3). Lin2 khia7-khi2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2--e5, kap Iu5-tai7 lang5 ah, taN chhiaN2 lin2 ti7 goa2 kap goa2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 tiong, phoaN3-toan3 tioh8 m7-tioh8.  4). Goa2 ui7 Goa2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 sou2-choe3-e5 i2-goa7, iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 thang choe3 ah? Goa2 ng3-bang7 kiat ho2 e5 phu5-to5, chaiN2-iuN7 hoan2-tng2 kiat ia2 phu5-to5 ah?  5). TaN Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2 Goa2 beh tui3 Goa2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 chaiN2-iuN7 kiaN5; Goa2 beh thiah--khi3 li5-pa, hou7 i siu7 thun-biat8; thiah-hui2 ui5-chhiuN5, hou7 i siu7 thun2-tah8.  6). Goa2 beh hou7 i hong-hoe3, bo5 koh siu-cheng2, bo5 koh thu5-thoaN2; hoan2-tng2 hoat chhi3-a2 kap chit8-le5; Goa2 ia7 beh beng7-leng7 hun5 bo5 loh8-hou7 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7.  7). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 phu5-to5-hng5 chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8-ke; I sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 chhiu7 chiu7-si7 Iu5-tai7 lang5; I sou2 ng3-bang7--e5 si7 kong-peng5, hoan2-tng2 u7 po7-giok8; sou2 ng3-bang7--e5 si7 kong-gi7, hoan2-tng2 u7 kio3 oan-ong2.
	8). U7 chai-e7 ah, hiah-e5 eng7 chhu3 chiap chhu3, eng7 chhan5 chiap chhan5, ti3-kau3 bo5 lau5 khang3-toe7--e5; chhun lin2 ka-ki7 khia7 hit e5 keng2-lai7.  9). Goa2 chhin-hi7 thiaN-kiN3 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Tek-khak u7 choe7-choe7 toa7 koh sui2 e5 chhu3-theh8 chiaN5-choe3 pha-hng, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  10). SaN-chap8 bou2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 chi2-u7 chhut chit8 pa-tek8 e5 chiu2; chit8 ho7-mui5-jiN2 e5 cheng2-chi2 chi2-u7 siu-seng5 chit8 i-hoat e5 bi2-niu5.
	11). Chai-e7 ah, hiah-e5 thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, hong3-chhiong3 lim kau7-chiu2, tit8-tit8 kau3 mi5 chhim, sim7-chi3 kau3 in-ui7 chiu2 hoat-kong5.  12). In ti7 ian5-toh toaN5-khim5 toaN5-sek, phah-kou2, pun5-tat8-a2, lim-chiu2, bo5 siuN7--tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sou2-kiaN5, iah8 bo5 liu5-sim I e5 chhiu2 sou2-choe3-e5.  13). Sou2-i2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 in-ui7 bu5-ti siu7 lang5 liah8-khi3; in chun-kui3 e5 lang5 chin iau-go7, kui-tin7 e5 peh-siN3 kek8-ki5 chhui3-ta.  14). In-ui7 im-kan khoah-toa7 i e5 sou2 ai3, khui i bo5 han7-liong7 e5 chhui3; in e5 eng5-kng, in e5 cheng3-lang5, in e5 chhia-hoa5, kap in tiong-kan khoai3-lok8 e5 lang5, long2 loh8 ti7 hit lai7-bin7.  15). Pi-chian7--e5 khut-loh8, chun-kui3--e5 kang3-ke7, bak8-thau5 koaiN5 e5 lang5 ia7 kang3-ke7;  16). chi2 u7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 sim2-phoaN3 lai5 chun-choe3 koaiN5, seng3 e5 Siong7-te3 tui3 kong-gi7 hian2-beng5 choe3-seng3.  17). Hit-si5 iuN5-a2 beh lai5 chiah8-chhau2 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 ka-ki7 e5 chhau2-tiuN5; pu3-lang5 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7, chhut-goa7 lang5 beh chiah8 i.
	18). U7 chai-e7 ah, eng7 hu-ke2 choe3 soh lai5 in2 choe7-ok, koh chhin-chhiuN7 eng7 thoa-chhia e5 soh lai5 khiu2 choe7-koa3.  19). In kong2, Goan7 I kin2-kin2 kiaN5, khoai3-khoai3 chiaN5 I e5 sou2-choe3, hou7 goan2 khoaN3-kiN3; goan7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 sou2 ke3-ek8--e5 pek-oa2 lai5, hou7 goan2 chai.
	20). U7 chai-e7 ah, hiah-e5 chheng phaiN2 choe3 ho2, chheng ho2 choe3 phaiN2, eng7 am3 choe3 kng, eng7 kng choe3 am3, eng7 khou2 choe3 tiN, eng7 tiN choe3 khou2 e5.
	21). U7 chai-e7 ah, hiah-e5 ka-ki7 khoaN3-choe3 u7 ti3-hui7, ka-ki7 khoaN3-choe3 thong-tat8--e5.
	22). U7 chai-e7 ah, hiah-e5 iong2-kam2 ti7 lim-chiu2, eng7 leng5-lek8 tiau-ho5 kau7-chiu2--e5.  23). In in-ui7 siu7 pou3-lou7 chiu7 chheng phaiN2-lang5 choe3 gi7, chiong gi7-lang5 e5 gi7 ka7 i chhiuN2--khi3.
	24). Sou2-i2 chhin-chhiuN7 he2-chih8 sio tiu7-ko2, ta-chhau2 loh8 ti7 he2-iam7-tiong, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni in e5 kun beh chhin-chhiuN7 hiu2-noa7 e5 mih8, in e5 hoe beh chhin-chhiuN7 tin5-ai pe--khi2-lai5; in-ui7 in khi3-sak ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 ka3-si7, khoaN3-khin I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 e5 oe7.  25). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 tui3 I e5 peh-siN3 hoat-choh, I e5 chhiu2 chhun-chhut kong-kek lai5 phah in; chiah e5 soaN-nia2 chiu7 io5-choah, in e5 sin-si ti7 koe-chhi7 chhin-chhiuN7 pun3-thou5.  Sui-jian5 an2-ni I e5 siu7-khi3 iau2-be7 siau, I e5 chhiu2 iau2 chhun--teh.
	26). I beh chhut ki5-ho7, chio hng7-hng7 e5 peh-siN3, chhut khau2-ho7 kio3 in tui3 toe7-kek8 lai5; khoaN3 ah, in beh kin2-kin2 chau2--lai5.  27). Ki5-tiong bo5 u7 ia3-sian7--e5, bo5 u7 poah8-to2--e5, bo5 u7 tuh-bin5--e5, bo5 u7 khun3--e5, io-toa3 ia7 bo5 pang3-sang, oe5-toa3 ia7 bo5 phah-tng7.  28). In e5 chiN3 chin-lai7, keng ia7 piN-an5; be2-toe5 chhin-chhiuN7 teng7 e5 chioh8, chhia-lun5 chhin-chhiuN7 kng2-le5-hong.  29). In beh hau2 chhin-chhiuN7 bu2 e5 sai, iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 soe3-chiah sai teh hau2; in beh hm7-hm7-hau2, lai5 lak8 in sou2 ka7 e5 mih8, thoa-kau3 un2-tang3 e5 sou2-chai7, bo5 lang5 oe7 kiu3 to3-tng2.  30). Hit-jit8 in beh tui3 in hm7-hm7-hau2, chhin-chhiuN7 hai2 hoa7-hoa7-hau2; lang5 na7 khoaN3 loh8 toe7, chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 u7 ou-am3 kan-khou2, kng-beng5 ti7 hun5-lai7 piN3-choe3 ou-am3.

[6]	Tng OU-se-a ong5 si2 hit-ni5, goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 Chu2 che7 ti7 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 po2-cho7, I e5 i-hok8 sui5-loh8 moa2-tian7.  2). Ti7 I e5 teng2-bin7 u7 se-lah8-peng kun-sui5 teh khia7; kok u7 lak8 e5 sit8, eng7 nng7 e5 sit8 jia-bin7, nng7 e5 sit8 jia-kha, nng7 e5 sit8 teh-pe.  3). Chit-e5 chhiuN3, hit-e5 ho7, kong2, Seng3--chai3, seng3--chai3, seng3--chai3, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa; I e5 eng5-kng chhiong-moa2 choan5-toe7.  4). Mng5-kheng in-ui7 chhiuN3-ho7 e5 siaN lai5 tin2-tang7; tian7 chiu7 u7 ian-hun5 moa2-moa2.  5). Hit-si5 goa2 kong2, Goa2 u7 chai-e7 ah, goa2 biat8-bo5 lah; in-ui7 goa2 si7 chhui3-tun5 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5, koh tiam3 ti7 chhui3-tun5 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 peh-siN3 tiong; in-ui7 goa2 bak8-chiu u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ong5, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  6). U7 chit8 e5 se-lah8-peng pe--lai5 oa2 goa2, i e5 chhiu2 theh8 jiat8-jiat8 e5 thoaN3, si7 eng7 he2-khiN5 tui3 toaN5-teng2 theh8--lai5-e5.  7). Chiong thoaN3 he7 ti7 goa2 e5 chhui3, kong2, KhoaN3 ah, chit-e5 he7 ti7 li2 e5 chhui3-tun5, li2 e5 choe7-koa3 chiu7 tu5--khi3, li2 e5 choe7-ok chiu7 sia3-bian2.  8). Goa2 koh thiaN-kiN3 Chu2 e5 siaN kong2, Goa2 thang chhe chi7-chui7 ah? chi7-chui7 beh ui7 Goan2 khi3? Goa2 chiu7 kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia, thang chhe goa2.  9). I kong2, Li2 khi3 ka7 chit e5 peh-siN3 kong2, Lin2 thiaN si7 beh thiaN, chong2-si7 boe7 beng5-pek8; khoaN3 si7 beh khoaN3, chong2-si7 boe7 hiau2--tit.  10). Hou7 chit e5 peh-siN3 sim tun7, hi7-khang tang7, bak8-chiu khoeh-bat8; bian2-tit in eng7 bak8-chiu khoaN3-kiN3, eng7 hi7-khang thiaN-kiN3, sim hiau2-ngou7, oat8-to3-tng2 lai5 tit-tioh8 i-ho2.  11). Goa2 chiu7 kong2, Chu2 ah, che beh joa7-ku2 ah? I kong2, Kau3 chiah e5 siaN5 pha-hng, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2, chhu3-lai7 bo5 lang5, thou2-toe7 kek8-ki5 pha-hng;  12). koh kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhian-soa2 hiah e5 lang5 kau3 hng7-hng7, chit e5 toe7 choe7-choe7 pang3-he7 teh.  13). Ti7 hit tiong-kan na7 iau2 chhun chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7, iah8 beh siu7 thun-biat8, chhin-chhiuN7 lek-chhiu7 siong7-chhiu7, sui-jian5 chho3--khi2-lai5, chong2-si7 chhiu7-thau5 iau2 lau5-teh; an2-ni u7 chit e5 seng3 e5 hou7-e3, chiu7-si7 hit e5 chhiu7-thau5.

[7]	OU-se-a e5 sun, Iok-than2 e5 kiaN2, Iu5-tai7 ong5 A-hap-su che7-ui7 e5 si5, A-lan5 ong5 Li7-sin3, kap I2-sek-liat8 ong5 Li7-ma2-li7 e5 kiaN2 Pi2-ka, chiuN7-lai5 kong-kek Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, chong2-si7 kong boe7-phoa3.  2). U7 lang5 ka7 Tai7-pit8 e5 ke kong2, A-lan5 kap I2-hoat-lian5 i2-keng hoe7-beng5; ong5 e5 sim kap peh-siN3 e5 sim long2 io5-tang7, chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-na5-lai7 e5 chhiu7 hou7 hong chhe tin2-tang7 chit8-iuN7.
	3). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 I2-sai3-a kong2, TaN li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2 Si-a-nga2-sut8 chhut-khi3 kau3 teng2 e5 ti5 e5 chui2-kau-khau2, ti7 phio3-pou3 sai-hu7 e5 chhan5 e5 toa7-lou7, ngia5-chih A-hap-su;  4). tui3 i kong2, Li2 tioh8 kin2-sin7 an-cheng7; boh8-tit in-ui7 chi2 nng7-ki chhut-ian e5 he2-pe2-thau5, chiu7-si7 A-lan5 e5 Li7-sin3 kap Li7-ma2-li7 e5 kiaN2, liat8 e5 siu7-khi3 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5 sit-taN2.  5). 	10). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh hoan-hu3 A-hap-su kong2,  11). Li2 tioh8 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kiu5 chit8 e5 tiau7-thau5; thang kiu5 i ti7 chhim-ian a2-si7 kek8-koaiN5 e5 thiN.  12). I2-sai3-a kong2, Tai7-pit8 e5 ke ah, lin2 tioh8 thiaN; lin2 hou7 lang5 ui5-lan5, kiam2 sng3-choe3 sio2-khoa2 su7, iah8 beh hou7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ui5-lan5 mah?  14). In-ui7 an2-ni, Chu2 pun2-sin beh hou7 lin2 chit8 e5 tiau7-thau5; khoaN3 ah, u7 chai7-sek-lu2 beh hoai5-in7 siN-kiaN2, ka7 i ho7-mia5 kio3 I2-ma2-loe7-li7.  15). Kau3 i oe7 hiau2-tit pang3-sak phaiN2, keng2 ho2 e5 si5, i chiah beh chiah8 lin-iu5 kap bit8.  16). In-ui7 ti7 chit e5 gin2-na2 iau2-be7 hiau2-tit pang3-sak phaiN2 keng2 ho2 e5 tai7-seng, li2 sou2 kiaN e5 hit nng7 e5 ong5 e5 toe7 beh tu2-tioh8 pang3-sak.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8 lim5-kau3 li kap li2 e5 peh-siN3, i2-kip8 li2 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, tui3 I2-hoat-lian5 li7-khui Iu5-tai7 i2-lai5, be7-bat u7 chit-ho7 e5 jit8, chiu7-si7 A-sut8 ong5 lai5.
	18). Hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chhut khau2-ho7, chio Ai-kip8 kang-ho5 e5 goan5-thau5 e5 hou5-sin5, i2-kip8 A-sut8 toe7 e5 phang.  19). Long2 beh pe--lai5, hioh ti7 pha-hng e5 soaN-kok, chioh8-phang7, kap it-chhe3 e5 chhi3-phe3, kap it-chhe3 e5 chhau2-tiuN5.  20). Hit-si5 Chu2 beh eng7 tui3 Ho5-goa7 kou3-chhiaN3 e5 thi3-thau5-to, chiu7-si7 A-sut8 ong5, lai5 thi3 in e5 thau5, kap kha e5 mng5; iah8 beh it-chin7 khun in e5 chhui3-chhiu.  21). Hit-si5 chit8-lang5 beh chhi7 chit8 chiah gu5-bu2, nng7 chiah mi5-iuN5-bu2.  22). Cheng5 hoan7-na7 chai chit8-chheng chang5 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7, tat8 chit8-chheng gun5, kau3 hit-si5 beh siN chhi3-phe3 kap chit8-le5.  24). [8]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 theh8 chit8 e5 toa7 e5 pai5, eng7 lang5 thong-heng5 e5 ji7 lai5 sia2, Lun7-khi2 Ma2-hek-jiN2-sa-lah8-lek8-hap-si-pa7-su.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tui3 goa2 kong2, Ka7 i ho7-mia5 kio3 Ma2-hek-jiN2-sa-lah8-lek8-hap-si-pa7-su.  4). In-ui7 chit e5 eN-a2 boe7 hiau2 kio3, A-pa, A-bu2, e5 tai7-seng, Tai7-ma2-sek e5 chai5-po2 kap Sat-ma2-li7-a siu7-chhiuN2 e5 mih8 long2 poaN ti7 A-sut8 ong5 e5 bin7-cheng5.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh tui3 goa2 kong2,  6). In-ui7 chit e5 peh-siN3 iam3-chian7 Se-lo5-a ban7-ban7 lau5 e5 chui2, hoaN-hi2 Li7-sin3 kap Li7-ma2-li7 e5 kiaN2;  7). sou2-i2 Chu2 beh hou7 hit e5 Ho5 chin-toa7 chin-hiong5 e5 chui2 lau5--lai5 im--in, chiu7-si7 A-sut8 ong5, kap i it-chhe3 e5 eng5-kng, beh poaN5-ke3 i it-chhe3 e5 chui2-kau, tiong3-moa2 i chiah e5 hoaN7;  8). beh chhiong-jip8 Iu5-tai7, tiong3-moa2 si3-koe3 im, koaiN5 kau3 am7-kun2; I2-ma2-loe7-li7 ah, i e5 sit8 thi2-khui, pian3-moa2 li2 e5 toe7.
	9). Liat8-kok e5 peh-siN3 ah, chhut-chai7 lin2 soan-hoa, kau3-be2 tek-khak pho3-hoai7; hng7 e5 lang5 ah, tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN; chhut-chai7 lin2 ha5-io, tek-khak beh pho3-hoai7, chhut-chai7 lin2 ha5-io, tek-khak beh pho3-hoai7.  10). Chhut-chai7 lin2 siat ke3-bou5, tek-khak kui khang-khang; chhut-chai7 lin2 gi7-lun7, tek-khak boe7 seng5-lip8; in-ui7 Siong7-te3 kap goan2 ti7-teh.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2 chi2-si7 goa2 eng7 oe7 keng2-kai3 goa2, kong2, M7-thang kiaN5 chit e5 peh-siN3 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7, tui3 goa2 kong2,  12). I beh choe3 seng3-sou2; iah8 beh ng3 I2-sek-liat8 nng7-ke choe3 poah8-to2 lang5 e5 chioh8, that-gai7 lang5 e5 chioh8-poaN5; ng3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, choe3 oah8-tauh kap lo5-bang7.  15). 	16). Li2 tioh8 chiong kan-cheng3 e5 oe7 kng2 an5-an5, hong-bat8 lut8-hoat ti7 Goa2 hak8-seng e5 tiong-kan.  17). KhoaN3 ah, goa2 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hou7 goa2 e5 kiaN2, long2 si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, tiam3 ti7 Sek-an soaN-e5, sou2 eng7 choe3 tiau7-thau5 ki3-ho7, ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong--e5.
	19). Na7 u7 lang5 tui3 lin2 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 khi3 mng7 tang5-ki kap kiaN5 sia5-sut8--e5, in e5 siaN-im ki-ki kiuh8-kiuh8, gian5-gu2 soe3-soe3; tioh8 in3 kong2, Peh-siN3 kiam2 m7-tioh8 mng7 i e5 Siong7-te3 mah? kiam2 thang ui7 oah8-lang5 khi3 mng7 hiah e5 si2--e5 mah?  20). Lang5 tioh8 chiau3 lut8-hoat kap kan-cheng3 e5 oe7; na7 bo5 than3 chit e5 oe7 lai5 kong2, chiu7 boe7 tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3 cha2-khi2-si5 e5 kng.  21). In beh keng-ke3 chit e5 toe7 siu7 kan-khou2 siu7 iau-go7; iau-go7 e5 si5, sim-lai7 ka-ki7 siu7-khi3, chiu3-chou2 in e5 ong5, kap in e5 Siong7-te3,  22). kiah8-thau5 khoaN3 thiN, aN3-loh8 khoaN3 toe7, bo5 phah-sng3 it-chin7 si7 kan-khou2 ou-am3, kap thong3-khou2 e5 ou-am3, siu7 koaN2 ti7 ou-ou am3-am3 e5 lai7-bin7.

[9]	Chong2-si7 hit-e5 bat siu7 thong3-khou2 e5 toe7 bo5 koh tiam3-ti7 ou-am3.  Cheng5 Siong7-te3 hou7 Se-pou3-lun5 kap Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 toe7 siu7 khoaN3-khin, au7-lai5 chiu7 hou7 ian5-hai2 e5 lou7, Iok-tan3 e5 ho5-goa7, goa7-pang e5 Ka-li7-li7, tit-tioh8 eng5-kng.  2). KiaN5 ti7 ou-am3-tiong e5 peh-siN3 khoaN3-kiN3 toa7-kng; khia7-khi2 ti7 si2-im3 e5 toe7--e5, u7 kng chio3 in.  3). Li2 hou7 chit e5 kok-bin5 choe7-choe7 , iah8 ke-thiN in e5 hoaN-hi2; in ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 hoaN-hi2, chhin-chhiuN7 siu-koah e5 hoaN-hi2, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 pun sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8, hit-ho7 e5 khoai3-lok8.  4). In-ui7 i sou2 pe7 tang7 e5 taN, kap keng-thau5-teng2 e5 koaiN2, i2-kip8 ap-che3 i--e5 e5 thui5, Li2 long2 ka7 i at-chih8, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Bi2-tian5 e5 jit8 chit8-iuN7.  5). In-ui7 kau-chian3-tiong chheng7-kah e5 lang5 e5 kun-chong, kap ko7 ti7 huih-lai7 e5 saN long2 beh siu7 sio, choe3 hiaN5-he2 e5 chha5.  6). In-ui7 u7 chit8 e5 eN-a2 ui7 lan2 lai5 chhut--si3, u7 chit8 e5 kiaN2 siuN2-su3 lan2; i beh hu7-tam kok-cheng3, i e5 mia5 chheng-choe3 Ki5-biau7, Bo5-su7, Choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3, Eng2-oan2 ti7-teh e5 Pe7, Ho5-peng5 e5 Jin5-kun.  7). I e5 kok-cheng3 kap peng5-an beh ke-thiN bu5-kiong5-chin7, chiu7-si7 ti7 Tai7-pit8 e5 po2-cho7 kap i e5 kok, beh eng7 sim2-phoaN3 kong-gi7 lai5 kian3-lip8 i, po2-hou7 i, tui3 taN kau3 eng2-oan2.  Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 jiat8-sim beh chiaN5 chit e5 su7.
	8). Chu2 hoat-chhut chit8-ku3-oe7 hou7 Nga2-kok ke, hit e5 oe7 iah8 lim5-kau3 I2-sek-liat8 chok8.  9). Chit e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 I2-hoat-lian5 kap khia7-khi2 ti7 Sat-ma2-li7-a--e5, long2 beh chai; in chiau3 in kiau-ngou7 chu7-toa7 e5 sim kong2,  10). Chng-phiah8 i2-keng to2, goan2 beh phah-chioh8 lai5 khi2; sng-chai5-chhiu7 i2-keng chho3, goan2 beh eng7 pek-hiuN-chhiu7 lai5 thoe3-oaN7.  11). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh khi2 Li7-sin3 e5 tui3-tek8 lai5 kong-kek i, iah8 beh kek-tong7 i e5 tui3-tek8;  12). tang u7 A-lan5 lang5, sai u7 Hui-li7-su7 lang5; in khui-chhui3 thun-chiah8 I2-sek-liat8.  Sui-jian5 an2-ni, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 iau2-be7 siau, I e5 chhiu2 iau2-ku2 chhun-teh.
	13). Chit e5 peh-siN3 iu5-goan5 bo5 kui-ng3 phah in e5 Chu2, iah8 bo5 chhe7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  14). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 chit8-jit8 e5 tiong-kan beh tui3 I2-sek-liat8 cham7-tng7 thau5 kap be2, chang-chhiu7-ki kap lou5-ui2.  15). Lau7-toa7 kap chun-kui3 e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 thau5, eng7 peh8-chhat8-oe7 ka3-si7 lang5 e5 sian-ti chiu7-si7 be2.  16). In-ui7 in2-chhoa7 chit e5 peh-siN3--e5, hou7 in kiaN5 chha-lou7; hou7 in in2-chhoa7--e5 long2 siu7 thun-biat8.  17). Sou2-i2 Chu2 bo5 hoaN-hi2 in e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, iah8 bo5 beh lin5-bin2 in e5 kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7; in-ui7 tak8-lang5 si7 siat-tok8--e5, si7 kiaN5-phaiN2--e5, koh tak8-lang5 e5 chhui3 long2 si7 kong2 gong7-oe7.  Sui-jian5 an2-ni, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 iau2-be7 siau, I e5 chhiu2 iu5-goan5 chhun--teh.
	18). In-ui7 sia5-ok chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8 sio-biat8 chhi3-phe3 kap chit8-le5; koh toh8 ti7 am7-am7 e5 chhiu7-na5, chiaN5-choe3 ian-thiau7, tng2-seh8 chheng3-chiuN7 koaiN5.  19). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toa7 siu7-khi3, toe7 pian3-pian3 siu7-sio; peh-siN3 chiaN5-choe3 he2-toh8 e5 chha5; hiaN-ti7 bo5 saN kho2-lin5.  20). Lang5 chiaN3-peng5 chhiuN2-theh8, iu5-goan5 si7 iau; to3-peng5 thun-ka7, iu5-goan5 boe7 pa2; tak8-lang5 ka7 i ka-ki7 chhiu2-kut e5 bah.  21). Ma2-na2-se kong I2-hoat-lian5, I2-hoat-lian5 kong Ma2-na2-se; nng7 chok8 hap8 kong Iu5-tai7.  Sui-jian5 an2-ni, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 iau2-be7 siau, I e5 chhiu2 iau2-ku2 chhun--teh.

[10]	U7 chai-e7 ah, hiah e5 siat-lip8 put-gi7 e5 lut8-le7--e5, kap ki3-chai3 kan-cha3 e5 phoaN3-su5 e5;  2). ong2-khut song3-hiong lang5 e5 an3-kiaN7, chhiuN2-toat8 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3-tiong khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 e5 cheng5-li2, eng7 koaN2-hu7 chun2-choe3 sou2-chhiuN2 e5 mih8, eng7 kou-ji5 chun2-choe3 sou2 kiap e5 mih8.  3). Tng kang3 heng5-hoat8 e5 jit8, u7 chai-e7 tui3 hng7-hng7 lim5-kau3, hit-si5 lin2 beh chaiN2-iuN7? lin2 beh chau2--khi3 kiu5 sim2-mih8 lang5 kiu3--lin2 ah? lin2 e5 chai5-po2 beh lau5 ti7 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7?  4). In chi2-u7 khut-sin ti7 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 e5 e7-bin7, to2 ti7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 e5 e7-bin7.  Sui-jian5 an2-ni, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 iau2-be7 siau, I e5 chhiu2 iu5-goan5 chhun--teh.
	5). U7 chai-e7 ah, A-sut8 si7 Goa2 siu7-khi3 e5 thui5, chhiu2-tiong kiah8 Goa2 e5 thong3-hun7 choe3 koaiN2.  6). Goa2 beh chhe i kong-kek sia5-ok e5 pang-kok, hoan-hu3 i kong-kek Goa2 sou2 siu7-khi3 e5 peh-siN3, chhiuN2 i sou2 chhiuN2--e5, liah8 i sou2-liah8--e5, chiong in thun2-tah8 chhin-chhiuN7 koe-lou7 e5 thou5-be5 chit8-iuN7.  7). Chong2-si7 i m7-si7 chit-ho7 i3-su3, i-e5 sim iah8 m7-si7 chit e5 taN2-sng3; i e5 sim-lai7 hoan2-tng2 siuN7 hui2-biat8, chau5-biat8 choe7-choe7 kok.  8). In-ui7 i kong2, Goa2 e5 jin5-sin5 kiam2 bo5 long2 si7 ong5 mah?  9). Ka-lek8-lo5 kiam2-m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Ka-ki-bi2-si mah? Hap-ma2 kiam2-m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 A-ni2-poat8 mah? Sat-ma2-li7-a kiam2-m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Tai7-ma2-sek mah?  10). Goa2 e5 chhiu2 i2-keng kau3 ngou2-siong7 e5 kok, in tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7 iaN5-ke3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kap Sat-ma2-li7-a e5 ngou2-siong7;  11). goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 Sat-ma2-li7-a kap ki5-tiong e5 ngou2-siong7, kiam2 boe7 chiau3 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kap ki5-tiong e5 ngou2-siong7 mah?
	12). Chu2 ti7 Sek-an soaN kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiaN5 I it-chhe3 sou2-choe3--e5 e5 si5, kong2, Goa2 beh heng5-hoat8 A-sut8 ong5 sim-kiau e5 kiaN5-choe3, kap i bak8-thau5 koaiN5 e5 eng5-kng.  13). In-ui7 i kong2, Goa2 sou2 chiaN5 e5 su7, si7 eng7 goa2 e5 chhiu2 e5 leng5-lek8, kap goa2 e5 ti3-hui7; goa2 pun2 u7 chhang-mia5; goa2 i5-soa2 liat8-kok e5 toe7-kai3, chhiuN2 in e5 chai5-po2, koh goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 iong2-su7 hou7 che7 koaiN5-ui7-e5 kang3 choe7 ke7.  14). Goa2 e5 chhiu2 theh8-tioh8 liat8-kok e5 chai5-po2, chhin-chhiuN7 theh8 chiau2-a2-siu7; goa2 tit-tioh8 choan5-toe7, chhin-chhiuN7 khioh-tioh8 sou2 pang3-sak e5 chiau2-a2-nng7; bo5 u7 phiat8-sit8 e5, bo5 u7 khui-chhui3 e5, bo5 u7 hau2-kio3 e5.
	15). TaN pou2-thau5 kiam2 oe7 tui3 eng7 i lai5 chho3-chha5--e5 ka-ki7 khoa-khau2 mah? ku3-a2 kiam2 oe7 tui3 hit e5 thoa ku3--e5 ka-ki7 phin2-phong2 mah? che si7 chhin-chhiuN7 thui5-a2 un7-choan2 hit e5 kiah8--i-e5, chhin-chhiuN7 koaiN2-a2 kiah8-khi2 hit e5 m7-si7 chha5--e5.  16). In-ui7 an2-ni Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Chu2, beh hou7 i pui5-e5 piN3-choe3 san2; ti7 i eng5-kng e5 e7-bin7 beh u7 he2 toh8--khi2-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 he2 sio chit8-iuN7.  17). I2-sek-liat8 e5 kng beh choe3 he2, i e5 Seng3--e5 beh choe3 he2-iam7; ti7 chit8-jit8 e5 tiong-kan, chiong i e5 chhi3-phe3 kap chit8-le5 sio liau2-liau2.  18). Koh chiong i e5 chhiu7-na5 kap pui5-toe7 e5 eng5-kng, tui3 sin5-hun5 kau3 jiok8-the2, long2 sio-biat8 i; se3-bin7 chhin-chhiuN7 phoa3-piN7 lang5 chiam7-chiam7 soe-pai7.  19). I e5 chhiu7-na5 chhun e5 chhiu7 bo5 kui2 chang5, gin2-na2 iah8 oe7 ki3 i e5 siau3-giah8.
	20). Kau3 hit-jit8 I2-sek-liat8 sou2 chhun-e5, kap Nga2-kok ke sou2 to5-thoat-e5, bo5 koh oa2-kho3 hit e5 phah in e5; si7 beh seng5-sit8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5.  21). Sou2-chhun-e5 beh to3-tng2-lai5, chiu7-si7 Nga2-kok ke sou2-chhun-e5, kui ti7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3.  22). I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 e5 peh-siN3 sui-jian5 choe7 chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-soa, chi2-u7 chhun-e5 to3-tng2--lai5; soe-pai7 e5 su7 i2-keng tiaN7-tioh8, eng7 kong-gi7 lai5 chhiong-moa2.  23). In-ui7 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ti7 choan5-toe7-tiong beh kiaN5 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 biat8-bo5.
	24). Sou2-i2 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, an2-ni kong2, Khia7-khi2 Sek-an, Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, A-sut8 sui-jian5 eng7 thui5 phah lin2, koh chhin-chhiuN7 Ai-kip8 e5 khoan2, kiah8 koaiN2-a2 kong-kek li2, li2 m7-bian2 kiaN i.  25). In-ui7 koh tiap-a2-ku2 siu7-khi3 chiu7 beh beng5-pek8, koh Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 beh tui3 in e5 biat8-bo5 lai5 soah.  26). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh kiah8-khi2 piN lai5 phah i, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Go5-lip8 e5 chioh8-poaN5 phah Bi2-tian5; I e5 koaiN2-a2 beh chhun ti7 hai2-teng2, I beh kiah8-khi2 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Ai-kip8 chit8-iuN7.  27). Kau3 hit-jit8 A-sut8 e5 tang7-taN3 beh li7-khui li2 e5 keng-thau5, i e5 taN beh li7-khui li2 e5 am7-kun2, i e5 taN ia7 beh in-ui7 boah-iu5 e5 ian5-kou3 lai5 hui2-hoai7.
	28). A-sut8 kau3 A-iap8, keng-ke3 Bi2-ki-lun5, pang3 heng5-li2 ti7 Bit8-boat8; in keng-ke3 ai3-khau2;  29). ti7 Ka-pa hioh-mi5; Lah8-ma2 lang5 kiaN-hiaN5; So3-lo5 e5 Ki-pi3-a lang5 to5-chau2.  30). Ka-lim5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 toa7-siaN au5-kio3; Lai5-soah e5 lang5 ah, tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang; chham2--ah, khun3-khou2 e5 A-na2-tut8 ah!  31). Ma2-tek-bi2-na2 lang5 siam2-pi7; Ki-peng3 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 to5-chau2.  32). Hit-jit8 i chat-peng ti7 Lo5-pek; pi2 chhiu2 ng3 Sek-an siaN5 e5 soaN, chiu7-si7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 soaN-thau5.
	33). KhoaN3 ah, Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, eng7 hou7 lang5 kiaN e5 ui-giam5 lai5 chho3 chhiu7-ki; tng5--e5 beh siu7-chho3, koaiN5--e5 beh kang3-ke7;  34). am7 e5 chhiu7-na5, I beh eng7 thih-khi3 chho3 i; koh Li7-pa-lun3 beh tui3 toa7 koan5-leng5--e5 lai5 to2--loh8-khi3.

[11]	Tui3 Ia5-se e5 chhiu7-thau5 beh hoat chit8 ki iN2, tui3 i e5 kun sou2 siN e5 ki beh kiat ke2-chi2.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sin5 beh tiam3 ti7 i, chiu7-si7 ti3-hui7 kap chhang-mia5 e5 sin5, ke3-ek8 kap leng5-lek8 e5 sin5, ti3-sek kap keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sin5;  3). i beh liah8 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 hoaN-hi2; i m7-si7 pin5 bak8-chiu sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 lai5 sim2-phoaN3, iah8 m7-si7 pin5 hi7-khang sou2 thiaN-kiN3 lai5 gi2-toan3;  4). i beh eng7 kong-gi7 sim2-phoaN3 song3-hiong lang5, eng7 cheng3-tit8 gi2-toan3 se3-chiuN7 khiam-pi e5 lang5; eng7 chhui3-tiong e5 koaiN2 phah se3-kai3, eng7 chhui3-tun5 e5 khi3 thai5-si2 phaiN2-lang5.  5). Kong-gi7 beh choe3 i e5 io-toa3, sin3-sit8 beh choe3 i e5 seng-khu e5 toa3.  6). Chhai5-long5 beh kap mi5-iuN5-a2 saN-kap toa3, pa3 kap soaN-iuN5-kiaN2 saN-kap to2--teh; gu5-a2 kap soe3-chiah sai kap pui5 e5 cheng-siN, choe3 soe3-han3 e5 gin2-na2 beh khan in.  7). Gu5 kap him5 beh saN-kap chiah8, in e5 kiaN2 beh saN-kap to2-teh; sai beh chiah8 chhau2 chhin-chhiuN7 gu5.  8). Chiah8-lin e5 gin2-na2 beh thit-tho5 ti7 ok-choa5 e5 khang-khau2; tng7-lin e5 gin2-na2 beh he7 chhiu2 ti7 tok8-choa5 e5 hiat8.  9). Ti7 Goa2 e5 seng3-soaN e5 pian3-toe7, tek-khak bo5 sun2-siong bo5 ham7-hai7; in-ui7 jin7-bat Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chai-bat beh chhiong-moa2 toe7-chiuN7, chhin-chhiuN7 chui2 im-moa2 ti7 iuN5-hai2.  10). Kau3 hit-jit8 Ia5-se e5 kun-thau5 khia7 choe3 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 toa7-ki5, liat8-pang beh kui-oa2 I; I an-hioh e5 sou2-chai7 u7 toa7 eng5-kng.
	11). Tng hit-jit8 Chu2 beh te7-ji7 pai2 chhun-chhiu2 kiu3-siok8 I e5 peh-siN3-tiong sou2 chhun--e5, tui3 A-sut8, Ai-kip8, Pa-thek-lo5, Kou2-sit8, I2-lan5, Si7-na2, Hap-ma2, kap cheng3 hai2-su7 to3--lai5.  12). I beh ng3 liat8-kok khia7 toa7-ki5, chio-chip8 I2-sek-liat8 siu7 koaN2-soaN3 e5 lang5, chu7-chip8 Iu5-tai7 si3-soaN3 e5 lang5, tui3 toe7 e5 si3-kek8 lai5.  13). I2-hoat-lian5 e5 oan3-tou3 beh siau-bo5, Iu5-tai7 e5 tui3-tek8 beh tu5-biat8; I2-hoat-lian5 bo5 beh oan3-tou3 Iu5-tai7, Iu5-tai7 bo5 beh tui3-tek8 I2-hoat-lian5.  14). In beh ng3-sai pe--khi3, phah ti7 Hui-li7-su7 lang5 e5 keng-thau5-teng2, saN-kap chhiuN2 tang-hng e5 lang5; chhun-chhiu2 ti7 I2-tong kap Mou5-ap; A-bun5 chok8 ia7 beh sun7-hok8 in.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 Ai-kip8 hai2 e5 kang2 ta--khi3; eng7 toa7-hong iat8 I e5 chhiu2 ti7 Toa7-ho5 e5 teng2-bin7, hou7 ho5 pun-choe3 chhit-tiau5, lang5 thoa-oe5 oe7--tit ke3--khi3.  16). Ui7-tioh8 I sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 tui3 A-sut8 chhun to3-lai5--e5, beh u7 chit8-tiau5 toa7-lou7 chhin-chhiuN7 tong-jit8 ui7-tioh8 I2-sek-liat8 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chiuN7-lai5--e5 chit8-iuN7.

[12]	Kau3 hit-jit8, li2 beh kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 beh kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 Li2 sui-jian5 bat siu7-khi3 goa2, taN Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 i2-keng soah, Li2 iah8 an-ui3 goa2.  2). KhoaN3 ah, Siong7-te3 si7 chin2-kiu3 goa2-e5; goa2 beh oa2-kho3 I, iah8 bo5 kiaN; in-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 khui3-lat8, si7 goa2 e5 si-koa; I iah8 chiaN5-choe3 kiu3-goa2--e5.  3). Lin2 beh tui3 kiu3-un e5 chui2-choaN5 hoaN-hi2 lai5 chhiuN7 chui2.  4). Ti7 hit-jit8 lin2 beh kong2, Tioh8 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kiu5-kio3 I e5 mia5, chiong I sou2-kiaN5--e5 po3-iong5 ti7 liat8-pang-tiong, kong2-khi2 I e5 mia5 i2-keng siu7 chun choe3-koaiN5.  5). Lin2 tioh8 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa; in-ui7 I sou2-kiaN5--e5 chin hian2-hek; goan7 chit e5 tai7-chi3 pian3-thoan5 ti7 thiN-e7.  6). Sek-an khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 chhut toa7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 ti7 lin2 e5 tiong-kan choe3-toa7.

[13]	A-mou5-su e5 kiaN2 I2-sai3-a sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 lun7 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 bek8-si7.
	2). Lin2 tioh8 ti7 kng-kho7-kho7 e5 soaN khia7 toa7-ki5, tui3 in chhut-siaN iat8-chhiu2, hou7 in jip8 kui3-chok8 e5 mng5.  3). Goa2 hoan-hu3 Goa2 sou2 keng2--chhut-lai5 e5 lang5, Goa2 i2-keng ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3, lai5 tiau3 Goa2 e5 iong2-su7, chiu7-si7 hiah e5 phin2-phong2 chu7-ko e5 lang5.  4). SoaN--nih u7 choe7-choe7 lang5 e5 siaN, chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-tin7 e5 peh-siN3, u7 choe7-choe7 kok e5 peh-siN3 chu7-chip8 hoa7-hoa7-hau2 e5 siaN; che si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa tiam2-choe5 kun-tui7, beh kau-chian3.  5). In tui3 hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5, tui3 thiN-piN lai5, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap kiaN5 I e5 siu7-khi3 e5 ke-si, beh hui2-biat8 chit e5 choan5-toe7.  6). Lin2 tioh8 ai-khau3, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 jit8-chi2 kun7--lah, chhin-chhiuN7 hui2-biat8 tui3 Choan5-leng5-e5 lai5.  7). Sou2-i2 long2-chong2 e5 chhiu2 beh nng2--loh8-khi3, cheng3-lang5 e5 sim beh siau-iuN5.  8). In beh kiaN-hiaN5; thang3-thiaN3 kan-khou2 beh khiN5-tioh8 in; in kiau-ka2 chhin-chhiuN7 beh siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5; tai7-ke gong5-ngiah8 saN-khoaN3, bin7 chhin-chhiuN7 he2-iam7 e5 bin7.  9). KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 jit8 lim5-kau3, beh u7 chan5-jim2, thong3-hun7, toa7 siu7-khi3; hou7 chit e5 toe7 pha-hng, tui3 hit tiong-kan tu5-biat8 u7-choe7 e5 lang5.  10). ThiN-teng2 e5 cheng3-chhiN liat8-siu3 long2 bo5 hoat-chhut kng, jit8-thau5 tu2-a2 chhut chiu7 pian3 ou-am3, geh8 iah8 bo5 hoat-chhut i e5 kng.  11). Goa2 beh in-ui7 sia5-ok heng5-hoat8 se3-kai3, in-ui7 choe7-giat8 heng5-hoat8 phaiN2-lang5; hou7 kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 e5 lam7-sam2 soah--khi3, ap-che3 kiong5-po7 e5 lang5 e5 chu7-ko.  12). Goa2 beh hou7 lang5 pi2 ho2-kim khah-chio2, hou7 lang5 pi2 O-hui e5 kim khah-chio2.  13). Sou2-i2 Goa2 beh hou7 thiN tin2-tang7, hou7 toe7 io5-choah, li7-khui i e5 pun2-ui7, chiu7-si7 ti7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 thong3-hun7 kap I toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 jit8.  14). In beh chhin-chhiuN7 siu7 tui-koaN2 e5 lok8, chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 lang5 chu7-chip8 e5 iuN5; tak8-lang5 to3--khi3 pun2-chok8, tak8-lang5 to5-chau2 kau3 pun2 sou2-chai7.  15). KiN3-na7 hou7 i tu2-tioh8-e5 beh siu7 chhak8-thang3, kiN3-na7 hou7 i liah8-tioh8-e5 beh hou7 to thai5-si2.  16). In e5 eN-a2 beh ti7 in e5 bak8-cheng5 hou7 lang5 siak-si2, in e5 chhu3 beh hou7 lang5 chhiuN2-toat8, in e5 bou2 beh hou7 lang5 leng5-jiok8.  17). Goa2 beh kek-tong7 Bi2-thai3 lang5 lai5 kong-kek in, in bo5 tui3-tiong7 gun5, iah8 bo5 ai3 tih8 kim.  18). In e5 keng beh phah-si2 i e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, bo5 lin5-bin2 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 thai-in7, in e5 bak8-chiu ia7 bo5 kho2-lin5 gin2-na2.  19). Pa-pi2-lun5 peng5-sou3 choe3 liat8-kok e5 eng5-kng, choe3 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 kiau-ngou7 e5 chng-thaN7, beh chhin-chhiuN7 Sou2-to-ma2 Go5-mou5-lah8 hou7 Siong7-te3 sou2 hui2-hoai7.  20). I e5 lai7-bin7 tek-khak eng2-eng2 bo5 lang5 toa3, tai7-tai7 bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2; A-lah8-pek lang5 bo5 ti7-hia tah pou3-piN5; kou3-iuN5 e5 lang5 iah8 bo5 hou7 iuN5-kun5 to2 ti7-hia.  21). Chi2-u7 khong3-ia2 e5 chau2-siu3 to2 ti7-hia, hm7-hm7-hau2 e5 siu3 moa2 chhu3-keng; to5-chiau2 tiam3 ti7-hia, ia2-soaN-iuN5 ti7-hia thiau3-bu2.  22). Chhai5-long5 beh hau2 ti7 i e5 iaN5-poaN5, soaN-kau2 beh hau2 ti7 i ian3-lok8 e5 kiong-tian7; i e5 si5 kun7--lah, i e5 jit8-chi2 bo5 ku2-tng5.

[14]	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh lin5-bin2 Nga2-kok, beh koh keng2 I2-sek-liat8, chiong in an-ti3 ti7 pun2 sou2-chai7, kia3-kha-e5 beh kui-oa2 in, kap Nga2-kok ke lian5-hap8.  2). Liat8-pang beh chiong in toa3-to3--lai5 pun2 sou2-chai7; I2-sek-liat8 ke beh ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toe7 tit-tioh8 in choe3 lou5-pok8 lu2-pi7, iah8 beh chhiuN2-liah8 cheng5 chhiuN2-liah8 in--e5, koan2-hat cheng5 ap-che3 in--e5.
	3). Tng Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 li2 thoat-li7 kan-khou2 hoan5-lo2, kap lang5 bian2-kiong2 li2 choe3 e5 khou2-kang, tit-tioh8 peng5-an e5 jit8,  4). li2 beh choe3 chit e5 koa lun7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, kong2, Che3-ap lang5-e5, chaiN2-iuN7 keng2-jian5 bo5--khi3! lek8-sek lang5 e5, chaiN2-iuN7 keng2-jian5 bo5-khi3!  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 at-chih8 phaiN2-lang5 e5 koaiN2, kap koan2-hat lang5--e5 e5 koan5-peng3,  6). chiu7-si7 ti7 siu7-khi3-tiong lian5-lian5 phah chiah e5 peh-siN3 e5, ti7 siu7-khi3-tiong koan2-hat liat8-kok, kiaN5 khun2-pek bo5 lang5 chou2-chi2 e5.  7). TaN choan5-toe7 tit-tioh8 an-hioh peng5-cheng7; lang5 long2 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.  8). Siong5-chhiu7 kap Li7-pa-lun3 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7, long2 in-ui7 li2 hoaN-hi2, kong2, Tui3 li2 to2--loh8-khi3, bo5 lang5 koh chiuN7-lai5 chho3 goan2.  9). Li2 loh8--khi3 e5 si5, im-kan chiu7 ui7 li2 tin2-tang7, lai5 ngia5-chih li2; koh in-ui7 li2 keng-tang7 hiah e5 bat ti7 se3-kan choe3 leng2-siu3 e5 im-hun5; iah8 hou7 hiah e5 bat choe3 liat8-kok e5 kun-ong5 e5 long2 tui3 i e5 cho7-ui7 khia7--khi2-lai5.  10). In long2 beh in3 li2 kong2, Li2 iah8 piN3-choe3 loan2-jiok8 chhin-chhiuN7 goan2 mah? li2 iah8 kap goan2 saN-chhin-chhiuN7 mah?  11). Li2 e5 ui-hong kap li2 e5 khim5-sek e5 siaN, long2 loh8 kau3 im-kan; phou ti7 li2 e5 e7-bin7--e5 si7 thang5, kham3 ti7 li2 e5 teng2-bin7--e5 si7 chhu.
	12). ThiN-kng-cha2 e5 khe2-beng5-chhiN ah, li2 chaiN2-iuN7 tui3 thiN tui7-loh8! li2 chit-e5 kong-phoa3 liat8-kok--e5, chaiN2-iuN7 siu7 kham2-to2 ti7 toe7-chiuN7.  13). Li2 e5 sim-lai7 bat kong2, Goa2 beh chiuN7-kau3 thiN-teng2, goa2 beh ku2-khi2 goa2 e5 cho7-ui7 ti7 Siong7-te3 cheng3-chhiN e5 teng2-bin7; goa2 beh che7 ti7 chu7-hoe7 e5 soaN, ti7 pak-hng e5 kek8-thau5.  14). Goa2 beh chiuN7-kau3 pi2 hun5 khah-koaiN5 e5 teng2-bin7; goa2 beh kap Chi3-koaiN5-e5 piN5-teng2.  15). Chong2-si7 li2 beh tui7-loh8 im-kan, kau3 chhim khiN e5 kek8-thau5.  16). Hoan7-na7 khoaN3-kiN3 li2-e5 long2 beh chu3-bak8 khoaN3 li2, liu5-sim siuN7 li2, kong2,  17). Hou7 toa7-toe7 io5-choah, hou7 liat8-kok tin2-tang7, hou7 se3-kai3 pha-hng, hou7 siaN5-chhiuN5 chhia-to2, bo5 thau2-pang3 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3--khi3 in tau, si7 chit e5 lang5 mah?  18). Liat8-kok e5 kun-ong5 long2 tak8-e5 u7 eng5-kng, khun3 ti7 i e5 bong7.  19). Tok8-tok8 li2 siu7 hiat-kak8, boe7 tit-tioh8 jip8 li2 e5 bong7, chhin-chhiuN7 thang iam3-chian7 e5 ki, eng7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 choe3 saN, chiu7-si7 siu7 to chhak8-si2, tui7-loh8 khiN-tiong chioh8-thau5 hit-ui7--e5; li2 koh chhin-chhiuN7 siu7 thun2-tah8 e5 sin-si.  20). Li2 boe7 tit-tioh8 kap in tang5 bai5-chong3, in-ui7 li2 pai7-hoai7 li2 e5 kok, thai5-si2 li2 e5 peh-siN3; phaiN2-lang5 e5 hou7-e3 tek-khak eng2-oan2 bo5-mia5.  21). In-ui7 chou2-kong e5 choe7, tioh8 pi7-pan7 thai5-si2 in e5 kiaN2-sun, bian2-tit in heng-khi2 lai5 chiam3-toe7, khi2 siaN5 pian3 se3-kan.  22). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh khi2-lai5 kong-kek in, beh tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5 tu5-biat8 i e5 mia5, kap sou2-chhun-e5, i2-kip8 i e5 kiaN2 i e5 sun; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.  23). Goa2 beh hou7 i e5 toe7 choe3 ho5-ti sou2 tiam3 e5 ui7, koh piN3-choe3 chui2-ti5; Goa2 beh eng7 biat8-bo5 e5 sau3-chiu2 sau3-tu5 i; che si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.
	24). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 sou2 siuN7-e5 koat-toan3 beh chiaN5; Goa2 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8-e5 koat-toan3 kian3-lip8.  25). Goa2 beh phah-pai7 A-sut8 lang5 ti7 Goa2 e5 toe7, thun2-tah8 i ti7 Goa2 e5 soaN; i e5 taN beh li7-khui Goa2 e5 peh-siN3; i e5 tang7-taN3 beh li7-khui Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 keng-thau5.  26). Che si7 i2-keng tiaN7-tioh8 beh kiaN5 ti7 choan5-toe7 e5 chi2-i3; che si7 chhun ti7 ban7-kok teng2-bin7 e5 chhiu2.  27). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng tiaN7-tioh8 chi2-i3, chi7-chui7 oe7 hoe3-bo5 i? I e5 chhiu2 i2-keng chhun-chhut, chi7-chui7 oe7 hou7 i kiu to3-tng2?
	28). A-hap-su ong5 si2 hit-ni5, u7 chit e5 bek8-si7.  29). Hui-li7-su7 e5 choan5-toe7 ah, boh8-tit in-ui7 phah li2 e5 koaiN2 i2-keng chih8 lai5 hoaN-hi2; in-ui7 tui3 choa5 e5 nng7 beh siN-chhut tok8-choa5, i sou2-siN-e5 si7 pe e5 he2-choa5.  30). Song3-hiong lang5 e5 toa7-kiaN2 beh tit-tioh8 chiah8, khiam3-kheh e5 lang5 beh an-jian5 to2-teh; Goa2 beh eng7 ki-hng go7-si2 li2 e5 cheng2-lui7, i beh thai5-si2 li2 sou2-chhun-e5.  31). Mng5--ah, tioh8 thi5-khau3; siaN5--ah, tioh8 au5-kio3; Hui-li7-su7 choan5-toe7 ah, li2 siau-bo5 lah; in-ui7 u7 ian tui3 pak--si3 lai5, i e5 peng-teng bo5 chit8-e5 lau3-tin7.  32). Beh chaiN2-iuN7 in3 liat8-kok e5 su3-chia2 ah? Tioh8 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kian3-lip8 Sek-an, I e5 peh-siN3-tiong khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 beh tau5-hioh ti7 hit lai7-bin7.

[15]	Lun7 Mou5-ap e5 bek8-si7.
	In-ui7 chit8-mi5 e5 tiong-kan Mou5-ap e5 A-jiN2 piN3-choe3 hong-hoe3, bo5--khi3; in-ui7 chit8-mi5 e5 tiong-kan Mou5-ap e5 Ki-jiN2 piN3-choe3 hong-hoe3, bo5--khi3.  2). I chiuN7 kau3 Pa-ek, koh khi3 Ti2-pun2, kau3 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 thi5-khau3; Mou5-ap lang5 in-ui7 Ni5-pho kap Bi2-ti2-pa ai-khau3, tak8-e5 thau5-khak kng-liu-liu, chhui3-chhiu thi3-liau2-liau2.  3). In ti7 koe-chhi7--nih io long2 ha5 moa5-pou3; ti7 chhu3-teng2 kap hit e5 khoan-khoah e5 sou2-chai7, tak8-lang5 long2 thi5-khau3, bak8-sai2 tit8-tit8 lau5.  4). Hi-sit8-pun2 kap I2-li7-a-li7, pi-ai e5 siaN thiaN kau3 Nga2-chap8; sou2-i2 Mou5-ap toa3 kun-khi3-e5 toa7-siaN hoah-hiam3; i e5 sim ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.  5). Goa2 e5 sim ui7-tioh8 Mou5-ap pi-ai; i e5 kui3-chok8 chau2 kau3 So2-jiN2, kau3 I2-ki-lah8 Si-li7-si-a; in chiuN7 Lou7-hi e5 lou7, na2-kiaN5 na2-hau2; ti7 Ho5-lo5-liam7 e5 lou7, in-ui7 hui2-biat8 chhut ai-khau3 e5 siaN.  6). In-ui7 Leng5-lim5 e5 chui2 beh ta--khi3; in-ui7 chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhau2 kou-ta5; ou-iu3 e5 chhai3-soe biat8-bo5, chhiN-chhui3 e5 mih8 long2 bo5--khi3.  7). In-ui7 an2-ni Mou5-ap lang5 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 chai5-but8 kap sou2 chek-chu7-e5, long2 beh toa3 ke3 liu2-chhiu7 khoe;  8). in-ui7 ai-chham2 e5 siaN pian3-moa2 Mou5-ap e5 si3-keng2, ai-khau3 e5 siaN thiaN kau3 I2-ki-lian5, ai-khau3 e5 siaN thiaN kau3 Pi2-jiN2-i2-lim5.  9). In-ui7 Ti2-bun5 e5 chui2 u7 huih moa2-moa2; Goa2 beh ke-thiN Ti2-bun5 e5 chai-lan7, hou7 sai lai5 tui-jip Mou5-ap to5-thoat e5 peh-siN3, kap hit sou2-chai7 sou2-chhun e5 lang5.

[16]	Lin2 tioh8 chiong iuN5-a2 hian3 hou7 toe7-hng chiang2-koan5--e5, tui3 Se-lah8 ng3 khong3-ia2, sang3 kau3 Sek-an siaN5 e5 soaN.  2). Mou5-ap khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ti7 A-loan2 e5 tou7-thau5, chhin-chhiuN7 si3-koe3 pe e5 chiau2, chhin-chhiuN7 thiah-phoa3 e5 chiau2-a2-siu7.  3). Li2 tioh8 siat ke3-bou5, kiaN5 kong-peng5, hou7 li2 e5 iaN2 ti7 tiong-tau3 e5 si5, chhin-chhiuN7 ou-am3 mi5; siu7 koaN2-tiok8 e5 lang5 hou7 i bih; to5-chau2 e5 peh-siN3 m7-thang ka7 i lou7-chhut.  4). Li2 tioh8 iong5-un2 Goa2 chiah e5 siu7 koaN2-tiok8 e5 lang5 kap li2 saN-kap tiam3.  Lun7-kau3 Mou5-ap, li2 tioh8 choe3 i siam2-bih e5 sou2-chai7, thoat-li7 chan5-hai7--e5 e5 bin7-cheng5; in-ui7 lek8-sek lang5-e5 kui ti7 bo5, hui2-biat8 e5 su7 soah--khi3, thun2-tah8 lang5--e5 tui3 kok-tiong tu5-biat8.  5). Beh u7 po2-cho7 in-ui7 chu5-ai3 lai5 kian3-siat, beh u7 seng5-sit8--e5 che7 ti7 hit teng2-bin7, ti7 Tai7-pit8 e5 pou3-piN5-lai7 teh sim2-phoaN3, kiu5 kong-peng5, kin2-kin2 kiaN5 kong-gi7.
	6). Goan2 thiaN-kiN3 Mou5-ap lang5 e5 kiau-ngou7, i kiau-ngou7 kau3-kek8; i e5 chu7-ko, i e5 kiau-ngou7, i e5 toa7 siu7-khi3; phin2-phong2 e5 oe7 si7 khang-khang.  7). Sou2-i2 Mou5-ap beh ui7-tioh8 Mou5-ap thi5-khau3, lang5-lang5 long2 beh thi5-khau3; lin2 beh ui7-tioh8 Kiat-jiN2 Hap-liat8-siat e5 phu5-to5-piaN2 lai5 thou2-khui3, siu7-phah chin siong-tiong7.  8). In-ui7 Hi-sit8-pun2 e5 chhan5 ta--khi3; Se-pi2-ma2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 iah8 si7 an2-ni; liat8-kok e5 chu2 at-chih8 i te7-it ho2 e5 ki, chiah e5 ki chhun kau3 Nga2-sia7, thoaN3 kau3 khong3-ia2; i e5 ki chhun-chhut poaN5-ke3 hai2.  9). Sou2-i2 goa2 beh ui7-tioh8 Se-pi2-ma2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 ai-khau3 kap Nga2-sia7 lang5 e5 ai-khau3 chit8-iuN7; Hi-sit8-pun2, I2-li7-a-li7 ah, goa2 beh eng7 bak8-sai2 koan3-ak li2, in-ui7 lin2 siu-seng5 ke2-chi2 kap gou7-kak e5 si5, hoah-hiam3 e5 siaN hut-jian5 kau3.  10). Tui3 pui5 e5 chhan5-tiong chhiuN2-khi3 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, ti7 phu5-to5-hng5 tek-khak bo5 chhiuN3-koa, iah8 bo5 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN; tah8-chiu2-e5 ti7 chiu2-khut-lai7 bo5 tah8-chhut chiu2; goa2 hou7 i hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN soah.  11). In-ui7 an2-ni, goa2 e5 sim-pak ui7-tioh8 Mou5-ap chhin-chhiuN7 khim5 chhut siaN, goa2 e5 sim-tng5 ui7-tioh8 Kiat-jiN2 Hap-liat8-siat iah8 si7 an2-ni.  12). Mou5-ap lang5 tiau5-kiN3 e5 si5, ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 ia3-sian7, koh kau3 i e5 seng3-sou2 ki5-to2, iah8 boe7 chiaN5.
	13). Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa cheng5 lun7 Mou5-ap sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.  14). Chong2-si7 hian7-chai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 kong2, SaN-ni5-lai7, chiau3 tng5-kang e5 ni5-han7, Mou5-ap e5 eng5-kng kap i e5 cheng3-lang5 beh tu2-tioh8 leng5-jiok8; sou2 chhun e5 lang5 chin-chio2, bo5 chiuN7-sng3.

[17]	Lun7 Tai7-ma2-sek e5 bek8-si7.
	KhoaN3 ah, Tai7-ma2-sek i2-keng siu7 hoe3--khi3, bo5 koh choe3 siaN5, tek-khak piN3-choe3 hau7-phiaN-phe3 e5 tui.  2). A-lo5-jiN2 e5 siaN5 i2-keng siu7 pang3-sak, tek-khak chiaN5-choe3 chhi7-iuN5 e5 sou2-chai7; iuN5 to2 ti7-hia, bo5 lang5 phah-kiaN in.  3). I2-hoat-lian5 e5 soaN-che7, Tai7-ma2-sek e5 kok-koan5, A-lan5 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3, long2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 eng5-kng bo5--khi3; che si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.
	4). Kau3 hit-jit8 Nga2-kok e5 eng5-kng beh soe-poh8, i e5 pui5 e5 sin-the2 beh siau-san2.  5). Chiu7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 siu-koah e5 lang5 siu gou7-kak, eng7 chhiu2 koah hiah e5 sui7; koh chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 ti7 Li7-hoat8-im e5 soaN-kok khioh beh8-seh.  6). In tiong-kan sou2 chhun--e5 bo5 loa7-choe7, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 kong2 kaN-na2-chhiu7, ti7 te7-it-koaiN5 e5 ki-be2, chi2-u7 nng7 saN liap8, ti7 ke2-chi2-chhiu7 chhun-hng7 e5 ki-be2, chi2-u7 si3 gou7 liap8; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 kong2 e5.  7). Tng hit-jit8 lang5 beh giong2-bong7 cho7-hoa3 i e5 Chu2, bak8-chiu beh koan-khoaN3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5.  8). In bo5 koh giong2-bong7 ka-ki7 e5 chhiu2 sou2 khi2 e5 che3-toaN5, bo5 koh koan-khoaN3 ka-ki7 e5 chng2-thau5-a2 sou2-cho7 e5 chha5-thiau7, a2-si7 jit8 e5 siong7.  9). Ti7 hit-jit8 in kian-kou3 e5 siaN5 beh chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-na5-lai7 kap soaN-be2-liu sou2 khi3-sak e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 in cha2-cheng5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 khi3-sak--e5; an2-ni toe7 chiu7 pha-hng.  10). In-ui7 li2 boe7 ki3--tit kiu3 li2 e5 Siong7-te3, bo5 ki3-liam7 choe3 li2 e5 khui3-lat8 e5 chioh8-poaN5; sou2-i2 li2 chai chin sim-sek e5 chhiu7-a2-chai, iah8 cheng3 pat8-iuN7 e5 cheng2.  11). Chai-cheng3 e5 jit8 li2 ka7 i ui5 li5-pa; kau3 cha2-khi2 si5, hou7 li2 sou2-cheng3-e5 khui-hoe; chong2-si7 ti7 iu-khou2 choat8-bang7 thang3-thiaN3 e5 jit8, sou2 siu-koah-e5 long2 pe-le--khi3.
	12). ThiaN ah, u7 choe7-choe7 peh-siN3 e5 siaN, in hoa7-hoa7-hau2 chhin-chhiuN7 hai2 e5 hoa7-hoa7-hau2; u7 liat8-kok e5 chau2-chong5, in chau2-chong5 chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-chui2 e5 chau2-chong5.  13). Liat8-pang chau2-chong5, chhin-chhiuN7 choe7-choe7 chui2 e5 chau2-chong5; chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 hoah in, in chiu7 chau2--khi3 hng7-hng7, koh siu7 tui-koaN2, chhin-chhiuN7 soaN-teng2 hong-cheng5 e5 chhou-khng, koh chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-hong thau5-cheng5 teh kng2 e5 mih8.  14). E5-hng si5 u7 kiaN-hiaN5; thiN iau2-be7 kng, in chiu7 bo5--khi3; che si7 chhiuN2 goan2 e5 lang5 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 hun7, si7 kiap goan2 e5 lang5 e5 po3-eng3.

[18]	Ha7 ah, Kou2-sit8 chiah e5 ho5-goa7, i e5 sit8 phiat8-phiat8 hau2 e5 toe7.  2). I chhe su3-chia2 ke3-hai2, che7 lou5-ui2 e5 chun5 ti7 chui2-bin7, kong2, Lin2 chiah e5 kin2-khoai3 e5 su3-chia2, tioh8 kau3 koaiN5-toa7 kng-kut8 e5 peh-siN3 hia, tui3 khai-kok i2-lai5, hiah e5 peh-siN3 kek8-ki5 thang kiaN, si7 pun toe7-kai3 thun2-tah8 lang5 e5, in e5 toe7 u7 kang-ho5 pun-khui.  3). Se3-chiuN7 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, kap tiam3 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 lang5 ah, soaN-teng2 khia7 toa7-ki5 e5 si5 lin2 tioh8 khoaN3, pun5 sau3-kak e5 si5 lin2 tioh8 thiaN.
	4). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 an2-ni kong2, Tng jit8-si5 u7 thiN-khi3 e5 iam7-jiat8, siu-koah e5 joah8-thiN u7 lou7-chui2 e5 hun5-bu7 e5 si5, Goa2 ti7 Goa2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 beh cheng7-cheng7 che7 teh-khoaN3.  5). Siu-koah e5 tai7-seng, hoe i2-keng khui sia7, hoe iah8 kiat-chiaN5 beh sek8 e5 phu5-to5, i beh eng7 liam5-a2 koah-khi3 nng2 e5 ki, koh beh chian2-tu5 am7-am7 e5 tin5.  6). Long2 beh hiat hou7 soaN-kan e5 eng-chiau2, kap toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3; he7-thiN e5 eng-chiau2 beh hioh ti7-hia, tang-thiN e5 ia2-siu3 long2 beh to2 ti7-hia.  7). Kau3 hit-si5 chit e5 koaiN5-toa7 kng-kut8 e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 tui3 khai-kok i2-lai5 kek8-ki5 thang kiaN, pun toe7-kai3 thun2-tah8 lang5 e5, in e5 toe7 u7 kang-ho5 pun-khui, in beh chiong le2-mih8 hian3 hou7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 hian3-kau3 Sek-an soaN, Ia5-ho5-hoa an-ti3 I e5 mia5 e5 sou2-chai7.

[19]	Lun7 Ai-kip8 e5 bek8-si7.
	KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa che7 kin2-kin2 e5 hun5 lim5-kau3 Ai-kip8; Ai-kip8 e5 ngou2-siong7 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah; Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 sim ti7 lai7-bin7 siau-iuN5.  2). Goa2 beh kek-tong7 Ai-kip8 lang5 kong-kek Ai-kip8 lang5, hiaN-ti7 kong-kek hiaN-ti7, chhu3-piN kong-kek chhu3-piN, siaN5 kong-kek siaN5, kok kong-kek kok.  3). Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 sim-sin5 beh ti7 lai7-bin7 sit-taN2; Goa2 beh pai7-hoai7 in e5 ke3-bou5; in beh kiu5 ngou2-siong7 kap liam7-chiu3--e5, choe3 tang5-ki e5, kiaN5 sia5-sut8 e5.  4). Goa2 beh chiong Ai-kip8 lang5 kau ti7 chan5-jim2 e5 chu2 e5 chhiu2, kiong5-po7 e5 ong5 beh koan2-hat in; che si7 Chu2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.
	5). Hai2-tiong e5 chui2 beh choat8-tng7, ho5-chui2 beh siau-bo5 ta--khi3.  6). Kang-ho5 beh piN3 chhau3-bi7, Ai-kip8 e5 ho5-chui2 beh kiam2-chio2, ta-la--khi3; lou5-ui2 kap lou5-tek long2 kou-ta5.  7). Ho5-piN kap Ho5-khau2 e5 chhau2-pou, i2-kip8 Ho5-piN sou2 chai-cheng3--e5 long2 kou-ta5, siu7 sau3-tu5 bo5--khi3.  8). Tho2-hi5--e5 beh thi5-khau3, pang3-tio3 ti7 Ho5--nih-e5 beh pi-siong; pha-bang7 ti7 chui2--nih-e5 beh soe-pai7.  9). Cheh iu3-toe7 e5, kap chit peh8-pou3 e5, long2 beh kian3-siau3.  10). Kok-ka e5 thiau7-chioh8 beh tu2-tioh8 phah-chhui3, sou2 u7 e5 chhiaN3-kang lang5 sim beh hoan5-lo2.
	11). So2-an e5 siu2-leng2 kek8-ki5 gu5-gong7; Hoat-lo2 toa7 ti3-hui7 e5 bou5-su7 sou2 ke3-ek8--e5 chiaN5-choe3 gu5-chhun2.  Lin2 thai2-tho2 kaN2 tui3 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Goa2 si7 ti3-hui7 lang5 e5 kiaN2-sun, goa2 si7 sian-ong5 e5 kiaN2-sun?  12). Li2 e5 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 ti7 toh-loh8? ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7 Ai-kip8 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 chi2-i3, in thang lai5 chai, thang ka7 li2 kong2 lah.  13). So2-an e5 siu2-leng2 long2 piN3-choe3 gong7, Lo5-hut e5 siu2-leng2 long2 siu7 be5-hek8; Ai-kip8 chi-phai3 chhu3-kak-thau5 e5 chioh8 chhoa7 i e5 peh-siN3 ti7 be5-lou7.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 koai7-biu7 e5 sin5 chham-jip8 ti7 in tiong-kan, ti3-kau3 in chhoa7 Ai-kip8 it-chhe3 sou2-kiaN5-e5 long2 chha-chhok, chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8-chiu2-chui3 e5 lang5 au2-thou3 e5 si5, tang-to2 sai-oai chit8-iuN7.  15). Ai-kip8 e5 tiong-kan, bo5-lun7 thau5 kap be2, chang-ki kap lou5-ui2 sou2 choe3 e5 kang, bo5 chit8-hang7 oe7 chiaN5.
	16). Kau3 hit-jit8 Ai-kip8 beh chhin-chhiuN7 hu7-jin5-lang5 chit8-iuN7, koh beh kiaN-hiaN5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, in-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 e5 bu2-lang7, chiu7-si7 I ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7 sou2 bu2-lang7 e5.  17). Iu5-tai7 toe7 beh choe3 Ai-kip8 sou2 kiaN-hiaN5 e5; kiN3-na7 tui3 i kong2-khi2 Iu5-tai7 toe7 i chiu7 kiaN-hiaN5; che si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 ti7 Ai-kip8 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 chi2-i3.  18). Tng hit-jit8 Ai-kip8 toe7 beh u7 gou7 e5 siaN5 kong2 Ka-lam5 e5 khuiN-khau2, koh ki2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 chiu3-choa7; beh u7 chit8-e5 chheng-choe3 biat8-bo5 e5 siaN5.
	19). Tng hit-jit8 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 tiong-kan, beh ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2 chit8-cho7-toaN5; ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 pian-kai3, beh ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khia7 chit8-ki thiau7.  20). Che long2 beh ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 ki3-ho7 kap cheng3-ku3; Ai-kip8 lang5 in-ui7 siu7 lang5 e5 che3-ap, ai-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I chiu7 chhe chit8-ui7 chin2-kiu3--e5, chiu7-si7 u7 chai5-leng5--e5 lai5 chin2-kiu3 in.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 Ai-kip8 lang5 bat I; ti7 hit-jit8 Ai-kip8 lang5 tek-khak bat Ia5-ho5-hoa, iah8 beh hian3 che3-mih8 kap le2-mih8 keng3-pai3 I; koh tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa he7-goan7 sia7-goan7.  22). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh phah Ai-kip8, iah8 phah, iah8 i-ti7 i; in beh kui-ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I beh thiaN in e5 ki5-to2, lai5 i-ti7 in.
	23). Tng hit-jit8 beh u7 toa7-lou7 tui3 Ai-kip8 thau3-kau3 A-sut8; A-sut8 lang5 beh jip8 Ai-kip8, Ai-kip8 lang5 iah8 beh jip8 A-sut8; Ai-kip8 lang5 beh kap A-sut8 lang5 saN-kap hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	24). Tng hit-jit8 I2-sek-liat8 beh kap Ai-kip8 chham A-sut8, saN-e5 piN5-liat8, hou7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 lang5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  25). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok in, kong2, Ai-kip8 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, A-sut8 Goa2 e5 chhiu2 sou2-cho7-e5, I2-sek-liat8 Goa2 e5 san2-giap8, long2 u7 hok-khi3.

[20]	A-sut8 ong5 Sat-jiN2-kun chhe Tha-jiN2-tham3 kau3 A-sit8-tut8 hit-ni5, Tha-jiN2-tham3 chiu7 kong-phoa3 A-sit8-tut8 lai5 chhu2 i;  2). hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok-tiong7 A-mou5-su e5 kiaN2 I2-sai3-a kong2, Khi3--ah, li2 tioh8 thau2 li2 io--nih e5 moa5-pou3, thng3 li2 kha--nih e5 oe5.  I2-sai3-a chiau3 an2-ni choe3, thng3-theh chhiah-kha lai5 kiaN5.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 I2-sai3-a thng3-theh chhiah-kha lai5 kiaN5 saN-ni5 ku2, choe3 koan-he7 ti7 Ai-kip8 kap Kou2-sit8 e5 tiau7-thau5 ki5-su7;  4). chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, A-sut8 ong5 beh chiong Ai-kip8 e5 siu7-liah8--e5, Kou2-sit8 e5 siu7 chhian-soa2--e5 chhoa7 khi3, bo5-lun7 lo2-iu3, thng3-theh chhiah-kha, lou7-chhut e7-the2, hou7 Ai-kip8 kian3-siau3.  5). In beh in-ui7 sou2 ng3-bang7 e5 Kou2-sit8, sou2 khoa-khau2 e5 Ai-kip8, lai5 kiaN-hiaN5 kian3-siau3.  6). Hit-si5 chiah e5 ian5-hai2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 beh kong2, KhoaN3 ah, lan2 chiah-e5 peng5-sou3 sou2 ng3-bang7--e5, chiu7-si7 lan2 in-ui7 beh thoat-li7 A-sut8 ong5; chau2-khi3 kiu5 i chin2-kiu3--e5, ki3-jian5 an2-ni, lan2 thai2-tho2 oe7 to5-thoat ah?

[21]	Lun7 hai2-piN khong3-ia2 e5 bek8-si7.
	U7 tui3 khong3-ia2 tui3 thang-kiaN e5 toe7 lai5--e5, chhin-chhiuN7 lam5-hng e5 kong5-hong sau3 ke3--khi3.  2). Hou7 lang5 kiaN e5 iN7-siong7 i2-keng bek8-si7 goa2; khui2-cha3-e5 kiaN5 khui2-cha3, hui2-biat8-e5 kiaN5 hui2-biat8.  I2-lan5 ah, li2 tioh8 chiuN7--khi3, Bi2-thai3 ah, li2 tioh8 ui5-khun3 i; it-chhe3 e5 thou2-khui3 Goa2 hou7 i soah.  3). Sou2-i2 goa2 moa2-io thang3-thiaN3; thong3-khou2 chiong goa2 khiN5-tiau5, chhin-chhiuN7 hu7-jin5-lang5 siN kiaN2 e5 thong3-khou2; goa2 kiau-ka2 thiaN3 kau3 boe7-oe7 thiaN; goa2 kiaN-hiaN5 kau3 boe7 khoaN3.  4). Goa2 e5 sim be5-loan7, kiaN-hiaN5 phah-kiaN goa2; goa2 sou2 ian3-lok8 e5 e5-hng pian3-choe3 goa2 e5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.  5). In pai5-siat ian5-siat8, phai3 lang5 siu2-bang7, iah8 chiah8, iah8 lim; siu2-leng2 ah, lin2 tioh8 khi2--lai5 eng7 iu5 boah tin5-pai5.  6). Chu2 tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 khi3 siat-hoat siu2-bang7 e5, hou7 i chiong sou2 khoaN3-kiN3--e5 lai5 po3-ko3.  7). I khoaN3-kiN3 kun-tui7, khia5-be2--e5, chit8-tui3 chit8-tui3, koh u7 lu5-tui7, lok8-to5-tui7, long2 teh lai5; chiu7 beh aN3 hi7-khang siong5-se3 thiaN.  8). I chhin-chhiuN7 sai hau2-kio3, kong2, Chu2--ah, goa2 jit8--si5 tiaN7-tiaN7 khia7 ti7 bang7-ko-lau5, kui-mi5 khia7 ti7 goa2 chiu2-kiN e5 sou2-chai7.  9). KhoaN3 ah, u7 chit8-tui7 e5 be2-peng, chit8-tui3 chit8-tui3 teh lai5.  I koh in3 kong2, Pa-pi2-lun5 to2-hoai7 lah, to2-hoai7 lah; i it-chhe3 sin5-beng5 e5 siong7 long2 phah-chhui3 ti7-toe7--nih.  10). Goa2 siu7 lun2 e5 tiu7-pe2, goa2 chhek-tiuN5 e5 gou7-kak ah, goa2 tui3 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, sou2 thiaN-kiN3--e5, long2 ka7 lin2 kong2 lah.
	11). Lun7 Tou7-ma2 e5 bek8-si7.
	U7 tui3 Se-jiN2 kio3 goa2 kong2, Siu2-bang7--e5 ah, mi5-kan sim2-mih8 si5? Siu2-bang7--e5 ah, mi5-kan sim2-mih8 si5?  12). Siu2-bang7--e5 in3 kong2, Cha2-khi2-si5 beh kau3, ou-am3-mi5 iah8 lai5; li2 na7 beh mng7 chiu7 thang mng7; thang hoe5-thau5, koh lai5.
	13). Lun7 A-lah8-pek e5 bek8-si7.
	Ti2-tan3 kui-tin7 e5 chhut-goa7 lang5 ah, lin2 beh hioh-mi5 ti7 A-lah8-pek e5 chhiu7-na5-lai7.  14). The5-ma2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 phang5 chui2 chhut-lai5 sang3 hou7 chhui3-ta--e5; theh8 piaN2 lai5 ngia5-chih to5-chau2--e5.  15). In-ui7 in siam2-pi7 lai7-kiam3, puih8-chhut e5 to, piN-an5 e5 keng, kap kau-chian3 e5 beng2-liat8.  16). Chu2 tui3 goa2 an2-ni kong2, Chit8-ni5 e5 lai7-bin7, chiau3 chhiaN3-kang e5 ni5-han7, Ki-tat8 it-chhe3 e5 eng5-kng beh long2 bo5--khi3.  17). Hiah-e5 kiah8 keng-chiN3 e5 Ki-tat8 e5 iong2-su7 sou2 chhun e5 giah8-siau3 chio2-chio2; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 kong2 e5.

[22]	Lun7 iN7-siong7 e5 soaN-kok e5 bek8-si7.
	U7 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3, hou7 li2 e5 peh-siN3 long2 chiuN7 chhu3-teng2 ah?  2). Li2 moa2-si3-koe3 hoah-hiam3, toa7-toa7 soan-hoa e5 siaN5, hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN5 ah, li2 tiong-kan siu7-thai5--e5 m7-si7 hou7 to thai5, iah8 m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 kau-chian3 lai5 si2.  3). Li2 sou2 u7 e5 koaN-tiuN2 choe3 chit8-e7 to5-chau2, long2 hou7 kiah8-keng e5 lang5 sou2 khun2-pak8; lin2 tiong-kan it-chhe3 hou7 lang5 chhe7--tioh8 e5, choe3 chit8-e7 siu7 khun2-pak8, in pun2 si7 chau2-khi3 hng7-hng7--e5.  4). Sou2-i2 goa2 kong2, Lin2 oat8-chau2 bo5 khoaN3 goa2, goa2 beh thong3-sim thi5-khau3; boh8-tit in-ui7 goa2 e5 peh-siN3 siu7 hui2-hoai7, lai5 bian2-kiong2 an-ui3 goa2.
	5). In-ui7 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, hou7 iN7-siong7 e5 soaN-kok u7 kiau2-jiau2 thun2-tah8 be5-loan7 e5 jit8, siaN5 tu2-tioh8 kong-phoa3, ai-kio3 e5 siaN thau3-kau3 soaN-kan.  6). I2-lan5 toa3 chiN3-te7, koh u7 chai3-peng e5 chhia kap be2-peng; Kiat-jiN2 theh8-chhut tin5-pai5.  7). Li2 sui2 e5 soaN-kok, chian3-chhia moa2-moa2, iah8 u7 be2-peng ti7 siaN5-mng5 cheng5 pai5-liat8.  8). I tu5-khi3 Iu5-tai7 e5 jia-chah8; hit-jit8 li2 chiu7 chha5-khoaN3 kun-chong-kek8 e5 kun-khi3;  9). lin2 khoaN3-kiN3 Tai7-pit8 e5 siaN5 e5 phoa3-khiah chin-choe7; chiu7 chek-chu7 e7-ti5 e5 chui2.  10). Koh sng3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 chhu3-theh8, chiong chhu3 thiah-hui2 lai5 siu-pou2 siaN5-chhiuN5.  11). Koh ti7 nng7 e5 chhiuN5 e5 tiong-kan khui chit8 e5 tham5, lai5 toe2 ku7-ti5 e5 chui2; chong2-si7 lin2 bo5 giong2-bong7 choe3 i e5, ia7 bo5 siuN7-tioh8 tui3 kou2-cha2 chiaN5 i e5.  12). Tng hit-jit8 Chu2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kah lang5 thi5-khau3, ai-siong thi3 thau5-mng5, ha5 moa5-pou3;  13). khoaN3 ah, u7 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, thai5-gu5 to2 iuN5, chiah8-bah lim-chiu2, kong2, Choe3 lan2 chiah8 choe3 lan2 lim, in-ui7 bin5-a2-jit8 beh si2--lah.  14). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 e5 hi7-khang chi2-si7 goa2, kong2, Lin2 chit e5 choe7 koat-toan3 boe7 sia3-bian2--tit, tit8-kau3 lin2 si2; che si7 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.
	15). Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, an2-ni kong2, Khi3 ah, li2 khi3 kiN3 chit e5 chiang2 khou3-pang5 e5 , chiu7-si7 koan2-ke e5 Sia7-pek-na2, tui3 i kong2 Li2 ti7-chia siaN2-su7?  16). Li2 ti7-chia u7 sim2-mih8 lang5, hou7 li2 ti7-chia ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 phah hun5-bong7? I ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 ui7 ka-ki7 phah hun5-bong7, ui7 ka-ki7 ti7 chioh8-poaN5 cho7 chit8 e5 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7.  17). KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-lat8 e5 lang5 chin7-lat8 ka7 li2 hiat--khi3; ia7 beh ka7 li2 pau bat8-bat8; I beh chiong li2 kng2 chiaN5 chit8-kng2, hiat ti7 khui-khoah e5 sou2-chai7 chhin-chhiuN7 hiat kiu5.  18). Li2 choe3 chu2-lang5 e5 ke e5 leng5-jiok8--e5, beh si2 ti7-hia; li2 eng5-kng e5 chhia ia7 beh ti7-hia.  19). Goa2 beh kek li2 e5 chit, lut li2 e5 ui7.  20). Kau3 hit-jit8 Goa2 beh tiau3 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8, Hi-lek8-ka e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-keng3, lai5;  21). Goa2 beh chiong li2 e5 goa7-phau3 hou7 i chheng7, chiong li2 e5 io-toa3 hou7 i ha5, chiong li2 e5 cheng3-su7 e5 koan5, kau i e5 chhiu2; i beh choe3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 kap Iu5-tai7 e5 ke e5 pe7.  22). Goa2 beh chiong Tai7-pit8 e5 ke e5 choan7-si5 he7 ti7 i e5 keng-thau5; i khui, chiu7 bo5 lang5 oe7 koaiN, i koaiN, chiu7 bo5 lang5 oe7 khui.  23). Goa2 beh kian3-lip8 i chhin-chhiuN7 teng teng3 ti7 kian-kou3 e5 sou2-chai7; i beh ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke choe3 eng5-kng e5 cho7-ui7.  24). Lang5 beh chiong i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke chiah e5 eng5-kng kiaN2 kap sun, hoan7-na7 khi3-ku7 e5 soe3-e5, tui3 poaN5 kau3 pan5 e5 khi3-ku7, long2 tiau3 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7.  25). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Tng hit-jit8 teng3 ti7 kian-kou3 e5 sou2-chai7 e5 teng beh se5--loh8-khi3; beh siu7 chho3-tng7 ka-lauh8 loh8-khi3, tiau3 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7 e5 mih8 beh bo5--khi3; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.

[23]	Lun7 Chhui-lo5 e5 bek8-si7.
	Tha-si e5 chun5 ah, lin2 tioh8 ai-khau3, in-ui7 Chhui-lo5 i2-keng pha-hng lah, sim7-chi3 bo5 chhu3-theh8, ia7 bo5 teh chhut-jip8; tui3 Ki-the5 e5 toe7-hng u7 po3 in chit e5 siau-sit.  2). Hai2-kiN5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, cha2-si5 Se-tun3 e5 seng-li2 lang5 ke3-hai2 hou7 lin2 tit-tioh8 chhiong-seng7, taN lin2 tioh8 cheng7-cheng7 bo5 oe7.  3). Ti7 toa7-chui2 e5 teng2-bin7, Se-hat e5 bi2-niu5, Ni5-lo5 ho5 e5 ngou2-kok si7 Chhui-lo5 sou2 chin3-jip8--e5, i choe3 liat8-kok e5 pou-thau5.  4). Se-tun3 ah, li2 tioh8 kian3-siau3, in-ui7 toa7-hai2 kong2, chiu7-si7 hai2-kiN5 e5 oe7-sou2 kong2, Goa2 bo5 hoai5-in7, ia7 bo5 u7 siN-kiaN2, bo5 u7 iuN2-chhi7 ta-pou-kiaN2 ia7 bo5 u7 bu2-iong2 chai7-sek-lu2.  5). Chit e5 hong-siaN thoan5 kau3 Ai-kip8, in beh ui7-tioh8 Chhui-lo5 e5 hong-siaN kek8-ki5 thang3-thiaN3.  6). Lin2 tioh8 ke3-khi3 Tha-si; hai2-kiN5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 ai-khau3.  7). Che si7 lin2 khoai3-lok8 e5 siaN5 mah? i e5 teng2 se3-tai7 chiu7-si7 tui3 kou2-cha2 i2-lai5, i e5 kha bat soa2 i kau3 hng7-hng7 khia7-khi2.  8). Chi7-chui7 tiaN7-tioh8 chit e5 i3-su3 kong-kek Chhui-lo5 ah? i pun2 si7 hoat-chhut bian2-liu5 e5, i e5 seng-li2-lang5 si7 ong5-chhin, i e5 boe2-boe7-e5 si7 se3-chiuN7 e5 kui3-chok8.  9). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa tiaN7-tioh8 i, beh leng5-jiok8 it-chhe3 eng5-kng e5 kiau-ngou7, hou7 se3-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 kui3-chok8 tu2-tioh8 khoaN3-khin.  10). Tha-si e5 peh-siN3 ah, li2 tioh8 pian3-kiaN5 li2 e5 toe7-hng chhin-chhiuN7 Ni5-lo5 ho5, bo5 koh u7 khu-sok.  11). I i2-keng chhun I e5 chhiu2 ti7 hai2--nih, hou7 liat8-kok tin2-tang7.  Lun7-kau3 Ka-lam5, Ia5-ho5-hoa bat hoan-hu3 tioh8 hui2-hoai7 i e5 oe7-sou2.  12). I kong2, Li2 siu7 leng5-jiok8 e5 chai7-sek-lu2, Se-tun3 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ah, li2 tek-khak bo5 koh tit-tioh8 khoai3-lok8 lah; khi2-lai5 ke3--khi3 Ki-the5, chiu7 ti7-hia ia7 bo5 tit-tioh8 an-hioh.  13). KhoaN3 ah, Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7, chit e5 peh-siN3 taN bo5--lah; A-sut8 lang5 hou7 i choe3 ia2-siu3 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7; in khi2 in e5 chiu2-kiN-lau5 hui2-hoai7 in e5 keng-tian7, hou7 i choe3 pha-hng.  14). Tha-si e5 chun5-chiah ah, lin2 tioh8 ai-khau3; in-ui7 lin2 e5 oe7-sou2 piN3-choe3 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7.
	15). Tng hit-jit8 Chhui-lo5 beh hou7 lang5 boe7-ki3--tit lek8-ke3 chhit-chap8 ni5, chiau3 chit8 e5 ong5 e5 jit8-chi2; chhit-chap8 ni5 au7 Chhui-lo5 e5 keng2-hong2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 ki7-lu2 sou2 chhiuN3 e5 koa.  16). Li2 chit e5 hou7 lang5 boe7-ki3--tit e5 ki7-lu2 ah, theh8 khim5 si3-koe3 kiaN5 siaN5-lai7; toaN5 ho2-thiaN, chhiuN3 choe7-choe7, hou7 lang5 koh ki3-tit li2.  17). Chhit-chap8 ni5 au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh koan3-kou3 Chhui-lo5, i chiu7 beh koh than3 chiN5, kap se3-chiuN7 e5 ban7-kok kau-koan.  18). I e5 he3-mih8 kap sou2 than3 e5 chiN5 beh choe3 seng3, kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, bo5 beh khng3--teh, bo5 beh chek-chu7; in-ui7 i e5 he3-mih8 beh hou7 tiam3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 e5 lang5, hou7 in chiah8-pa2, koh chheng7 tong3--tit ku2-ku2 e5 saN.

[24]	KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 toe7 khang-hu, piN3-choe3 pha-hng, koh chiong toa7-toe7 hoan-lin3-tng2, hou7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 si3-soaN3.  2). Hit-si5 peh-siN3 chaiN2-iuN7, che3-si iah8-si7 an2-ni; lou5-pok8 chaiN2-iuN7, chu2-lang5 iah8-si7 an2-ni; lu2-pi7 chaiN2-iuN7, chu2-bu2 iah8-si7 an2-ni; boe2-mih8--e5 chaiN2-iuN7, boe7-mih8--e5 iah8-si7 an2-ni; pang3-che3--e5 chaiN2-iuN7, chioh-che3-e5 iah8-si7 an2-ni; theh8 li7-sek--e5 chaiN2-iuN7, chhut li7-sek--e5 iah8-si7 an2-ni.  3). Toe7 beh choe3-chit8-e7 khang-hu, long2 tu2-tioh8 chhiuN2-kiap; in-ui7 chit e5 oe7 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  4). Toe7-chiuN7 pi-ai soe-the3, se3-kai3 hu2-pai7 soe-the3, toe7-chiuN7 tiam3-ti7 koaiN5-ui7 e5 lang5 iah8 hu2-pai7.  5). Toe7 hou7 khia7-khi2 hit e5 teng2-bin7 e5 peh-siN3 phah la5-sam5, in-ui7 in hoan7-tioh8 hiah e5 lut8-hoat, hoe3-bo5 lut8-le7, poe7-biu7 eng2-oan2 e5 iok.  6). Sou2-i2 toe7 hou7 chiu3-chou2 thun-biat8, khia7-khi2 ti7 hit teng2-bin7--e5 siu7 gi2-choe7; toe7-chiuN7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 siu7-sio, sou2-chhun e5 lang5 chio2-chio2.  7). Sin e5 chiu2 pi-ai, phu5-to5-chhiu7 hui2-hoai7; sim-lai7 khoai3-lok8--e5 long2-chong2 thou2-khui3.  8). Phah-kou2 e5 khoai3-lok8 cheng7-cheng7, ian3-lok8--e5 e5 siaN-im long2 soah; toaN5-khim5 e5 khoai3-lok8 iah8 cheng7-cheng7.  9). In boe7 tit-tioh8 chhiuN3-koa lim-chiu2; kau7-chiu2 tui3 ti7 lim e5 lang5 beh chiaN5-choe3 khou2.  10). Pha-hng e5 siaN5 i2-keng thiah-hui2; tak8-keng chhu3 long2 koaiN-mng5, lang5 long2 boe7-tit jip8.  11). Ti7 koe-lou7 in-ui7 chiu2 u7 pi-ai e5 siaN; it-chhe3 e5 hoaN-hi2 piN3-choe3 ou-am3, toe7-chiuN7 e5 khoai3-lok8 long2 bo5--khi3.  12). SiaN5-lai7 i2-keng pha-hng, siaN5-mng5 long2 hui2-hoai7.  13). In-ui7 ti7 toe7-chiuN7, ban7 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan, beh chhin-chhiuN7 phah-ke3-liau2 e5 kaN-na2-chhiu7, koh chhin-chhiuN7 phu5-to5 ban2-liau2 iau2 chhun--e5 chit8-iuN7.  14). Chiah e5 lang5 beh chhut toa7-siaN, beh hoaN-hi2 kio3; in ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 ui-giam5, tui3 hai2--nih lai5 au5-kio3.  15). In-ui7 an2-ni lin2 tioh8 ti7 tang-hng eng5-kng Ia5-ho5-hoa; ti7 chiah e5 hai2-su7 eng5-kng Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5.
	16). Goan2 thiaN-kiN3 tui3 toe7-kek8 u7 lang5 chhiuN3-koa, kong2, Eng5-kng kui ti7 gi7 e5 lang5.  Chong2-si7 goa2 kong2, Goa2 siau-biat8 lah, goa2 siau-biat8 lah; goa2 u7 chai-e7 ah, khui2-cha3--e5 kiaN5 khui2-cha3, khui2-cha3-e5 toa7 kiaN5 khui2-cha3.  17). Toe7-chiuN7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, kiaN-hiaN5, ham7-khiN, oah8-tauh long2 lim5-kau3 li2.  18). Siam2-pi7 kiaN-hiaN5 e5 siaN--e5, beh poah8-loh8 ham7-khiN; tui3 ham7-khiN khi2-lai5--e5 beh hou7 oah8-tauh tauh-tioh8; in-ui7 thiN-teng2 e5 thang-a2 long2 khui, toe7 e5 kun-ki iah8 tin2-tang7.  19). Toe7 choe3 chit8-e7 pho3-hoai7, toe7 it-chin7 pang-lih8, toe7 toa7-toa7 io5-choah.  20). Toe7 beh tian-tian to2-to2, chhin-chhiuN7 chiu2-chui3 e5 lang5; koh io5-lai5 io5-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 tiau3-chhng5; choe7-koa3 tang7-tang7 teh--in, tek-khak to2--loh8-khi3, boe7-oe7 koh khi2-lai5.
	21). Kau3 hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 chek-hoat8 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 e5 cheng3 kun-peng; ti7 toe7-chiuN7 beh chek-hoat8 toe7-chiuN7 e5 liat8-ong5.  22). In beh siu7 chu7-chip8, chhin-chhiuN7 hoan7-lang5 siu7 chu7-chip8 ti7 ham7-khiN; iah8 beh siu7 koaiN ti7 kaN-lai7; choe7-choe7 jit8 liau2-au7, chiu7 beh u7 lim5-kau3 in--e5.  23). Hit-si5 geh8 beh kian3-siau3, jit8 beh lau3-khui3; in-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ti7 Sek-an soaN ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 choe3-ong5, ti7 I e5 tiong2-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 beh u7 eng5-kng.

[25]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 beh chun li2 choe3-koaiN5, goa2 beh o-lo2 li2 e5 mia5; in-ui7 Li2 eng7 tiong-sin3 seng5-sit8 kiaN5 ki5-biau7 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 Li2 tui3 kou2-cha2 sou2 gi2-tiaN7--e5.  2). In-ui7 Li2 hou7 siaN5 piN3-choe3 thou5-tui, hou7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5 piN3-choe3 hau7-phiaN-phe3, hou7 goa7-pang lang5 e5 keng-tian7 bo5 koh choe3-siaN5, eng2-oan2 bo5 koh khi2-cho7.  3). Sou2-i2 iong2-beng2 e5 peh-siN3 beh eng5-kng Li2, kiong5-po7 e5 kok e5 siaN5 beh kiaN-ui3 Li2.  4). In-ui7 tng kiong5-po7 e5 lang5 chhui-pek lang5 e5 si5, chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-hong tit8-tit8 chhe chhiuN5-piah, Li2 chiu7 choe3 song3-hiong lang5 e5 oe7-sou2, choe3 khun3-khou2 lang5 kip-lan7-tiong e5 oe7-sou2, choe3 siam2-pi7 toa7-hong e5 sou2-chai7, choe3 siam2-pi7 iam7-jiat8 e5 im3-ng2.  5). Li2 beh chou2-chi2 goa7-pang lang5 e5 soan-hoa, chhin-chhiuN7 ta-toe7 e5 jiat8-khi3 he5--loh8-khi3; kim3-chi2 kiong5-po7 e5 lang5 chhiuN3 thai5-iaN5 e5 koa, chhin-chhiuN7 jiat8-khi3 siu7 hun5 e5 iaN2 siau-bo5.
	6). Ti7 chit e5 soaN ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ui7-tioh8 ban7 peh-siN3 eng7 ho2-mih8 pai5-siat ian5-toh, eng7 ku7-chiu2 kap kut-chhe2 moa2-moa2 e5 ho2-mih8, i2-kip8 che7-chheng e5 ku7-chiu2, pai5-siat ian5-toh.  7). Koh ti7 chit e5 soaN I beh tu5--khi3 ta3 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 phe3, kap jia-kham3 ban7-kok e5 pou3-phang5.  8). I u7 thun-biat8 si2-bo5 kau3 eng2-oan2; Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chhit-khi3 cheng3-lang5 bin7--nih e5 bak8-sai2; koh tui3 phou2-thiN-e7 tu5--khi3 I e5 peh-siN3 e5 kian3-siau3; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.
	9). Kau3 hit-jit8 lang5 beh kong2, KhoaN3 ah, che si7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3, goan2 peng5-sou3 theng3-hau7 I.  I beh chin2-kiu3 goan2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; goan2 peng5-sou3 theng3-hau7 I, goan2 beh in-ui7 I e5 kiu3-un lai5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 beh hoaN7 ti7 chit e5 soaN, Mou5-ap lang5 ti7 sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7 beh siu7 thun2-tah8, chhin-chhiuN7 ta-chhau2 siu7 thun2-tah8 ti7 pun3-so3-ti5 e5 chui2-lai7.  11). I beh ti7 hit tiong-kan thi2-khui chhiu2, chhin-chhiuN7 siu5-chui2--e5 thi2-khui chhiu2 teh siu5; chong2-si7 I beh hou7 i e5 kiau-ngou7 kap i e5 chhiu2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 khui2-ke3, choe3 chit8-e7 pai7--loh8-khi3.  12). Li2 siaN5-chhiuN5 kian-kou3 e5 koaiN5-tai5, I beh chhia-to2 i, hui2-biat8 i, thiah kau3 piN5-toe7, ke7 kau3 tin5-ai.

[26]	Tng hit-jit8 ti7 Iu5-tai7 toe7, lang5 tek-khak chhiuN3 chit e5 koa, kong2, Goan2 u7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5; I beh eng7 kiu3-un lip8 choe3 siaN5-chhiuN5, choe3 goa7-teng5-siaN5.  2). Tioh8 khui chiah e5 mng5, hou7 siu2 sin3-sit8 gi7 e5 peh-siN3 tit-tioh8 chin3-jip8.  3). Kian-sim oa2-kho3 Li2 e5, Li2 beh po2-siu2 i chap8-hun peng5-an, in-ui7 i oa2-kho3 Li2.  4). Lin2 tioh8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2; in-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 eng2-oan2 e5 chioh8-poaN5.  5). I hou7 tiam3 ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7--e5 kap koaiN5 e5 siaN5 choe3 chit8-e7 pai7--loh8-khi3; I beh chhia-to2 i ti7 toe7--nih, loh8 kau3 tin5-ai.  6). Kha beh thun2-tah8 i, chiu7-si7 song3-hiong lang5 e5 kha, khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 e5 kha-pou7.  7). Gi7-lang5 lou7 si7 cheng3-tit8; Li2 cheng3-tit8--e5 ah, siu-piN5 gi7-lang5 e5 lou7.
	8). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goan2 ti7 Li2 sim2-phoaN3 e5 lou7 theng3-hau7 Li2; goan2 e5 sim sou2 him-bou7--e5, si7 Li2 e5 mia5 kap ki3-liam7 Li2.  9). Goa2 eng7 goa2 e5 sim mi5-kan him-bou7 Li2; iah8 eng7 goa2 e5 sin5 thiN-kng-cha2 chhe7 Li2; in-ui7 Li2 sim2-phoaN3 se3-chiuN7 e5 si5, chiu7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 peh-siN3 beh hak8-sip8 gi7.  10). Eng7 un-hui7 khoan2-thai7 phaiN2-lang5, i iu5-goan5 m7 hak8-sip8 gi7; ti7 cheng3-tit8 e5 toe7-hng, i beh kiaN5 put-gi7, iah8 bo5 chu3-i3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 ui-giam5.
	11). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 chhiu2 kiah8-koaiN5, in iu5-goan5 m7-khoaN3; in beh khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 ui7-tioh8 peh-siN3 e5 jiat8-sim lai5 kian3-siau3; koh u7 he2 sio-biat8 Li2 e5 tui3-tek8.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 beh chu3-tiaN7 goan2 tit-tioh8 peng5-an, in-ui7 goan2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, long2 si7 Li2 ka7 goan2 chiaN5-e5.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 i2-goa7 bat u7 pat8 e5 chu2 koan2-hat goan2; chong2-si7 goan2 beh choan-choan oa2-kho3 Li2, ki3-liam7 Li2 e5 mia5.  14). In si2-liau2 tek-khak boe7-oe7 koh-oah8; in e5 im-hun5 boe7 koh khi2-lai5; in-ui7 Li2 lim5-kau3 in, chau5-biat8 in, hou7 in e5 mia5 long2 bo5--khi3.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 ke-thiN kok-bin5, Li2 ke-thiN kok-bin5; Li2 tit-tioh8 eng5-kng; koh khui-khoah chit e5 toe7 si3-bin7 e5 keng2-kai3.
	16). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, in ti7 hoan7-lan7-tiong chhe7 Li2; Li2 e5 keng2-kai3 kau3 in sin-chiuN7, in chiu7 piaN3-sim ki5-to2 Li2.  17). Chhin-chhiuN7 hu7-jin5-lang5 hoai5-in7, beh siN e5 si5, chiu7 kiau-ka2, ti7 thong3-khou2 e5 si5 au5-kio3; Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goan2 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 iah8 si7 an2-ni.  18). Goan2 iah8 bat hoai5-in7 bat kiau-ka2, sou2-siN--e5 keng2-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 hong; goan2 ti7 toe7--nih be7-bat kiaN5 sim2-mih8 chin2-kiu3 e5 su7; se3-chiuN7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 iah8 bo5 poah8-loh8.  19). Li2 e5 si2-lang5 beh koh-oah8; goa2 chiah e5 sin-si beh koh khi2--lai5; to2 ti7 tin5-ai--e5 ah, lin2 tioh8 cheng-sin5 khi2-lai5 chhiuN3-koa; in-ui7 Li2 e5 lou7-chui2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-chhai3-teng2 e5 lou7-chui2, toe7 iah8 beh kau-chhut im-hun5.
	20). Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 jip8 bat8-pang5 koaiN li2 e5 mng5, bih tiap-a2-ku2, theng3-hau7 siu7-khi3 ke3-khi3.  21). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 I e5 sou2-chai7 chhut-lai5, beh heng5-hoat8 toe7-chiuN7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 choe7-ok; toe7 iah8 beh lou7-chhut i sou2 u7 e5 huih, bo5 koh jia-kham3 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5.

[27]	Kau3 hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh eng7 I kong-ngi7 u7-lat8 e5 toa7 ki to heng5-hoat8 gok8-hi5, chiu7-si7 hit-ho7 gau5-chau2 e5 choa5, heng5-hoat8 gok8-hi5 chiu7-si7 hit-ho7 oan-oan oat-oat e5 choa5; iah8 beh thai5-si2 hai2-tiong e5 leng5.
	2). Tng hit-jit8 u7 chhut ho2-chiu2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5, lin2 tioh8 ki2 chit e5 hng5 chhiuN3-koa,  3). kong2, Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 kou3-siu2 phu5-to5-hng5--e5; Goa2 si5-khek koan3-ak i, mi5-jit8 kou3-siu2 i, bian2-tit lang5 sun2-hai7 i.  4). Goa2 bo5 chun5 siu7-khi3; goan7 u7 chhi3-phe3 chit8-le5 kap Goa2 kau-chian3, Goa2 chiu7 ho2-taN2 chin3-cheng5 khi3 chhe7 i, ka7 i choe3 chit8-e7 sio--khi3.  5). Na7-bo5 an2-ni, hou7 i khiN5-tioh8 Goa2 e5 leng5-lek8, lai5 kap Goa2 ho5-ho2; goan7 i kap Goa2 ho5-ho2.  6). Chiong-lai5 Nga2-kok beh teng3 i e5 kun, I2-sek-liat8 beh hoat-ge5 khui-hoe; in e5 ke2-chi2 beh chhiong-moa2 se3-kai3.
	7). Chu2 phah i, kiam2 chhin-chhiuN7 phah hiah-e5 bat phah-i e5 lang5 mah? i siu7-thai5, kiam2 chhin-chhiuN7 hiah-e5 thai5-i--e5 e5 siu7-thai5 mah?  8). Li2 chhe in khi3, si7 chiau3 sou2 hap8-gi5 kap in saN-chiN; khi2 tang-hong e5 jit8, chiu7 eng7 toa7-hong ka7 in koaN2--khi3.  9). Sou2-i2 Nga2-kok e5 choe7-ok beh an2-ni tit-tioh8 soe2-tu5, i e5 choe7-koa3 tit-tioh8 tu5--khi3 e5 hau7-ko2, chai7-ti7 chit-e5; hit-si5 i hou7 che3-toaN5 e5 chioh8-thau5 piN3-choe3 phah-chhui3 e5 he-chioh8; ti3-kau3 chha5-thiau7 kap jit8-siong7 bo5 koh khia7--teh.  10). In-ui7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5 piN3-choe3 chhiN-chhin3; lou7-ke soaN3-theh8 chhin-chhiuN7 khong3-ia2; gu5-a2 beh chiah8-chhau2 ti7-hia, to2 ti7-hia, iah8 beh chiah8-oan5 i e5 chhiu7-ki.  11). I e5 ki kou-ta5 siu7 at-chih8, hu7-jin5-lang5 beh lai5 ka7 i sio-lio--khi3; in-ui7 chiah e5 peh-siN3 gong7-gong7; sou2-i2 cho7-hoa3 in--e5, bo5 beh lin5-bin2 in, cho7-chiaN5 in--e5, bo5 beh si-un hou7 in.  12). Kau3 hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh kha3 i e5 ke2-chi2, tui3 Toa7-ho5 kau3 Ai-kip8 e5 khoe; lin2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chit8-e5 chit8-e5 hou7 I siu-khioh.
	13). Tng hit-jit8 beh pun5 toa7 e5 ho7-thau5; kiN3-na7 phiau-liu5 ti7 A-sut8 toe7, kap siu7-koaN2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7-e5, long2 beh lai5 ti7 seng3-soaN, ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, keng3-pai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[28]	Chai-e7 ah, I2-hoat-lian5 e5 chui3-han3 kiau-ngou7 e5 bian2-liu5, kap i sui2 e5 chng-thaN7 teh sia7 e5 hoe, chiu7-si7 ti3 ti7 hiah-e5 hou7 chiu2 sou2 khun3-khou2--e5, in e5 pui5 e5 soaN-kok e5 thau5.  2). KhoaN3 Chu2 u7 chit8-e5 toa7 koan5-leng5 toa7 khui3-lat8--e5, chhin-chhiuN7 chit8-chun7 e5 toa7-phauh8, chhin-chhiuN7 hui2-biat8 e5 kong5-hong, chhin-chhiuN7 hiong-lau5 e5 toa7-chui2, I beh eng7 toa7-lat8 hiat i ti7 toe7--nih.  3).
