I2-hoat-lian5 e5 chui3-han3 kiau-ngou7 e5 bian2-liu5 beh siu7 tah8 ti7 kha-e7.  4). I sui2 e5 chng-thaN7 teh sia7 e5 hoe chiu7-si7 ti7 pui5 e5 soaN-kok e5 thau5, beh chhin-chhiuN7 he7-thiN i2-cheng5, khi2-thau5 sek8 e5 bu5-hoa-ko2; kiN3-na7 khoaN3-kiN3--e5 chiu7 chu3-i3 khoaN3, chit8-e7 kau3-chhiu2 chiu7 thun--loh8-khi3.  5). Tng hit-jit8 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh choe3 I hiah-e5 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3 eng5-kng e5 bo7, sui2 e5 bian2-liu5.  6). Iah8 choe3 che7-ui7 lai5 sim2-phoaN3--e5 kong-gi7 e5 sin5, iah8 choe3 siaN5-mng5-khau2 phah-the3 tui3-tek8--e5 e5 khui3-lat8.  7). Tok8-tok8 chit-ho7 lang5 tui3 chiu2 lai5 chha-biu7, tui3 kau7-chiu2 lai5 be5-lou7; che3-si kap sian-ti long2 tui3 kau7-chiu2 lai5 chha-biu7, hou7 chiu2 sou2 thun-chiah8, tui3 kau7-chiu2 lai5 be5-lou7; tui3-ti7 bek8-si7 chiu7 chha-chhok, tui3 ti7 sim2-phoaN3 bo5 peng5-un2.  8). In-ui7 tak8 te3 toh la5-sam5, thou3 kau3 moa2-moa2, bo5 chit8-ui7 chheng-khi3.
	9). I beh eng7 ti3-hui7 ka3-si7 chi7-chui7 ah? beh hou7 chi7-chui7 beng5-pek8 sou2-thoan5-e5 ah? si7 hit-ho7 tu2-a2 tng7-lin li7-khui heng-cheng5--e5 mah?  10). In-ui7 beng7-leng7 koh beng7-leng7, beng7-leng7 koh beng7-leng7; lut8-le7 koh lut8-le7, lut8-le7 koh lut8-le7, chit-ui7 tam7-poh8, hit-ui7 tam7-poh8.  11). Boe7--lah; Chu2 beh eng7 pat8-iuN7 e5 chhui3-tun5 kap bo5 siang5-lui7 e5 chih8, tui3 chit e5 peh-siN3 kong2-oe7.  12). I bat tui3 in kong2, Chit-e5 chiu7-si7 an-hioh, lin2 tioh8 hou7 ia3-sian7 e5 lang5 tit-tioh8 an-hioh; koh kong2, Chit-e5 chiu7-si7 khuiN3-oah8; chong2-si7 in m7-kheng2 thiaN.  13). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 in kong2 e5 oe7, si7 beng7-leng7 koh beng7-leng7, beng7-leng7 koh beng7-leng7; lut8-le7 koh lut8-le7, lut8-le7 koh lut8-le7; chit-ui7 tam7-poh8, hit-ui7 tam7-poh8; ti3-kau3 in khi3, chiu7 hiaN3-au7 poah8-to2, koh poah8 kau3 chhui3-chhui3, ham7-loh8 lo5-bang7, siu7 liah8-tioh8.
	14). Sou2-i2 lin2 chiah e5 bu2-ban7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 koan2-hat tiam3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiah e5 peh-siN3--e5, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  15). In-ui7 lin2 bat kong2, Goan2 kap si2-bo5 lip8-iok, kap im-hu2 kiat-beng5, chai-e7 toa7 liu5-heng5 e5 si5 tek-khak bo5 kau3 ti7 goan2; in-ui7 goan2 eng7 peh8-chhat8 choe3 siam2-pi7 e5 sou2-chai7, ti7 hu-ke2 e5 sou2-chai7 ka-ki7 bih.  16). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 ti7 Sek-an he7 chit8 te3 chioh8 choe3 toe7-ki, si7 i2-keng chhi3-giam7 e5 chioh8, kian-kou3 e5 toe7-ki, po2-kui3 e5 chhu3-kak; oa2-kho3 i e5 lang5 tek-khak bo5 tioh8-kip.  17). Goa2 beh eng7 kong-peng5 choe3 chun2-chin5 eng7 kong-gi7 choe3 tui7-soaN3; peng-phauh8 beh phah-to2 hu-ke2 siam2-pi7 e5 sou2-chai7, toa7-chui2 beh im-bat8 siam2-bih e5 sou2-chai7.  18). Lin2 kap si2-bo5 sou2 lip8 e5 iok tek-khak hoe3-bo5, kap im-hu2 sou2 kiat e5 beng5 tek-khak khia7-boe7-tiau5; chai-e7 toa7 liu5-heng5 e5 si5, lin2 beh siu7 i thun2-tah8.  19). Tak8-pai2 keng-ke3, beh chiong lin2 liah8-khi3; in-ui7 tak8 cha2-khi2 i beh keng-ke3, bo5 lang3 jit8-mi5; beng5-pek8 sou2-thoan5-e5, kan-ta kiaN-hiaN5.  20). Bin5-chhng5 te2, hou7 lang5 boe7 chhun-tit8; mi5-phe7 oeh8, hou7 lang5 kah boe7-bat8.  21). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh khi2-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Pi2-lah8-sim soaN, I beh siu7-khi3 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Ki-pian3 e5 soaN-kok; thang choe3 I e5 kang, chiu7-si7 han2-tit choe3 e5 kang, thang chiaN5 I e5 su7, chiu7-si7 ki5-iN7 e5 su7.  22). TaN lin2 m7-thang bu2-ban7, kiaN-liau2 pak8 lin2 e5 soh khun2 khah-an5; in-ui7 goa2 tui3 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3, i2-keng koat-toan3 beh ti7 choan5-toe7-chiuN7 kiaN5 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 biat8-bo5 e5 su7.
	23). Lin2 tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 siaN, liu5-sim thiaN goa2 e5 oe7.  24). Hit-e5 loe5-hng5 beh ia7-cheng2--e5, kiam2-si7 siong5-siong5 teh loe5 mah? kiam2-si7 siong5-siong5 teh kut8 lai5 pe7 i e5 thou5 mah?  25). I i2-keng chhong3-piN5 thou5-bin7, kiam2 bo5 ia7 poeh-kak, chai ma2-khun5, chiau3-choa7 cheng3 sio2-beh8, ti7 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 sou2-chai7 cheng3 toa7-beh8, ti7 hng5-piN cheng3 chhou-beh8 mah?  26). In-ui7 i e5 Siong7-te3 eng7 hap8-gi5 e5 hoat-tou7 chi2-tiam2 i, koh ka3-si7 i.  27). Poeh-kak m7-si7 eng7 lai7 e5 khi3-ku7 phah--e5, ma2-khun5 m7-si7 eng7 chhia-lun5 lun2--e5; chiu7-si7 eng7 thui5-a2 phah poeh-kak, eng7 koaiN2-a2 phah ma2-khun5.  28). Choe3-piaN2 e5 gou7-kak kiam2 khoeh hou7 i chhui3 mah? Bo5--lah, bo5 tng5-tng5 phah i; sui-jian5 eng7 chhia-lun5 be2-toe5 phah-soaN3 i, iah8 bo5 hou7 i chhui3--khi3.  29). Che iah8 chhut ti7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa; I e5 ke3-ek8 ki5-biau7, I e5 ti3-hui7 khoah-toa7.

[29]	Ai--ah, A-li7-i-lek8, A-li7-i-lek8, Tai7-pit8 an-iaN5 e5 siaN5, lin2 chit8-ni5 ke3 chit8-ni5, choeh-ki5 chiau3-siong5 lun5-liu5.  2). Goa2 beh hou7 A-li7-i-lek8 khun3-lan5, i beh u7 pi-siong ai-khau3; chong2-si7 Goa2 beh khoaN3 i choe3 A-li7-i-lek8.  3). Goa2 beh si3-ui5 an-iaN5 kong-kek li2, khi2 thou5-tui phah li2, khi2 koaiN5-tai5 kong-kek li2.  4). Li2 beh kang3-ke7, tui3 toe7-tiong kong2-oe7, li2 e5 gian5-gu2 beh soe3-soe3, tui3 tin5-ai chhut-lai5; li2 e5 siaN-im, beh chhin-chhiuN7 kui2 chiuN7-sin--e5 e5 siaN-im tui3 toe7 chhut-lai5, li2 e5 gian5-gu2 kiu7-kiu7-hau2 tui3 tin5-ai chhut.
	5). Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 toa7-tui7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 iu3 e5 thou5-hun2, kiong5-po7 lang5 e5 toa7-tui7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 pe e5 chhou-khng; chit e5 su7 beh tiap-a2-ku2 e5 tiong-kan hut-jian5 lim5-kau3.  6). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho-hoa beh eng7 lui5-tan5, toe7-tang7, toa7-siaN, kng2-le5-hong, toa7-hong, kap thun-biat8 e5 he2-iam7 lim5-kau3 i.  7). Hit-si5 kong-kek A-li7-i-lek8 cheng3-kok e5 toa7-tui7, chiu7-si7 it-chhe3 kong-kek i kap i e5 oe7-sou2, kap khou2-chhou2 i e5, beh chhin-chhiuN7 bang7-kiN3, chhin-chhiuN7 mi5-si5 e5 iN7-siong7.  8). Beh chhin-chhiuN7 iau e5 lang5 bang7-kiN3 teh-chiah8, kau3 cheng-sin5 sim iu5-goan5 chai khang-khang; a2-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chhui3-ta e5 lang5 bang7-kiN3 teh lim, kau3 cheng-sin5 iu5-goan5 ia3-sian7, siuN7 beh lim; cheng3-kok e5 toa7-tui7 kap Sek-an soaN kau-chian3--e5, iah8 beh chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni.
	9). Lin2 tioh8 gong5-ngiah8 ki5-koai3, lin2 tioh8 ka-ki7 jia-pe3 lai5 chhiN-mi5.  In chui3, m7-si7 in-ui7 chiu2, in tian-lai5 tian-khi3, m7-si7 in-ui7 kau7-chiu2.  10). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiong khun3 tang7-bin5 e5 sin5 koan3 ti7 lin2 e5 teng2-bin7, hong-bat8 lin2 e5 bak8-chiu, kham3-bat8 lin2 e5 thau5-khak; lin2 e5 bak8-chiu chiu7-si7 sian-ti, lin2 e5 thau5-khak chiu7-si7 sian-kian3--e5.  11). Sou2-u7 e5 bek8-si7 tui3-ti7 lin2 chhin-chhiuN7 hong--teh e5 ji7-iuN7; lang5 chiong chit e5 ji7-iuN7 kau hou7 bat-ji7 e5 lang5, kong2, ChhiaN2 thak8 i; i kong2, Goa2 boe7-oe7, in-ui7 hong--teh.  12). Koh chiong chit e5 ji7-iuN7 kau hou7 m7-bat-ji7 e5 lang5, kong2, ChhiaN2 thak8 i; i kong2, Goa2 m7-bat ji7.  13). Chu2 kong2, In-ui7 chit e5 peh-siN3 chhin-kun7 Goa2, eng7 chhui3, eng7 chhui3-tun5 chun-keng3 Goa2, sim chiu7 li7-khui Goa2 hng7-hng7; in e5 chun-keng3 Goa2, put-ko3 si7 than3 lang5 sou2 ka3-si7 e5 beng7-leng7 na7-tiaN7;  14). sou2-i2 Goa2 beh koh eng7 ki5-biau7 e5 su7 khoan2-thai7 chit e5 peh-siN3, hit e5 su7 chiu7-si7 ki5-biau7 koh ki5-iN7; in ti3-hui7 lang5 e5 ti3-hui7 beh siau-bo5, in chhong-beng5 lang5 e5 chhong-beng5 beh kham3-bat8.
	15). Chai-e7 ah, hiah-e5 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhim-chhim khng3 in e5 ke3-bou5, koh ti7 am3-tiong kiaN5 tai7-chi3-e5, kong2, Chi7-chui7 khoaN3-kiN3 goan2? chi7-chui7 chai goan2 ah?  16). Hai7 ah, lin2 poe7-biu7 lah! Kiam2 thang khoaN3 sio-hui5 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 thou5 mah? siu7-cho7 e5 mih8 kiam2 thang lun7 cho7-i--e5, kong2, I bo5 cho7 goa2 mah? a2-si7 siu7-choe3 e5 mih8-kiaN7, kiam2 thang lun7 choe3-i--e5 kong2, I bo5 chhang-mia5 mah?
	17). Kiam2 m7-si7 tiap-a2-ku2 e5 si5, Li7-pa-lun3 pian3-choe3 ho2 e5 chhan5, ho2 e5 chhan5 khoaN3-choe3 chhiu7-na5 mah?  18). Hit-jit8 chhau3-hi7-lang5--e5 beh thiaN-kiN3 chheh-lai7 e5 oe7, chhiN-mi5-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu beh tui3 bong5-bu7 ou-am3-tiong tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3,  19). Khiam-pi7 e5 lang5 beh in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 ke-thiN in e5 hoaN-hi2; jin5-kan e5 song3-hiong lang5 beh in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 lai5 khoai3-lok8.  20). In-ui7 kiong5-po7 lang5 i2-keng kui ti7 bo5, bu2-ban7 e5 lang5 i2-keng biat8-choat8; it-chhe3 chhe7 ki-hoe7 choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5 long2 siu7 chian2-tu5.  21). In ui7-tioh8 chit8-ku3-oe7 lai5 chek-choe7 lang5, siat oah8-tauh lai5 ham7-hai7 ti7 siaN5-mng5 tok-chek lang5--e5, eng7 bo5-iaN2 e5 su7 ong2-khut gi7-lang5.  22). Sou2-i2 kiu3-siok8 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7 Nga2-kok e5 ke an2-ni kong2, Nga2-kok taN tek-khak bo5 koh kian3-siau3, i e5 bin7 iah8 bo5 pian3-sek.  23). Chong2-si7 i khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 cheng3-kiaN2, chiu7-si7 Goa2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5, ti7 i e5 tiong-kan, in beh chun Goa2 e5 mia5 choe3-seng3, beh chun Nga2-kok e5 Seng3--e5 choe3-seng3, beh keng3-ui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3.  24). Sim-lai7 hou5-tou5-e5 beh tit-tioh8 beng5-pek8, m7 kam-goan7--e5 beh siu7 kau3-hun3.

[30]	Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Chai-e7 ah, chiah e5 poe7-gek8 e5 kiaN2, in saN-kap ke3-bou5, bo5 tui3 Goa2 e5 i3-su3, in kiat beng5-iok bo5 tui3 Goa2 e5 sin5, ti3-kau3 choe7-siong7 ka-choe7.  2). Khi2-sin loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8, peng7-bo5 chheng2-mng7 Goa2, beh oa2-kho3 Hoat-lo2 e5 se3-lek8, ke-thiN ka-ki7 e5 se3-lek8, iah8 siam2-bih ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 ti3-im3-e7.  3). Sou2-i2 Hoat-lo2 e5 se3-lek8 beh choe3 lin2 e5 kian3-siau3; siam2-bih ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 ti3-im3-e7 beh choe3 lin2 e5 lau3-khui3.  4). I e5 siu2-leng2 i2-keng kau3 So2-an, i e5 su3-chia2 i2-keng kau3 Hap-loe7-su.  5). In beh in-ui7 boe7 li7-ek in e5 peh-siN3 lai5 kian3-siau3, hit e5 peh-siN3 m7-si7 choe3 pang-chan7, iah8 m7-si7 choe3 li7-ek, tok8-tok8 si7 choe3 kian3-siau3, choe3 leng5-jiok8.
	6). Lun7 lam5-hng e5 cheng-siN e5 bek8-si7.  In chiong chai5-but8 to5 ti7 lu5-a2 ka-chiah-teng2, chiong po2-mih8 chai3 ti7 lok8-to5 e5 nia7, keng-ke3 kan-lan5 khun3-khou2 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 bu2 e5 sai, kang e5 sai, tok8-choa5 kap he2-iam7 pe e5 leng5 e5 toe7, khi3 hit e5 bo5 li7-ek in e5 peh-siN3 hia.  7). Ai-kip8 e5 pang-chan7 si7 khang-khang bo5 li7-ek; sou2-i2 goa2 chheng i choe3 che7-teh boe7 tin2-tang7 e5 Lah8-hap-pek.
	8). TaN li2 khi3, ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5, chiong chit e5 oe7 sia2 ti7 pai5--nih, ki3 ti7 chheh--nih, lau5 ti7 au7-tai7, kau3 eng2-oan2.  9). In-ui7 in si7 poe7-gek8 e5 peh-siN3, kong2 peh8-chhat8 e5 kiaN2-ji5, m7-kheng2 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 ka3-si7 e5 kiaN2-ji5.  10). In tui3 sian-kian3--e5 kong2, Boh8--tit sian-kian3; tui3 sian-ti kong2, Boh8-tit tui3 goan2 kong2 cheng3-tit8 e5 oe7, tioh8 tui3 goan2 kong2 jiu5-loan2 e5 oe7, kong2 hu-ke2 e5 su7;  11). lin2 tioh8 pang3-sak chiaN3-lou7, li7-khui cheng3-tit8 e5 lou7, m7-thang ti7 goan2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koh the5-khi2 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5.  12). Sou2-i2 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 lin2 khi3-sak chit e5 oe7, pin5-sin3 po7-giok8 kap koai7-phiah, lai5 oa2-kho3 i;  13). sou2-i2 chit e5 choe7-ok ti7 lin2 e5 sin-chiuN7, chhin-chhiuN7 beh-to2 e5 lih8-hun5, phong3-chhut ti7 koaiN5-chhiuN5--e5; tiap-a2-ku2 e5 tiong-kan hut-jian5-kan to2-hoai7.  14). I beh hui2-hoai7 i, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 hui2-hoai7 sio-hui5 lang5 e5 hui5-khi3, kong3-chhui3 iah8 bo5 po2-sioh; ti3-kau3 chhui3-te3 e5 tiong-kan, chhe7 bo5 chit8-phiN3 thang tui3 he2-lou5 lai5 chhu2 he2, tui3 ti5-lai7 lai5 iuN2 chui2.
	15). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5, bat an2-ni kong2, Lin2 e5 tit-tioh8 kiu3 chai7-ti7 oat8-to3-tng2 kap an-hioh; lin2 tit-tioh8 khui3-lat8 chai7-ti7 peng5-cheng7 kap sin3-kho3; chong2-si7 lin2 bo5 beh.  16). Lin2 kong2, Bo5--ah, goan2 beh khia5-be2 lai5 chau2, sou2-i2 lin2 tit-beh chau2; koh kong2, Goan2 beh khia5 hit-e5 chin gau5-chau2 e5 cheng-siN, sou2-i2 tui-koaN2 lin2-e5 iah8 beh chin gau5 chau2.  17). Chit8-lang5 hang2-hoah, chiu7 chit8-chheng lang5 to5-chau2; gou7-lang5 hang2-hoah, chiu7 lin2 long2 beh to5-chau2; ti3-kau3 sou2 chhun-e5 chhin-chhiuN7 soaN-teng2 e5 ki5-koaN, soaN-thau5 e5 toa7-ki5.  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa in-ui7 an2-ni beh theng3-hau7 lai5 si un-hui7 hou7 lin2, koh in-ui7 an2-ni beh khi2-lai5 lin5-bin2 lin2; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 kong-peng5 e5 Siong7-te3; hoan7-na7 theng3-hau7 I--e5, long2 u7 hok-khi3.
	19). Lin2 chiah-e5 khia7-khi2 ti7 Sek-an, ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, li2 tek-khak bo5 koh thi5-khau3; Chu2 beh in-ui7 li2 ai-kiu5 e5 siaN toa7 si-un hou7 li2; I thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 beh in3 li2.  20). Chu2 beh hou7 lin2 ti7 hoan7-lan7-tiong u7 piaN2, ti7 kan-khou2-tiong u7 chui2; lin2 e5 sian-siN bo5 koh siam2-bih; li2 beh chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 e5 sian-siN.  21). Li2 phian ti7 cho2 phian ti7 iu7 e5 si5, hi7-khang-lai7 beh thiaN-kiN3 u7 siaN ti7 li2 e5 au7-bin7 kong2, Che chiu7-si7 lou7, li2 tioh8 kiaN5 i.  22). Li2 sou2 tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7, eng7 gun5 siuN--e5, sou2 chu3-cho7 e5 ngou2-siong7 eng7 kim tou7--e5, li2 beh phah la5-sam5 i, beh khi3-sak i, chhin-chhiuN7 u3-oe3 e5 mih8; tui3 i kong2, Khi3--ah.  23). Li2 ia7 cheng2-chi2 ti7 toe7--nih, I beh ka7 i loh8-hou7, iah8 beh hou7 toe7 sou2 chhut e5 bi2-niu5 chin-ho2, chin hong-seng7; kau3 hit-si5 li2 e5 cheng-siN beh ti7 khoan-khoah e5 chhau2-tiuN5 chiah8-chhau2.  24). Loe5 hng5 e5 gu5 kap lu5-a2-kiaN2 beh chiah8 soah-iam5 e5 liau7; chit e5 liau7 si7 eng7 hong-kou2 kap poa3-ki ke3 chhiuN5--e5.  25). Ti7 toa7-thai5 lang5, chiu2-kiN-lau5 to2-hoai7 e5 jit8, tak8 e5 koaiN5-soaN toa7-nia2 beh u7 ho5-chui2 khoe-lau5.  26). Tng Ia5-ho5-hoa pau I e5 peh-siN3 sun2-siong e5 sou2-chai7, i-ti7 I e5 peh-siN3 phah-siong e5 jit8, geh8 e5 kng beh chhin-chhiuN7 jit8 e5 kng, jit8 e5 kng beh ke chhit-pe7, chhin-chhiuN7 chhit e5 jit8 e5 kng chit8-iuN7.
	27). KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 tui3 hng7-hng7 lai5, siu7-khi3 toh8--khi2-lai5, bat8-bat8 e5 ian chheng3-koaiN5; I e5 chhui3-tun5 u7 siu7-khi3 moa2-moa2; I e5 chit8 chhin-chhiuN7 thun-biat8 e5 he2.  28). I e5 khi3 chhin-chhiuN7 tiong3-moa2 e5 ho5-chui2, tiong3 kau3 am7-kun2; beh eng7 hui2-biat8 e5 thai lai5 thai ban7-kok; koh ti7 cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 chhui3-lai7, beh u7 hou7 lang5 kiaN5 chho3-gou7 e5 be2-ka7-kiuN.  29). Lin2 beh chhiuN3-koa, chhin-chhiuN7 siu2 seng3-choeh e5 mi5; koh sim-lai7 hoaN-hi2, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 pun5 tat8-a2 chiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 soaN, kau3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Chioh8-poaN5 hia.  30). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 lang5 thiaN I ui-giam5 e5 siaN, koh hou7 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 I e5 chhiu2 phah--loh8-khi3, kap siu7-khi3-tiong e5 siu7-khi3, thun-biat8 e5 he2-iam7, chhe3-lui5, toa7-hong, peng-phauh8.  31). Sou2-i2 A-sut8 lang5 beh in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN toa7 kiaN-hiaN5; I beh eng7 koaiN2-a2 lai5 phah i.  32). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chiong tiaN7-tioh8 e5 koaiN2-a2, kau3 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7; tak8-pai2 phah--loh8-khi3, chiu7 thiaN-kiN3 toaN5-khim5 phah-kou2 e5 siaN; kau-chian3 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa tang7-khi2 I e5 chhiu2 kap i kau-chian3.  33). In-ui7 To5-hui-tek8 tui3 cha2 chiu7 siat-lip8; ui7-tioh8 ong5 lai5 pi7-pan7 chhim koh khoah; ki5-tiong kui-tui--e5 si7 he2 kap choe7-choe7 chha5; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 chit8-tiau5 e5 jiu5-ng5 he2, hou7 i toh8--khi2-lai5.

[31]	U7 chai-e7 ah, hiah-e5 loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8 kiu5 pang-chan7--e5, in oa2-kho3 be2; iah8 oa2-kho3 chhia, in-ui7 i choe7; oa2-kho3 be2-peng, in-ui7 i kiong5; chong2-si7 bo5 i3-hiong3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5, iah8 bo5 kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa ki5-sit8 u7 ti3-hui7, I beh kang3 chai-e7, bo5 siu to3-tng2 I e5 oe7; beh khi2-lai5 kong-kek hiah e5 phaiN2-lang5 e5 ke, koh kong-kek hiah-e5 pang-chan7 lang5 choe3 phaiN2--e5.  3). Ai-kip8 lang5 put-ko3 si7 lang5, m7-si7 Siong7-te3; in e5 be2 put-ko3 si7 bah, m7-si7 sin5; Ia5-ho5-hoa chit8-e7 chhun-chhiu2, hit e5 pang-chan7 lang5--e5 beh tak--tioh8, hit-e5 siu7 pang-chan7--e5 beh poah8-to2, long2 saN-kap biat8-bo5.
	4). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 an2-ni kong2, Chhin-chhiuN7 sai kap soe3-chiah sai kou3 i sou2 jiau3--tioh8 e5 mih8, chiu7 hm7-hm7-hau2, sui-jian5 tiau3-chip8 choe7-choe7 bok8-chia2 lai5 kong-kek i, i long2 bo5 in-ui7 in e5 siaN lai5 kiaN-hiaN5, iah8 bo5 in-ui7 in e5 soan-hoa lai5 khut-hok8; chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh lim5-kau3, kau-chian3 ti7 Sek-an soaN kap i e5 soaN-nia2.  5). Chhin-chhiuN7 chiau2 thi2-khui sit8, an2-ni ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh po2-hou7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2; koh po2-hou7 i, koh khan-kiu3 i, koh poaN5-ke3 lai5 kiu3 i.  6). I2-sek-liat8 e5 kiaN2-sun ah, lin2 sou2 chhim-chhim poe7-gek8-e5, taN tioh8 kui-ng3 I.  7). In-ui7 kau3 hit-jit8, tak8-lang5 beh chiong i gun5 e5 ngou2-siong7, kim e5 ngou2-siong7, chiu7-si7 lin2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 cho7, ham7-loh8 lin2 ti7 choe7--e5, long2 pang3-sak i.  8). A-sut8 lang5 beh si2 ti7 to-e7, m7-si7 tui3-ti7 lang5, iah8 m7-si7 peng5-siong5 lang5 e5 to beh biat8 i; i beh tui3 to e5 bin7-cheng5 lai5 to5-siam2, i e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 beh choe3 khou2-kang.  9). I e5 chioh8-poaN5 beh in-ui7 kiaN-hiaN5 lai5 bo5--khi3; i e5 siu2-leng2 beh in-ui7 toa7-ki5 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5; che si7 hit e5 u7 he2 ti7 Sek-an, u7 lou5 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.

[32]	KhoaN3 ah, beh u7 chit8 e5 ong5 chiau3 kong-gi7 lai5 choe3-ong5, beh u7 siu2-leng2 chiau3 kong-peng5 lai5 chiang2-koan5.  2). Beh u7 lang5 choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 siam2-pi7 hong e5 sou2-chai7, choe3 bih toa7-hou7 e5 ui7; chhin-chhiuN7 khoe-lau5 e5 chui2 ti7 ta-toe7, chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-chioh8 e5 im3-ng2 ti7 ia3-sian7 e5 sou2-chai7.  3). Hit-e5 oe7 khoaN-kiN3 e5 lang5, bak8-chiu bo5 koh ian-ng7; oe7 thiaN e5 lang5, hi7-khang beh aN3 teh-thiaN;  4). so3-seng3 lang5 e5 sim beh beng5-pek8 ti3-sek; tioh-chih8-kun e5 lang5 e5 chih8 beh kong2-oe7 kin2 koh beng5.  5). Gong7-lang5 bo5 koh chheng-choe3 ko-beng5, kian-lin7 e5 lang5 bo5 koh chheng choe3 toa7-liong7.  6). In-ui7 gong7-lang5 beh kong2 gong7-oe7, sim siuN7 choe3-phaiN2, koaiN3-si3 kiaN5 siat-tok8 e5 su7, kong2 chha-biu7 e5 oe7 kong-kek Ia5-ho5-hoa, hou7 iau e5 lang5 bo5 mih8 thang chiah8, chhui3-ta e5 lang5 bo5 chui2 thang lim.  7). Kian-lin7 e5 lang5 sou2 eng7 e5 hoat-tou7 si7 phaiN2--e5, i siat ke3-bou5, eng7 peh8-chhat8 oe7 hui2-biat8 kan-khou2 lang5; song3-hiong e5 lang5 kang2-lun7 kong-li2 e5 si5, i iah8 iu5-goan5 kiaN5 hui2-biat8;  8). chong2-si7 ko-beng5 e5 lang5 ke3-ek8 ko-beng5 e5 su7, iah8 tng5-tng5 tiam3 ti7 ko-beng5.
	9). Chheng-eng5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, tioh8 khi2-lai5 thiaN goa2 e5 siaN; bo5 khoa3-lu7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ah, tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 oe7.  10). Bo5 khoa3-lu7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ah, koh ke3 chit8-ni5 khah-ke, beh kiaN-hiaN5; in-ui7 bo5 phu5-to5 thang ban2, bo5 ke2-chi2 thang siu-seng5.  11). Chheng-eng5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, tioh8 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah; bo5 khoa3-lu7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ah, tioh8 kiaN-hiaN5, thng3-saN chhiah-theh, io ha5 moa5-pou3.  12). In beh ui7-tioh8 ho2 e5 chhan5-toe7 kap bou7-seng7 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 tui5-heng.  13). Chhi3-phe3 chit8-le5 beh hoat-siN ti7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 toe7; iah8 beh hoat-siN ti7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN5, khoai3-lok8 e5 chhu3.  14). In-ui7 ong5-kiong beh hong-hoe3, lau7-jiat8 e5 siaN5 beh leng2-cheng7; soaN-thau5 kap chiu2-kiN-lau5 eng2-oan2 choe3 soaN-tong7, choe3 ia2-lu5 hoaN-hi2 e5 sou2-chai7, choe3 kui-tin7 cheng-siN e5 chhau2-tiuN5.  15). Theng3-hau7 seng3 e5 Sin5 tui3 teng2-bin7 piaN3-loh8 ti7 lan2, khong3-ia2 pian3-choe3 pui5 e5 chhan5, pui5 e5 chhan5 khoaN3-choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-na5.  16). Hit-si5 kong-peng5 beh toa3 ti7 khong3-ia2, kong-gi7 beh tiam3 ti7 pui5 e5 chhan5.  17). Gi7 e5 kong-hau7 si7 peng5-an, gi7 e5 hau7-giam7 si7 peng5-cheng7 an-un2, kau3 ti7 eng2-oan2.  18). Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 beh tiam3 ti7 peng5-an e5 theh8, an-un2 e5 chhu3, chheng-cheng7 hioh-khun3 e5 sou2-chai7.  19). Tok8-tok8 chhiu7-na5 to2--loh8-khi3 e5 si5 beh loh8-phauh8; koh hit e5 siaN5 beh kang3-loh8 kau3 chin-ke7.  20). Lin2 chiah-e5 ia7-cheng2 ti7 tak8 e5 chui2-piN--e5, pang3 gu5 lu5 ti7-hia e5, u7 hok-khi3.

[33]	Chai-e7 ah, li2 chit-e5 chhiuN2-toat8 lang5--e5, ka-ki7 bo5 siu7 chhiuN2-toat8; kiaN5 tai7-chi3 khui2-cha3--e5, lang5 bo5 eng7 khui2-cha3 khoan2-thai7 li2!  Li2 chhiuN2-toat8 tu2-a2 soah, ka-ki7 beh siu7 chhiuN2-toat8; li2 kiaN5 khui2-cha3 tu2-a2 soah, lang5 beh eng7 khui2-cha3 khoan2-thai7 li2.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 si-un hou7 goan2; goan2 theng3-hau7 Li2, kiu5 Li2 tak8 cha2-khi2 choe3 goan2 e5 chhiu2, tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5, choe3 goan2 e5 chin2-kiu3.  3). Soan-hoa e5 siaN chit8-e7 hoat, cheng3 peh-siN3 to5-chau2; Li2 chit8-e7 khi2-lai5, liat8-kok si3-soaN3.  4). Lin2 sou2-chhiuN2--e5 beh hou7 lang5 siu-sip8, chhin-chhiuN7 chian2-a2-thang5 e5 siu-sip8 mih8; lang5 chau2--khi3 hia, chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-meh thiau3-lai5 thiau3-khi3.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa siu7 chun-choe3 koaiN5; in-ui7 I tiam3 ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7; I eng7 kong-peng5 kong-gi7 chhiong-moa2 Sek-an.  6). Li2 it-seng it-si3 beh tit-tioh8 an-un2, u7 hong-seng7 e5 kiu3-un, kap ti3-hui7 kap chai-bat; keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 li2 e5 po2-poe3.
	7). KhoaN3 ah, in e5 ho5-kiat8 ti7 goa7-bin7 ai-siong; kiu5-ho5 e5 su3-chia2 thong3-sim thi5-khau3.  8). Toa7-lou7 pha-hng, long2 bo5 lang5 ke3-lou7; i poe7-iok, khoaN3-khin chiah e5 siaN5, bo5 iau3-kin2 peh-siN3.  9). Toe7-chiuN7 pi-ai soe-the3; Li7-pa-lun3 kian3-siau3 kou-ta5; Sa-lun5 chhin-chhiuN7 khong3-ia2; Pa-san kap Ka-bit8 e5 chhiu7-bak8 lak kng-kng.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, TaN Goa2 beh khi2-lai5; taN Goa2 beh heng-khi2; taN Goa2 beh ka-ki7 koaiN5.  11). Lin2 hoai5-in7 chhou-khng lai5 siN tiu7-ko2; lin2 e5 khi3 beh chhin-chhiuN7 he2 lai5 thun-biat8 lin2.  12). Liat8-pang beh chhin-chhiuN7 i2-keng sio e5 chioh8-he; chhin-chhiuN7 i2-keng koah e5 chhi3-phe3, siu7-sio ti7 he2-tiong.
	13). Lin2 hng7 e5 lang5, tioh8 thiaN Goa2 sou2-kiaN5--e5, lin2 kun7 e5 lang5 tioh8 chai Goa2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5.  14). Sek-an tiong e5 choe7-jin5 long2 kiaN-hiaN5, bo5 keng3-khian5 e5 lang5 beh tit8-tit8 chhoah.  Lan2 tiong-kan chi7-chui7 oe7 kap thun-biat8 e5 he2 saN-kap toa3? Lan2 tiong-kan chi7-chui7 oe7 kap eng2-oan2 e5 sio-hui2 saN-kap toa3 ah?  15). KiaN5 tai7-chi3 kong-gi7, kong2-oe7 cheng3-tit8, oan3-hun7 lek8-sek e5 chai5-li7, io5 chhiu2 bo5 siu7 pou3-lou7, that-bat8 hi7-khang bo5 thiaN lau5-huih e5 oe7, khoeh bak8-chiu bo5 khoaN3 phaiN2-tai7--e5;  16). i beh tiam3 ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7; kian-kou3 e5 chioh8-poaN5 choe3 i e5 oe7-sou2; beh u7 bi2-niu5 kiong-kip i, i e5 chui2 tek-khak boe7 choat8-tng7.  17). Li2 e5 bak8-chiu beh khoaN3-kiN3 ong5 e5 sui2, beh khoaN3-kiN3 khui-khoah e5 toe7.  18). Li2 e5 sim beh siau3-liam7 hit e5 kiaN-hiaN5 e5 su7; koan2-siau3--e5 ti7 toh-loh8? pheng5 kong3-gun5 e5 ti7 toh-loh8? sng3 chiu2-kiN-lau5--e5 ti7 toh-loh8?  19). Li2 tek-khak bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 kiong5-beng2 e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 kong2-oe7 oh-thiaN, li2 boe7 beng5-pek8; gian5-gu2 gi2-bu2 gi2-ngiau2, li2 boe7 hiau2-tit--e5.  20). Li2 tioh8 khoaN3 Sek-an, lan2 siu2 seng3-choeh e5 siaN5, li2 e5 bak8-chiu beh khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 choe3 an-cheng7 e5 chhu3-theh8, choe3 bo5 i5-soa2 e5 pou3-piN5, i e5 khit8 eng2 bo5 puih8-chhut, i e5 soh long2 bo5 tng7.  21). Ti7-hia Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hian2-beng5 ui-giam5 kap lan2 saN-kap ti7-teh, chhin-chhiuN7 kang-ho5 khui-khoah e5 toe7; hit tiong-kan tek-khak bo5 u7 ko3-chiuN2 e5 chun5 ong2-lai5, iah8 bo5 u7 ui-hong e5 chun5 keng-ke3.  22). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 lan2 e5 sim2-phoaN3-si, Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 ka7 lan2 siat lut8-hoat--e5; Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 lan2 e5 ong5; I beh chin2-kiu3 lan2.  23). Li2 e5 phang5-soh long2 lut--khi3; chun5-ui5 khia7-boe7-chai7; hong-phang5 chhia boe7-khi2-lai5; hit-si5 choe7-choe7 chhiuN2--lai5 e5 mih8 hou7 lang5 pun--khi3; pai2-kha--e5 iah8 chhiuN2-tioh8 mih8.  24). Khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 tek-khak bo5 kong2, Goa2 u7 phoa3-piN7; ki5-tiong khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, choe7-koa3 long2 sia3-bian2.

[34]	Liat8-kok ah, lin2 tioh8 kun7-cheng5 lai5 thiaN; cheng3 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN; toe7 kap i sou2 chhiong-moa2--e5, se3-kai3 kap kiN3-na7 tui3 i lai5 chhut--e5, long2 tioh8 thiaN.  2). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa siu7-khi3 kau3 liat8-kok, toa7 siu7-khi3 in e5 choan5-kun; gi2-tiaN7 long2 biat8 i, chiong in kau hou7 lang5 thai5.  3). In siu7-thai5-e5 tek-khak hiat-kak8, sin-si e5 chhau3-bi7 chheng3--khi2-lai5, chiah e5 soaN siu7 in e5 huih iuN5-hoa3.  4). ThiN e5 ban7-siong7 beh siau-bo5, thiN beh chhin-chhiuN7 chhak kng2--khi2-lai5; i e5 ban7-siong7 beh soe-pai7, chhin-chhiuN7 phu5-to5-chhiu7 e5 hioh8 soe-pai7, koh chhin-chhiuN7 bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7 e5 soe-pai7 chit8-iuN7.  5). In-ui7 Goa2 e5 to ti7 thiN--nih i2-keng lim kau3-giah8; khoaN3 ah, chit e5 to beh kau3 I2-tong, i2-kip8 Goa2 sou2 gi2-tiaN7 beh biat8-bo5 e5 peh-siN3, lai5 sim2-phoaN3 i.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 to u7 huih moa2-moa2, bak-tioh8 iu5 kap iuN5-a2-kiaN2 kap soaN-iuN5 e5 huih, i2-kip8 kang e5 mi5-iuN5 io-chi2 e5 iu5; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Pho-su-lah8 u7 che3-su7, ti7 I2-tong toe7 u7 toa7 thai5-lang5 e5 su7.  7). Ia2-gu5 beh kap in loh8--lai5, gu5-a2 kap kang e5 gu5 iah8 si7 an2-ni; in e5 toe7 in-ui7 huih lai5 chui3, in e5 thou5-hun2 in-ui7 iu5 lai5 pui5.  8). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 po3-siu5 e5 jit8, ui7-tioh8 Sek-an e5 an3-kiaN7, u7 po3-eng3 e5 ni5.  9). I2-tong chiah e5 khoe beh piN3-choe3 lek8-chhiN, thou5-hun2 beh piN3-choe3 jiu5-ng5, i e5 toe7 chiaN5-choe3 i2-keng toh8 e5 lek8-chhiN.  10). Mi5-jit8 long2 bo5 sit; i e5 ian eng2-oan2 chheng3--khi2-lai5, tai7-tai7 pha-hng; eng2-oan2 bo5 lang5 keng-ke3.  11). The5-ou5 ho5-ti beh tit-tioh8 choe3-giap8; niau-thau5-eng ou-a beh tiam3 ti7 hit tiong-kan; I beh chiong hong-hoe3 e5 chun2-chin5, hun7-tun7 e5 tui7-soaN3, khan ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7.  12). In beh kio3 chun-kui3 e5 lang5 lai5 ti7-li2 kok, ti7-hia long2 bo5 chit8-e5, kui3-chok8 iah8 long2 bo5.  13). In e5 keng-tian7 beh hoat chhi3-phe3, oe7-sou2 beh hoat chit8-le5 kap chhau2-chhi3; beh choe3 soaN-kau2 e5 hiat8, to5-chiau2 e5 siu7.  14). Ia2-siu3 kap chhai5-long5 saN tu2-tioh8; ia2-soaN-iuN5 beh kap i e5 phoaN7 tui3-kio3; mi5--si5 e5 iau-koai3 beh ti7-hia hioh, ka-ki7 chhe7 an-hioh e5 sou2-chai7.  15). ChiN3-choa5 beh ti7-hia choh siu7, siN-nng7, pu7-nng7, chhut-kiaN2, koh chu7-chip8 kiaN2 ti7 i e5 pak-tou2-e7; eng-chiau2 kui-tui3 chu7-chip8 ti7-hia.  16). Lin2 tioh8 kang2-kiu3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chheh lai5 thak8 i; ki5-tiong bo5-khiam3 chit8-hang7 bo5 chit8-chiah bo5 phit-phoe3; in-ui7 Goa2 e5 chhui3 i2-keng chhut beng7-leng7, I e5 sin5 i2-keng chu7-chip8 in.  17). I iah8 ui7 in liam-khau, koh chhin-chhiu2 eng7 chun2-chin5 ka7 in pun-toe7; in beh eng2-oan2 tit-tioh8 i choe3-giap8, tak8 se3-tai7 tiam3 ti7-hia.

[35]	Khong3-ia2 kap ta-so3 e5 toe7 tek-khak hoaN-hi2; soa-bou5 iah8 beh khoai3-lok8, koh chhin-chhiuN7 mui5-kui3 khui-hoe.  2). I beh khui-hoe bou7-seng7, lai5 hoaN-hi2, beh u7 hoaN-hi2 kap chhiuN3-koa; Li7-pa-lun3 e5 eng5-kng, Ka-bit8 kap Sa-lun5 e5 sui2, beh kui i; in beh khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng, lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bi2-biau7.
	3). Lin2 tioh8 hou7 loan2-jiok8 e5 chhiu2 iong2-chong3, bo5-lat8 e5 kha-thau5-u chu7-chai7.  4). Tui3 sio2-taN2 e5 lang5 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 kong-kiong5, m7-bian2 kiaN; khoaN3 ah, lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh lai5 po3-siu5, beh lai5 kiaN5 kek8-toa7 e5 po3-eng3; I beh lai5 chin2-kiu3 lin2.  5). Hit-si5 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu beh khui, chhau3-hi7-lang5 e5 hi7-khang beh lai7.  6). Hit-si5 pai2-kha--e5 beh tio5-thiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 lok8, e2-kau2 e5 chih8 beh chhiuN3-koa; in-ui7 chui2 chheng3-chhut ti7 khong3-ia2, khoe-lau5 chheng3-chhut ti7 soa-bou5.  7). Hoat-chhut-kng e5 soa, beh piN3-choe3 chui2-ti5, ta-so3 e5 toe7 beh piN3-choe3 chui2-choaN5; ti7 soaN-kau2 to2 teh-khun3 e5 sou2-chai7 beh u7 chhiN-chhau2 lou5-ui2 kap pou5-chhau2.  8). Ti7-hia beh u7 chit8 tiau5 koaiN5 e5 lou7, chit tiau5 lou7 beh chheng-choe3 Seng3 e5 lou7; u3-oe3 e5 lang5 boe7-tit-thang keng-ke3; choan-choan beh choe3 in e5 lou7-eng7; kiaN5-lou7 e5 lang5, sui-jian5 gu5-gong7, iah8 boe7 kiaN5-chho3.  9). Ti7-hia tek-khak bo5 sai, beng2-siu3 iah8-bo5 chiuN7 chit tiau5 lou7; ti7-hia long2 bo5 tu2-tioh8 in; tok8-tok8 tit-tioh8 siok8-hoe5 e5 peh-siN3 ti7-hia kiaN5.  10). Koh Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu3-siok8 e5 peh-siN3 beh to3-tng2--lai5, beh chhiuN3-koa lai5 kau3 Sek-an; tit-tioh8 eng2-oan2 e5 hoaN-hi2 choe3 bian2-liu5; in beh hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, iu-bun7 thou2-khui3 long2 beh chau2--khi3.

[36]	Hi-se-ka ong5 chap8-si3 ni5, A-sut8 ong5 Se-na2-ki-lip8 chiuN7 lai5 kong-kek Iu5-tai7 it-chhe3 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5 lai5 chhu2 i.  2). A-sut8 ong5 tui3 Lah8-kiat chhe Lah8-pek-sa-ki chhoa7 toa7-tui7 peng khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, kau3 Hi-se-ka ong5 hia; i chiu7 khia7 ti7 teng2-ti5 e5 chui2-kau-piN, ti7 phio3-pou3 sai-hu7 e5 chhan5 e5 toa7-lou7.  3). Hit-tiap8 u7 koan2-ke e5 Hi-lek8-ka e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-keng3, kap su-ki3 Sia3-pek-na2, kap su2-koaN A-sat e5 kiaN2 Iok-a, chhut-lai5 kiN3 i.
	4). Lah8-pek-sa-ki tui3 in kong2, Lin2 khi3 ka7 Hi-se-ka kong2, A-sut8 ong5 tai7-ong5 an2-ni kong2, Li2 sou2 oa2-kho3 e5, si7 oa2-kho3 sim2-mih8?  5). Li2 kong2, U7 ke3-bou5 u7 khui3-lat8 thang kau-chian3; goa2 kong2 che si7 khang-khang e5 oe7 na7-tiaN7; li2 tau3-ti2 oa2-kho3 chi7-chui7 chiah poe7-poan7 goa2 ah?  6). KhoaN3 ah, li2 sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 Ai-kip8 si7 hit e5 pit-phoa3 e5 lou5-tek-koaiN2; lang5 na7 oa3 i, chiu7 oe7 chhiah-jip8 i e5 chhiu2; Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 tui3 it-chhe3 oa2-kho3 i e5 lang5 iah8 si7 an2-ni.  7). Li2 na7 ka7 goa2 kong2, Goa2 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3; chit e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kiam2-m7-si7 Hi-se-ka bat hoe3 I e5 soaN-thau5-toaN5 kap I e5 che3-toaN5, iah8 bat tui3 Iu5-tai7 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 lang5 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 ti7 chit e5 toaN5-cheng5 keng3-pai3--e5 mah?  8). TaN chhiaN2 li2 eng7 chun2-tng3 hou7 goa2 e5 chu2 A-sut8 ong5, goa2 hou7 li2 nng7-chheng chiah be2, khoaN3 li2 hit-bin7 oe7 pi7-pan7 lang5 khia5 i a2-boe7.  9). Na7 boe7, thai2-tho2 oe7 phah-the3 goa2 e5 chu2 chiah e5 te7-it soe3 e5 lou5-pok8-tiong chit8 e5 kun-tiuN2, iah8 keng2-jian5 oa2-kho3 Ai-kip8, ai3 tit-tioh8 chian3-chhia kap be2-peng ah?  10). TaN goa2 chiuN7-lai5 kong-kek hui2-biat8 chit e5 toe7, kiam2 bo5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 i3-su3 mah? Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 goa2 kong2, Li2 chiuN7-khi3 kong-kek hui2-biat8 chit e5 toe7.  11). I2-li7-a-keng3, Sia3-pek-na2, Iok-a tui3 Lah8-pek-sa-ki kong2, Kiu5 li2 eng7 A-lan5 e5 oe7 kap li2 e5 lou5-pok8 kong2; in-ui7 goan2 oe7 hiau2 thiaN; m7-thang eng7 Iu5-tai7 e5 oe7 kap goan2 kong2, hou7 siaN5-teng2 e5 peh-siN3 hi7-khang thiaN-kiN3.  12). Lah8-pek-sa-ki kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 chhe goa2 lai5, kiam2-si7 tui3 li2 e5 chu2 kap li2 kong2 chiah e5 oe7 mah? kiam2-m7-si7 tui3 che7 ti7 siaN5-teng2 e5 lang5 kong2, hou7 in kap lin2 piN5-piN5 chiah8 ka-ki7 e5 pun3, lim ka-ki7 e5 jio7 mah?  13). Lah8-pek-sa-ki chiu7 khia7--teh, eng7 Iu5-tai7 e5 oe7 toa7-siaN kio3 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 thiaN A-sut8 ong5 tai7-ong5 e5 oe7.  14). Ong5 an2-ni kong2, Lin2 m7-thang hou7 Hi-se-ka sou2 phian3; in-ui7 i boe7-oe7 kiu3 lin2;  15). iah8 boh8-tit thiaN Hi-se-ka kah lin2 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak beh kiu3 lan2, chit e5 siaN5 tek-khak bo5 kau ti7 A-sut8 ong5 e5 chhiu2.  16). Boh8-tit thiaN Hi-se-ka e5 oe7; in-ui7 A-sut8 ong5 an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 kap goa2 ho5-ho2, chhut-lai5 tau5-hang5 goa2, tak8-lang5 chiu7 thang chiah8 ka-ki7 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 kap bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7 e5 ke2-chi2, lim ka-ki7 e5 chiN2-chui2;  17). theng3-hau7 goa2 chhoa7 lin2 kau3 chit8 e5 toe7 kap lin2 pun2-toe7 bo5 koh-iuN7, chiu7-si7 u7 gou7-kak kap sin-chiu2 e5 toe7, u7 bi2-niu5 kap phu5-to5-hng5 e5 toe7.  18). Lin2 tioh8 kin2-sin7 ti5-hong5, kiaN-liau2 Hi-se-ka in2-iu2 lin2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak kiu3 lan2.  Liat8-kok e5 siong7-te3 kiam2 u7 chit8-e5 bat kiu3 i e5 kok thoat-li7 A-sut8 ong5 e5 chhiu2 ah?  19). Hap-ma2 kap A-ni2-poat8 e5 siong7-te3 ti7 toh-loh8 ah? Se-hoat-oa2-im e5 siong7-te3 ti7 toh-loh8 ah? in kiam2 bat kiu3 Sat-ma2-li7-a thoat-li7 goa2 e5 chhiu2 mah?  20). Chiah e5 kok e5 siong7-te3 u7 chi7-chui7 bat kiu3 ka-ki7 e5 kok thoat-li7 goa2 e5 chhiu2 ah, boh8-kioh Ia5-ho5-hoa kiam2 oe7 kiu3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 thoat-li7 goa2 e5 chhiu2 mah?
	21). In cheng7-cheng7, iah8 bo5 in3 chit8-ku3; in-ui7 ong5 bat hoan-hu3 kong2, Boh8-tit in3 i.  22). Hit-si5 Hi-lek8-ka e5 kiaN2 koan2-ke e5 I2-li7-a-keng3, kap su-ki3 Sia3-pek-na2, kap su2-koaN A-sat e5 kiaN2 Iok-a, long2 thiah-lih8 saN lai5 kau3 Hi-se-ka hia, chiong Lah8-pek-sa-ki e5 oe7 ka7 i kong2.

[37]	Hi-se-ka ong5 thiaN-kiN3, chiu7 thiah-lih8 i e5 saN, chheng7 moa5-pou3, jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7.  2). Chhe koan2-ke e5 I2-li7-a-keng3, kap su-ki3 Sia3-pek-na2, kap che3-si tiong e5 lo2-poe3--e5, long2 chheng7 moa5-pou3, khi3 kiN3 A-mou5-su e5 kiaN2 sian-ti I2-sai3-a.  3). Tui3 i kong2, Hi-se-ka an2-ni kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 si7 hoan7-lan7, chek-hoat8, leng5-jiok8 e5 jit8, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 kiaN2 beh chhut-si3, iah8 bo5 lat8 thang siN-chhut.  4). Kiam2-chhai2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 e5 Siong7-te3, thiaN-kiN3 Lah8-pek-sa-ki e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 i e5 chu2 A-sut8 ong5 chhe i lai5 bu2-ban7 eng2-oah8 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, kiam2-chhai2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 e5 Siong7-te3, ui7-tioh8 thiaN-kiN3 chiah e5 oe7, chiu7 beh chek-pi7 i; sou2-i2 kiu5 li2 ui7-tioh8 iau2 chhun e5 peh-siN3 chhut-siaN ki5-to2.  5). Hi-se-ka ong5 e5 jin5-sin5 chiu7 khi3 kiN3 I2-sai3-a.  6). I2-sai3-a tui3 in kong2, Tioh8 an2-ni tui3 lin2 e5 chu2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 thiaN-kiN3 A-sut8 ong5 e5 lou5-pok8 siat-tok8 Goa2 e5 oe7, m7-bian2 kiaN in.  7). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh eng7 chit8 e5 sin5 jip8 i e5 sim, i beh thiaN-kiN3 hong-siaN, chiu7 to3-tng2-khi3 pun2 sou2-chai7; Goa2 beh hou7 i ti7 pun2 sou2-chai7 to2 ti7 to-e7.
	8). Lah8-pek-sa-ki to3-khi3, tu2-tioh8 A-sut8 ong5 teh phah Lip8-na2; si7 in-ui7 i u7 thiaN-kiN3 A-sut8 ong5 u7 thiat-iaN5, li7-khui Lah8-kiat.  9). Ong5 thiaN-kiN3 kong2, Kou2-sit8 ong5 Tek8-hap-ka chhut-lai5 beh kap li2 kau-chian3; i chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 chhe su3-chia2 khi3 kiN3 Hi-se-ka, hoan-hu3 in, kong2,  10). Tioh8 ka7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Hi-se-ka an2-ni kong2, Li2 sou2 oa2-kho3 li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kong2, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 tek-khak bo5 kau ti7 A-sut8 ong5 e5 chhiu2, li2 boh8-tit hou7 I khi-phian3.  11). KhoaN3 ah, li2 chong2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 A-sut8 chiah e5 ong5 tui3 liat8-kok sou2-kiaN5--e5, si7 it-chin7 biat8 in; chong2 bo5 li2 iau2 oe7 tit-tioh8 kiu3 mah?  12). Goa2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 hui2-biat8--e5, chiu7-si7 Ko-san3, Hap-lan5, Li7-sek, kap siok8 The5-lah8-sat e5 Ai-tian5 lang5; chiah e5 kok e5 siong7-te3 kiam2 bat kiu3 i mah?  13). Hap-ma2 e5 ong5, A-ni2-poat8 e5 ong5, Se-hoat-oa2-im siaN5 e5 ong5, Hi-na2 kap I2-oa2 e5 ong5, long2 ti7 toh-loh8?
	14). Hi-se-ka tui3 su3-chia2 e5 chhiu2 chih-tioh8 phoe, thak8 i; Hi-se-ka chiu7 chiuN7--khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7, chiong phoe pai5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  15). Hi-se-ka tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ki5-to2 kong2,  16). Che7 ti7 ki-lou7-peng e5 tiong-kan, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, tok8-tok8 Li2 choe3 thiN-e7 ban7-kok e5 Siong7-te3; Li2 bat chhong3-cho7 thiN toe7.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 khui bak8-chiu lai5 khoaN3; tioh8 thiaN Se-na2-ki-lip8 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, si7 chhe su3-chia2 lai5 bu2-ban7 eng2-oah8 Siong7-te3 e5.  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, A-sut8 chiah e5 ong5 ko2-jian5 hou7 liat8-kok kap i e5 toe7 piN3-choe3 pha-hng,  19). ia7 chiong in e5 siong7-te3 hiat ti7 he2--nih; in-ui7 in m7-si7 Siong7-te3, si7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 sou2-cho7--e5, si7 chha5--e5, chioh8--e5; in chiu7 chau5-biat8--in.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, taN kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goan2 thoat-li7 i e5 chhiu2, hou7 thiN-e7 ban7-kok long2 chai tok8-tok8 Li2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	21). A-mou5-su e5 kiaN2 I2-sai3-a chiu7 chhe lang5 khi3 kiN3 Hi-se-ka kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Li2 ki3-jian5 in-ui7 A-sut8 ong5 Se-na2-ki-lip8 e5 ian5-kou3 ki5-kiu5 Goa2;  22). taN lun7-kau3 i, Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 an2-ni kong2, Sek-an e5 chai7-sek-lu2 biau2-si7 li2, thi2-chhio3 li2; Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 tui3 li2 io5-thau5.  23). Li2 leng5-jiok8 bu2-ban7 chi7-chui7? chhut toa7-siaN, bak8-chiu niah koaiN5-koaiN5, kong-kek chi7-chui7 ah? chiu7-si7 kong-kek I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5.  24). Li2 chhe li2 e5 lou5-pok8 bu2-ban7 Chu2 kong2, Goa2 chhoa7 choe7-choe7 chian3-chhia chiuN7-kau3 soaN-chiam, kau3 Li7-pa-lun3 kek8-chhim e5 sou2-chai7; goa2 beh chho3 hit-te3 koaiN5-toa7 e5 pek-hiuN-chha5, kap siong7-ho2 e5 siong5-chhiu7; goa2 beh chiuN7 kek8-koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7, kap i pui5-toe7 e5 chhiu7-na5.  25). Goa2 i2-keng khui-chiN2 lim goa7-pang e5 chui2, goa2 eng7 kha-chiuN2 tah8 Ai-kip8 it-chhe3 e5 ho5, hou7 i ta--khi3.  26). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 kiam2 be7-bat thiaN-kiN3 Goa2 ti7 goan5-khi2-thau5 sou2-choe3--e5, ti7 kou2-cha2 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8--e5 mah? taN Goa2 chiaN5 i, si7 hou7 li2 hui2-hoai7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5, piN3-choe3 hau7-phiaN-phe3.  27). Sou2-i2 ki5-tiong khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 khui3-lat8 chin-chio2, kiaN-hiaN5 kian3-siau3; in chhin-chhiuN7 khong3-ia2 e5 chhau2, chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhai3, chhin-chhiuN7 chhu3-teng2 e5 chhau2, chhin-chhiuN7 chhan5--nih be7 toa7-chang5 e5 tiu7-a2.  28). Li2 che7-loh8-khi3, li2 chhut-khi3, li2 jip8-lai5, li2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 Goa2, Goa2 long2 chai.  29). In-ui7 li2 toa7 siu7-khi3 Goa2, koh in-ui7 li2 kiau-ngou7 e5 oe7 thang3-kau3 Goa2 e5 hi7-khang, Goa2 chiu7 beh eng7 Goa2 e5 kau kau li2 e5 phiN7, eng7 Goa2 e5 be2-ka7-kiuN koa3 ti7 li2 e5 chhui3, hou7 li2 tui3 goan5-lou7 to3--khi3.  30). Hi-se-ka ah, chit-e5 hou7 li2 choe3 tiau7-thau5; kin-ni5 lin2 beh chiah8 ka-ki7 hoat e5 mih8, me5-ni5 beh chiah8 tui3 hit-e5 sou2-chhut-e5; kau3 te7-saN ni5, lin2 tioh8 cheng3-choh siu-koah, chai-cheng3 phu5-to5-hng5, lai5 chiah8 i e5 ke2-chi2.  31). Iu5-tai7 ke thoat-li7 hoan7-lan7 sou2-chhun e5 peh-siN3 beh iu5-goan5 e7-bin7 teng3-kun, teng2-bin7 kiat ke2-chi2.  32). In-ui7 beh u7 chhun e5 peh-siN3 tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chhut--lai5, beh u7 to5-chau2 e5 lang5 tui3 Sek-an soaN lai5; ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 jiat8-sim beh chiaN5 chit e5 su7.  33). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7 A-sut8 ong5 kong2, I tek-khak boe7 kau3 chit e5 siaN5, iah8 boe7 ti7-chia sia7-chiN3, boe7-oe7 gia5 tin5-pai5 kau3 siaN5-cheng5, iah8 boe7 khi2 thou5-tui lai5 kong-kek i.  34). I tui3 hit tiau5 lou7 lai5, beh tui3 hit tiau5 lou7 to3-khi3, boe7-oe7 lai5 kau3 chit e5 siaN5, che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.  35). In-ui7 Goa2 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 ian5-kou3, koh ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 e5 ian5-kou3, beh po2-hou7 chit e5 siaN5, lai5 chin2-kiu3 i.
	36). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 chhut--khi3, ti7 A-sut8 iaN5-tiong phah-si2 chap8-poeh-ban7 gou7-chheng lang5; kau3 thiN-kng-cha2 khi2--lai5 e5 si5, khoaN3 ah, long2 si7 si2 e5 sin-si.  37). A-sut8 ong5 Se-na2-ki-lip8 chiu7 li7-khui to3-khi3, tiam3 ti7 Ni5-ni5-bi5.  38). Ti7 i e5 siong7-te3 Ni5-su-lok8 e5 bio7 kui7-pai3 e5 si5, i e5 kiaN2, A-tek-bi2-lek8 kap Sa-li7-sek, eng7 to thai5 i; in chiu7 chau2 kau3 A-lah8-liap8 e5 toe7.  I e5 kiaN2 I2-sat-hap-tun3 soa3-chiap i choe3-ong5.

[38]	Hiah e5 jit8 e5 tiong-kan, Hi-se-ka phoa3-piN7 teh-beh si2.  A-mou5-su e5 kiaN2, sian-ti I2-sai3-a, khi3 kiN3 i, tui3 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 tioh8 siat-hoat li2 e5 ke-su7, in-ui7 li2 teh-beh si2, boe7-oah8.  2). Hi-se-ka chiu7 oat8-tng2 bin7 ng3 piah, ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kong2,  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 ki3-liam7 goa2 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chaiN2-iuN7 chun5 oan5-choan5 e5 sim, chiau3 seng5-sit8 lai5 kiaN5, koh choe3 Li2 sou2 khoaN3-choe3 ho2--e5.  Hi-se-ka chiu7 toa7-siaN thi5-khau3.  4). Tui3 an2-ni Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 I2-sai3-a kong2,  5). Li2 khi3 ka7 Hi-se-ka kong2, Li2 e5 chou2 Tai7-pit8 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3 li2 e5 ki5-to2, khoaN3-kiN3 li2 e5 bak8-sai2; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh ke-thiN li2 e5 he3-siu7 chap8-gou7 ni5.  6). Koh Goa2 beh kiu3 li2 kap chit e5 siaN5 thoat-li7 A-sut8 ong5 e5 chhiu2; iah8 beh po2-hou7 chit e5 siaN5.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chiaN5 I sou2 kong2--e5, che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 li2 e5 tiau7-thau5;  8). khoaN3 ah, A-hap-su e5 jit8-kui te3-jit8 chin3-cheng5 e5 iaN2, Goa2 beh hou7 i the3-au7 chap8-tou7.  Tui3 an2-ni chin3-cheng5 e5 jit8-iaN2, ko2-jian5 ti7 jit8-kui e5 teng2-bin7, the3-au7 chap8-tou7.
	9). Iu5-tai7 ong5 Hi-se-ka phoa3-piN7 i2-keng ho2, chiu7 choe3 si, kong2:
10). Goa2 kong2, tu2-tu2 ti7 goa2 tiong-lian5 e5 jit8, beh jip8 im-kan e5 mng5;
Boe7-tit-thang hiong2-siu7 goa2 iau2 chhun e5 ni5.
11). Goa2 kong2, Goa2 boe7 kiN3--tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7, boe7 kiN3-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa;
Goa2 boe7-tit-thang kap tiam3 toe7-chiuN7 e5 peh-siN3 saN-kap khoaN3 lang5 e5 bin7.
12). Goa2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 siu7 chhian-soa2 li7-khui goa2, chhin-chhiuN7 kou3-iuN5 e5 lang5 e5 pou3-piN5 chit8-iuN7;
Goa2 chiong siN3-mia7 kng2--khi2-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 chit-pou3 e5 lang5 kng2-pou3 chit8-iuN7; I beh chiong goa2 tui3 pou3-kui-thau5 chian2-tng7.
Tui3 cha2-khi2 kau3 e5-hng, Li2 beh hou7 goa2 kiat-kiok8.
13). Goa2 hou7 ka-ki7 an-cheng7 kau3 thiN-kng; I chhin-chhiuN7 sai at-chih8 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 kut-thau5;
Tui3 cha2-khi2 kau3 e5-hng, Li2 beh hou7 goa2 kiat-kiok8.
14). Goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 iN3-a2, chhin-chhiuN7 peh8-hoh8, gi2-bu2 gi2-ngiau2; koh chhin-chhiuN7 ka-chui ai-kio3;
Goa2 in-ui7 kiah8-thau5 khoaN3, bak8-chiu ian-ng7.
Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 siu7 ap-che3, kiu5 Li2 ka7 goa2 po2-jin7.
15). Goa2 beh kong2 sim2-mih8 ah? I ka7 goa2 kong2--e5, iah8 ka7 goa2 chiaN5--lah;
Goa2 in-ui7 sim-lai7 e5 khou2-chhou2, ti7 it-seng e5 ni5-jit8, beh un5-un5-a2 kiaN5.
16). Chu2 ah, lang5 tit-tioh8 oah8 si7 chai7-ti7 chiah-e5,
Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 oah8--teh, iah8 long2 si7 tui3 an2-ni;
Sou2-i2 kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 koh-ho2, iu5-goan5 oah8--teh.
17). KhoaN3 ah, goa2 siu7 chin-toa7 e5 kan-khou2, si7 ui7-tioh8 beh hou7 goa2 tit-tioh8 peng5-an;
Li2 in-ui7 thiaN3 goa2 e5 leng5-hun5, chiu7 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 biat8-bo5 e5 khiN;
In-ui7 Li2 chiong goa2 it-chhe3 e5 choe7, hiat ti7 Li2 e5 ka-chiah-au7.
18). In-ui7 im-kan boe7-oe7 kam2-sia7 Li2, si2-bo5 boe7-oe7 o-lo2 Li2;
Loh8 hun5-bong7 e5 lang5 boe7-oe7 ng3-bang7 Li2 e5 seng5-sit8.
19). Chi2-u7 oah8-lang5, oah8-lang5, beh kam2-sia7 Li2, chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 kam2-sia7 Li2 chit8-iuN7;
Choe3 lau7-pe7-e5 beh hou7 kiaN2-ji5 chai Li2 e5 seng5-sit8.
20). Ia5-ho5-hoa pian7-pian7 beh kiu3 goa2, 
Sou2-i2 goan2 chai7-siN e5 jit8 beh ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3,
Eng7 si-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3, chhiuN3 goa2 e5 si-koa.
	21). I2-sai3-a bat kong2, Tioh8 theh8 chit8 te3 bu5-hoa-ko2-piaN2, lai5 tah ti7 liap8-a2.  Ong5 chiu7 tit-tioh8 ho2.  22). Hi-se-ka ia7 bat kong2, Goa2 oe7 chiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, u7 sim2-mih8 tiau7-thau5?

[39]	Tng-si5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, Pa-lah8-tan3 e5 kiaN2 Bi2-lo5-tat8-pa-lah8-tan3 thiaN-kiN3 Hi-se-ka bat phoa3-piN7, chiu7 sang3 phoe-sin3 kap le2-mih8 hou7 Hi-se-ka.  2). Hi-se-ka in-ui7 su3-chia2 lai5 hoaN-hi2, chiu7 chiong i khng3 po2-mih8 e5 chhu3, kim, gun5, hiuN-liau7, kui3-khi3 e5 iu5, kap i e5 kun-chong-kek8, kap hu2-khou3-lai7 it-chhe3 sou2 u7--e5, long2 hou7 in khoaN3; i e5 ke-tiong kap choan5-kok e5 lai7-bin7, Hi-se-ka bo5 chit8-hang7 bo5 hou7 in khoaN3.  3). Tui3 an2-ni sian-ti I2-sai3-a lai5 kiN3 Hi-se-ka ong5, mng7 i kong2, Chiah e5 lang5 kong2 sim2-mih8? in tui3 toh-loh8 lai5 kiN3 li2? Hi-se-ka kong2, In tui3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5, lai5 kiN3 goa2.  4). I2-sai3-a kong2, In ti7 li2 e5 ke khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8? Hi-se-ka kong2, Hoan7-na7 goa2 ke-tiong sou2-u7--e5, in long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3; goa2 e5 chai5-po2 e5 tiong-kan bo5 chit8-hang7 bo5 hou7 in khoaN3-kiN3.  5). I2-sai3-a tui3 Hi-se-ka kong2, Li2 tioh8 thiaN ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  6). KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, hoan7-na7 li2 ke-lai7 sou2-u7--e5, kap li2 e5 liat8-chou2 chek-chu7 kau3 hian7-kim--e5 long2 beh siu7-chhiuN2 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, bo5 lau5 chit8-hang7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  7). Koh tui3 li2 pun2-sin siN e5 kiaN2-sun, ki5-tiong u7-e5 beh siu7-liah8--khi3, ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 ong5-kiong tng thai3-kam3.  8). Hi-se-ka tui3 I2-sai3-a kong2, Li2 sou2 thoan5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 si7 ho2.  Koh kong2, In-ui7 ti7 goa2 ni5-jit8 e5 tiong-kan beh u7 thai3-peng5 kap kian-kou3.

[40]	Lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 an-ui3, an-ui3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3.  2). Tioh8 tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kong2 ho2-oe7, koh po3 i chai, i e5 kau-chian3 i2-keng chin7, i e5 choe7-koa3 i2-keng sia3; i ui7-tioh8 i it-chhe3 e5 choe7, tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 ka-pe7 siu7 heng5-hoat8.
	3). U7 siaN kio3 kong2, Ti7 khong3-ia2 pi7-pan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou7, ti7 soa-bou5 e5 toe7, siu-piN5 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 toa7-lou7.  4). Chiah e5 soaN-kok long2 beh thun7 hou7 i tiN7, toa7-soe3 e5 soaN-thau5 long2 beh kut8 hou7 i ke7; oan-oat--e5, beh koe2 hou7 i tit8, kham5-khiat8--e5, beh siu hou7 i piN5.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng tek-khak hian2-hian7, hoan7-na7 u7 hiat-khi3-e5 beh long2 khoaN3-kiN3; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhin-chhui3 kong2--e5.
	6). U7 siaN kong2, Li2 tioh8 kio3, i kong2, Goa2 tioh8 kio3 sim2-mih8? kiN3-na7 u7 hiat-khi3--e5 long2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2, i e5 eng5-kng long2 chhin-chhiuN7 soaN--nih e5 hoe; chhau2 oe7 ta, hoe oe7 sia7;  7). in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 khi3 chhe ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7; peh-siN3 chin-chiaN3 si7 chhau2.  8). Chhau2 oe7 ta, hoe oe7 sia7; tok8-tok8 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7 tek-khak eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
	9). Po3 ho2 siau-sit hou7 Sek-an--e5 ah, li2 tioh8 chiuN7 koaiN5-soaN; po3 ho2 siau-sit hou7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2--e5 ah, li2 tioh8 chin7-lat8 chhut li2 e5 siaN; tioh8 chhut-siaN, m7-bian2 kiaN; tui3 Iu5-tai7 e5 siaN5 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  10). KhoaN3 ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chhin-chhiuN7 toa7 koan5-leng5--e5 lim5-kau3 , I e5 chhiu2 tek-khak ui7 I chiang2-koan5; khoaN3 ah, I e5 siuN2-su3 ti7 I hia, I e5 po3-tap iah8 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5.  11). I beh chhin-chhiuN7 bok8-chia2 kou3 I e5 iuN5-kun5, I beh eng7 chhiu2 aN5-oa2 iuN5-a2-kiaN2, pho7 i ti7 heng-cheng5, ban7-ban7 chhoa7 hiah-e5 hou7 iuN5-a2 suh-lin--e5.
	12). Chi7-chui7 bat eng7 chhiu2-sim niu5 chiah e5 chui2, eng7 chhiu2-hou2-khau2 niu5 kiong-chhong, eng7 tau2 toe2 toa7-toe7 e5 thou5-hun2, eng7 chhin3 chhin3 soaN-nia2, eng7 thian-pheng5 pheng5 soaN-thau5 ah?  13). Chi7-chui7 bat chhek-tok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sim, a2-si7 choe3 I e5 bou5-su7 lai5 chi2-kau3 I ah?  14). I kap chi7-chui7 siong-liong5, chi7-chui7 ka3-si7 I, chiong kong-peng5 e5 lou7 chi2-si7 I, koh chiong ti3-sek ka3-si7 I, chiong thong-tat8 e5 to7-lou7 chi2-kau3 I ah?  15). KhoaN3 ah, ban7 peh-siN3 long2 chhin-chhiuN7 chui2-thang2 e5 chit8-tih-chui2, koh chhin-chhiuN7 thian-pheng5-teng2 e5 tin5-ai; I theh8 chiah e5 hai2-su7 khi2-lai5 chhin-chhiuN7 kek8 bi5-soe3 e5 mih8.  16). Li7-pa-lun3 bo5 kau3-giah8 thang choe3 he2-chha5, ki5-tiong e5 chau2-siu3 bo5 kau3-giah8 choe3 sio-che3.  17). Ban7 peh-siN3 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 mih8; hou7 I khoaN3 kek8-ki5 bo5, chiu7-si7 khang-khang.
	18). Lin2 kiu3-keng3 beh chiong chi7-chui7 pi2-pheng7 Siong7-te3? eng7 sim2-mih8 heng5-siong7 kap Siong7-te3 pi2-pheng7 ah?  19). Ngou2-siong7 si7 sai-hu7 chu3-cho7, gun5-chhiuN7 eng7 kim an--i, ka7 i chu3 gun5-lian7.  20). Song3-hiong lang5 bo5 lat8 thang hian3 chit-ho7 mih8, chiu7 keng2 boe7-oe7 hiu2-hoai7 e5 chha5, ui7 i chhe7 ki5-khiau2 e5 sai-hu7, chhai7 boe7-oe7 io5-tang7 e5 ngou2-siong7.  21). Lin2 kiam2 be7 chai mah? lin2 kiam2 be7 thiaN-kiN3 mah? tui3 khi2-thau5 kiam2 bo5 ka7 lin2 kong2 mah? tui3 siat-lip8 toe7 e5 kun-ki lin2 kiam2 bo5 beng5-pek8 mah?  22). Chu2 che7 ti7 toe7 e5 toa7-khoan5, toe7-chiuN7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-meh; I tian2-khui thiN chhin-chhiuN7 tiuN3-pak, an-ti3 i, chhin-chhiuN7 thang khia7-khi2 e5 pou3-piN5.  23). I hou7 kun-ong5 kui ti7 bo5; hou7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 sim2-phoaN3-koaN chiaN5-choe3 khang-hu.  24). In si7 tu2-a2 chai, tu2-a2 cheng3; i e5 chang5 tu2-a2 teng3-kun ti7 toe7--nih; I chit8-e7 chhe ti7 i teng2-bin7, chiu7 long2 kou-ta5, kng2-le5-hong chiong i chhe--khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-iu3 chit8-iuN7.  25). Chi3-seng3-e5 kong2, Lin2 beh eng7 chi7-chui7 pi2-pheng7 Goa2, hou7 Goa2 kap i piN5 ah?  26). Lin2 kiah8-bak8 khoaN3 teng2-bin7, khoaN3 chi7-chui7 chhong3-cho7 chiah-e5, chiau3 siau3-bak8 chhoa7 hiah e5 ban7-kun chhut-lai5; I chit8-e5 chit8-e5 chheng in e5 mia5; in-ui7 I e5 koan5-leng5, koh in-ui7 I e5 toa7 koan5-leng5, toa7 khui3-lat8, lian5 chit8-e5 iah8 bo5 khiam3.
	27). Nga2-kok ah, li2 siaN2-su7 kong2, I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 siaN2-su7 kong2, Goa2 e5 to7-lou7 un2-bat8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goa2 e5 an3-kiaN7 bo5 tit-tioh8 Siong7-te3 liau7-li2.  28). Li2 kiam2 be7 chai mah? Li2 kiam2 be7 thiaN-kiN3 mah? eng2-eng2 ti7-teh e5 Siong7-te3, Ia5-ho5-hoa, chhong3-cho7 toe7-kek8--e5, I bo5 ia3, iah8 bo5 sian7; I e5 ti3-hui7 bo5 thang chhek-tok8.  29). Ia3-sian7--e5 I hou7 i leng5-lek8; nng2-chiaN2-e5, I ke-thiN i e5 khui3-lat8.  30). Siau3-lian5 lang5 iah8 oe7 ia3 oe7 sian7, iong2-chong3 e5 lang5 iah8 oe7 poah8-to2.  31). Tok8-tok8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5 beh tit-tioh8 sin e5 khui3-lat8; in beh chhin-chhiuN7 eng-chiau2 thi2-sit8 pe-koaiN5; in chau2, iah8 bo5 ia3; kiaN5 iah8 bo5 sian7.

[41]	Cheng3 hai2-su7 ah, tioh8 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 cheng7-cheng7; cheng3 peh-siN3 tioh8 tit-tioh8 sin e5 khui3-lat8; long2 tioh8 kun7-cheng5 lai5, chiah thang lai5 kong2-oe7; lan2 thang tai7-ke lai5 pian7-lun7.  2). Chi7-chui7 tui3 tang-hng heng-khi2 chit8-lang5, eng7 kong-gi7 tiau3 i lai5 kau3 I e5 kha-cheng5 ah? chiong liat8-kok kau-hou7 i, hou7 i koan2-hat kun-ong5; chiong in chhin-chhiuN7 tin5-ai kau hou7 i e5 to, chhin-chhiuN7 hong-chhe e5 chhau2-a2-iu3 kau-hou7 i e5 keng.  3). I tui-koaN2 in, kiaN5 i sou2 be7-bat kiaN5 e5 lou7, an-jian5 ke3-khi3.  4). Chi7-chui7 choe3 chit-e5 lai5 chiaN5--i, tui3 khi2-thau5 tiau3 lek8-tai7 ah? Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, si7 khi2-thau5 e5, iah8 si7 lou7-be2--e5, Goa2 chiu7-si7 I.  5). Hai2-su7 khoaN3-kiN3 chiu7 kiaN-hiaN5; toe7-kek8 iah8 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, chiu7 kun7-oa2 lai5.  6). In tak8-lang5 saN pang-chan7; tui3 hiaN-ti7 kong2, Tioh8 chong3-taN2.  7). Bak8-chhiuN7 bian2-le7 gun5-chhiuN7; eng7 thui5 phah-kng--e5 bian2-le7 phah-tiam--e5, lun7 hoaN7-ioh8 e5 kang-hu kong2, HoaN7-liau2 ho2; koh eng7 teng teng3-tiau5, hou7 i bo5 io5-tang7.
	8). Tok8-tok8 li2, I2-sek-liat8, si7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8; Nga2-kok si7 Goa2 sou2 keng2-soan2 e5, Goa2 e5 peng5-iu2 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 hou7-e3;  9). li2 si7 Goa2 tui3 toe7-kek8 sou2 toa3--lai5-e5, tui3 toe7 e5 kak-thau5 sou2 tiau3--lai5-e5, koh tui3 li2 kong2, Li2 si7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8, Goa2 keng2-soan2 li2, iah8 bo5 khi3-choat8 li2.  10). Li2 boh8-tit kiaN-hiaN5, in-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 saN-kap ti7-teh; boh8-tit lun2-neh, in-ui7 Goa2 si7 li2 e5 Siong7-te3; Goa2 tek-khak kian-kou3 li2, Goa2 tek-khak pang-chan7 li2, Goa2 tek-khak eng7 Goa2 kong-gi7 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 hu5-chhi5 li2.  11). KhoaN3 ah, hoan7-na7 toa7 siu7-khi3 li2--e5, tek-khak long2 lau3-khui3 kian3-siau3; kap li2 saN-chiN--e5 tek-khak chhin-chhiuN7 bo5, iah8 beh biat8-bo5.  12). Kap li2 saN-chiN--e5, li2 beh chhe7 in, iah8 chhe7 bo5; kap li2 cheng-chian3--e5, beh chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 mih8, chiaN5-choe3 khang-hu.  13). In-ui7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 e5 Siong7-te3, beh khan li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2, ka7 li2 kong2, M7-bian2 kiaN, Goa2 beh pang-chan7 li2.  14). Chhin-chhiuN7 tou7-un2 e5 Nga2-kok, kap lin2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, m7-bian2 kiaN; Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh pang-chan7 li2, kiu3-siok8 li2--e5 chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5.  15). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 choe3 phah gou7-kak sin e5 khi3-ku7, lai7 koh u7-khi2; li2 beh chiong soaN-nia2 phah kau3 chhui3-chhui3, hou7 soaN-thau5 chhin-chhiuN7 chhou-khng.  16). Li2 beh poa3--in, hong beh ka7 in chhe--khi3, kng2-le5-hong beh ka7 in sau3--khi3; chong2-si7 li2 beh in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 hoaN-hi2, in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 lai5 khoa-khau2.
	17). Song3-hiong khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 chhe7 chui2, iah8 chhe7 bo5; in in-ui7 chhui3 khoah, chih8 ta; Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh in3--in, Goa2 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 tek-khak bo5 pang3-sak in.  18). Goa2 beh ti7 bo5-chhau2 e5 soaN khui kang-ho5, ti7 soaN-kok-tiong khui chui2-choaN5; Goa2 beh hou7 soa-bou5 piN3-choe3 chui2-ti5, hou7 ta-toe7 piN3-choe3 chui2-choaN5.  19). Goa2 beh ti7 khong3-ia2 chai pek-hiuN-chhiu7, cho7-kiap-chhiu7, kong-liam-chhiu7, kap ia2 kaN-na2-chhiu7; Goa2 ti7 soa-bou5 beh chiong siong5-chhiu7, sam-chhiu7, kap ng5-iong5-chhiu7 choe3 chit8-e7 chai;  20). thang hou7 lang5 lai5 khoaN3, lai5 chai lai5 siuN7, saN-kap beng5-pek8; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5, si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 sou2 chhong3-cho7--e5.
	21). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 tioh8 the5-khi2 lin2 e5 an3-kiaN7; Nga2-kok e5 Jin5-kun kong2, Lin2 tioh8 pai5-liat8 lin2 u7 cheng3-ku3 e5 li2-iu5.  22). In tioh8 pai5-liat8 i, tioh8 hou7 goan2 chai chiong-lai5 beh chaiN2-iuN7; hou7 goan2 chai i2-cheng5 e5 su7 si7 sim2-mih8, hou7 goan2 thang kang2-kiu3, tit-tioh8 chai su7 e5 kiat-kiok8; a2-si7 chiong beh lai5 e5 su7 kong2 hou7 goan2 thiaN.  23). Tioh8 hou7 goan2 chai chiong-lai5 e5 su7, thang hou7 goan2 chai lin2 si7 siong7-te3; hek8-si7 ho2, hek8-si7 phaiN2, lin2 tioh8 kiaN5 i, hou7 goan2 gong5-ngiah8 lai5 saN-kap khoaN3.  24). KhoaN3 ah, lin2 siok8 ti7 bo5, lin2 e5 sou2-choe3 siok8 ti7 khang-hu; hit-e5 keng2-soan2 lin2--e5 si7 kho2-ouN3.
	25). Goa2 tui3 pak-hng heng-khi2 chit8-lang5, i chiu7 lai5; i tui3 jit8-chhut e5 sou2-chai7 kiu5-kio3 Goa2 e5 mia5--e5; i beh tah8 chiang2-koan5--e5 chhin-chhiuN7 he-thou5, chhin-chhiuN7 sio-hui5 sai-hu7 tah8-thou5 chit8-iuN7.  26). Chi7-chui7 tui3 khi2-thau5 kong2-beng5 chit e5 su7, hou7 goan2 chai; chi7-chui7 tui3 khi2-thau5 kong2-beng5, hou7 goan2 kong2, I bo5-chho3 ah? chong2-si7 bo5 u7 kong2-beng5, bo5 u7 pai5-liat8, bo5 u7 thiaN-kiN3 lin2 e5 oe7--e5.  27). Goa2 tai7-seng tui3 Sek-an kong2, KhoaN3 ah, khoaN3 ah; Goa2 beh chiong chit8-ui7 po3 ho2 siau-sit--e5 siuN2-su3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  28). Goa2 khoaN3 i, bo5 chit8-lang5; in tiong-kan iah8 bo5 bou5-su7, ti7 Goa2 mng7 e5 si5, thang in3 chit8-ku3.  29). KhoaN3 ah, in long2-si7 khang-hu, in e5 sou2-choe3 si7 bo5-mih8; in sou2 chu3 e5 ngou2-siong7 long2-si7 hong, long2-si7 khang-hu e5.

[42]	 KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8, Goa2 sou2 hu5-chhi5 e5, Goa2 sou2 keng2-soan2 e5, Goa2 e5 sim sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5, Goa2 u7 chiong Goa2 e5 sin5 hou7 i, i beh chiong kong-li2 thoan5 hou7 goa7-pang.  2). I bo5 soan-hoa, bo5 chhut-siaN, iah8 bo5 hou7 koe-lou7--nih thiaN-kiN3 i e5 siaN.  3). Siu7-siong e5 lou5-ui2, i bo5 at-chih8, beh hoa e5 teng-he2, i bo5 phah-sit; i chiau3 chin-sit8, chiong kong-li2 thoan5-pou3.  4). I bo5 chhin3-sim, iah8 bo5 sit-taN2, tit8-kau3 i ti7 toe7-chiuN7 siat-lip8 kong-li2; hai2-su7 long2 theng3-hau7 i e5 ka3-si7.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3, chhong3-cho7 chiah e5 thiN lai5 thi2-khui i, khui-khoah toe7 kap i sou2-chhut--e5, eng7 oah8-khi3 hou7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, eng7 sin5-hun5 hou7 kiaN5 ti7 hit teng2-bin7 e5 lang5 e5, kong2,  6). Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 kong-gi7 tiau3--li2, beh khan li2 e5 chhiu2, po2-siu2 li2, hou7 li2 choe3 peh-siN3 e5 iok e5 tiong-po2, choe3 goa7-pang lang5 e5 kng;  7). lai5 khui chhiN-mi5 e5 bak8-chiu, chhoa7 siu7-koaiN--e5 chhut-kaN; hou7 tiam3 ti7 ou-am3--e5 chhut kaN-lo5.  8). Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, che si7 Goa2 e5 mia5, Goa2 bo5 chiong Goa2 e5 eng5-kng kui hou7 pat8 e5 sin5, iah8 bo5 chiong Goa2 e5 mia5-siaN kui-hou7 tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7.  9). KhoaN3 ah, cheng5 e5 su7 i2-keng chiaN5, taN Goa2 iah8 beh chiong sin e5 su7 kong2-beng5; chiah e5 su7 be7 hoat-khi2 i2-cheng5, Goa2 chiu7 kong2 hou7 lin2 thiaN.  10). Ke3-hai2-e5, kap hai2-lai7 sou2-u7--e5, hai2-su7 kap ki5-tiong khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, long2 tioh8 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiuN3 sin e5 koa, tui3 toe7-kek8 o-lo2 I.  11). Khong3-ia2 kap ki5-tiong e5 siaN5, kap Ki-tat8 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 hiuN-sia7, long2 tioh8 chhut-siaN; Se-lah8 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 tioh8 chhiuN3-koa, ti7 soaN-teng2--e5 tioh8 chhut toa7-siaN.  12). In tioh8 chiong eng5-kng kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ti7 hai2-su7-tiong po3-iong5 I e5 mia5-siaN.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chhin-chhiuN7 iong2-beng2 e5 lang5 chhut-khi3; beh chhin-chhiuN7 kau-chian3 e5 lang5 kek-tong7 jiat8-sim ; beh au5-kio3, toa7-siaN hoah, beh eng7 toa7 khui3-lat8 kong-kek I e5 tui3-tek8.  14). Goa2 ku2-ku2 bo5 khui-chhui3, cheng7-cheng7 ka-ki7 at-chi2; taN Goa2 beh au5-kio3, chhin-chhiuN7 beh siN e5 hu7-jin5-lang5; Goa2 beh ha7-ha7-chhoan2 boe7 chih khui3.  15). Goa2 beh hou7 toa7-soaN sio2-soaN piN3-choe3 pha-hng, hou7 hit teng2-bin7 e5 hoe-chhau2 long2 kou-ta5; Goa2 beh hou7 kang-ho5 piN3-choe3 chiu-su7, hou7 chui2-ti5 long2 ta--khi3.  16). Goa2 beh chhoa7 chhiN-mi5--e5 kiaN5 in m7-bat e5 to7-lou7; chhoa7 in kiaN5 m7-bat e5 lou7-keng3; ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 hou7 ou-am3 piN3-choe3 kng-beng5, hou7 oan-khiau piN3-choe3 piN5-tit8.  Chiah e5 su7 Goa2 long2 beh kiaN5, iah8 bo5 pang3-sak in.  17). Oa2-kho3 tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7, tui3 chu3-cho7 e5 ngou2-siong7 kong2, Li2 si7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3, chit-ho7 lang5 siu7 koaN2-chau2, toa7 kian3-siau3.
	18). Lin2 chhau3-hi7-lang5-e5 tioh8 thiaN; lin2 chhiN-mi5--e5 tioh8 khoaN3, hou7 lin2 oe7 khoaN3-kiN3.  19). Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 i2-goa7, chi7-chui7 chhiN-mi5 ah? Chi7-chui7 chhau2-hi7 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 sou2 chhe e5 su3-chia2 ah? chi7-chui7 chhiN-mi5 chhin-chhiuN7 hit-e5 kap Goa2 ho5-ho2--e5, a2-si7 chhiN-mi5 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou5-pok8 ah?  20). Li2 khoaN3-kiN3 choe7-choe7 tai7-chi3 iah8 bo5 chu3-i3; khui hi7-khang, ia7 bo5 thiaN-kiN3.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa in-ui7 ka-ki7 e5 kong-gi7, hoaN-hi2 hou7 lut8-hoat choe3 toa7 choe3 chun-kui3.  22). Chong2-si7 chit e5 peh-siN3 si7 siu7 chhiuN2-toat8--e5; ti7 soaN-hiat8 siu7 tng-tioh8, koaiN-bat8 ti7 kaN--nih; in hou7 lang5 liah8-tioh8, bo5 lang5 chin2-kiu3; hou7 lang5 chhiuN2-liah8--khi3, bo5 lang5 kong2, Pang3 i to3--khi3.  23). Lin2 tiong-kan chi7-chui7 kheng2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN che? chi7-chui7 kheng2 liu5-sim, au7-lai5 thiaN-than3 i ah?  24). Chi7-chui7 chiong Nga2-kok kau i hou7 lang5 chhiuN2, chiong I2-sek-liat8 kau hou7 chhat8 ah? kiam2-m7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lan2 sou2 tek-choe7--e5 mah? in m7-kheng2 kiaN5 I e5 to7-lou7, iah8 m7-kheng2 thiaN-than3 I e5 lut8-hoat.  25). Sou2-i2 I chiong beng2-liat8 e5 siu7-khi3, kap cheng-chian3 e5 hiong5-beng2, piaN3 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7; ti7 i e5 si3-ui5 chhin-chhiuN7 he2-toh8, i iau2 m7-chai; he2 sio-tioh8 i, i iah8 bo5 khoa3-i3.

[43]	Nga2-kok ah, chhong3-cho7 li2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 ah, hit e5 cho7-chiaN5 li2--e5, an2-ni kong2, Li2 m7-sai2 kiaN, in-ui7 Goa2 kiu3-siok8 li2; Goa2 bat kio3 li2 e5 mia5, tiau3 li2; li2 si7 Goa2-e5.  2). Li2 tui3 chui2-tiong keng-ke3, Goa2 tek-khak kap li2 saN-kap ti7-teh; li2 keng-ke3 kang-ho5, chui2 tek-khak bo5 im-bat8 li2; li2 tui3 he2-tiong kiaN5-ke3--khi3, tek-khak bo5 siu7 sio; he2-iam7 iah8 bo5 toh8 ti7 li2 e5 sin-chiuN7.  3). In-ui7 Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5, li2 e5 Kiu3-chu2; Goa2 i2-keng hou7 Ai-kip8 choe3 li2 siok8-hoe5 e5 ke3-chiN5, hou7 Kou2-sit8 kap Se-pa choe3 li2 e5 thoe3-sin.  4). In-ui7 Goa2 khoaN3 li2 choe3 po2-poe3, choe3 chun-kui3, koh in-ui7 Goa2 thiaN3 li2, sou2-i2 Goa2 hou7 lang5 thoe3 li2, hou7 liat8-kok e5 lang5 thoe3 li2 e5 siN3-mia7.  5). Boh8-tit kiaN, in-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 saN-kap ti7-teh; Goa2 beh chhoa7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 tui3 tang-hng lai5, koh tui3 sai-hng chio-chip8 li2.  6). Goa2 beh tui3 pak-hng kong2, Pang3--chhut-lai5; tui3 lam5-hng kong2, Boh8-tit khu-liu5; chiong Goa2 e5 cheng3-kiaN2 tui3 hng7-hng7 chhoa7--lai5, chiong Goa2 e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tui3 toe7-kek8 chhoa7 to3-lai5.  7). KiN3-na7 eng7 Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5 chheng--e5 si7 Goa2 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 eng5-kng chhong3-cho7--e5; si7 Goa2 sou2 choe3-chiaN5, sou2 chhong3-cho7 e5.
	8). Li2 tioh8 chiong u7 bak8-chiu iah8 chhiN-mi5, u7 hi7-khang iah8 chhau3-hi7-lang5 e5 peh-siN3, long2-chong2 chhoa7 i chhut-lai5.  9). Ban7-kok tioh8 chu7-chip7, cheng3 peh-siN3 tioh8 chu7-hoe7; ki5-tiong chi7-chui7 oe7 chiong chit-e5 kong2-beng5, iah8 chiong cheng5 e5 su7 kong2 hou7 goan2 thiaN ah? in thang chhoa7 kan-cheng3 lai5, ka-ki7 hian2-beng5 in choe3-tioh8, a2-si7 in thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 kong2, Che si7 chin-sit8.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 si7 Goa2 e5 kan-cheng3 e5, si7 Goa2 sou2 keng2 e5 lou5-pok8; hou7 lin2 chai lai5 sin3 Goa2, koh beng5-pek8 Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; ti7 Goa2 e5 tai7-seng bo5-u7 siu7-cho7 e5 Siong7-te3, ti7 Goa2 e5 i2-au7 iah8-bo5.  11). Chi2-u7 Goa2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; tu5 Goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 u7 kiu3-chu2.  12). Goa2 bat chi2-si7, Goa2 bat chin2-kiu3, Goa2 bat kong2-beng5, koh ti7 lin2 tiong-kan bo5 u7 pat8-iuN7 e5 Siong7-te3; sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 si7 Goa2 e5 kan-cheng3, Goa2 chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3.  13). Tui3 u7 jit8-chi2 i2-lai5, Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; bo5 chit8-e5 oe7 kiu3 lang5 thoat-li7 Goa2 e5 chhiu2; Goa2 beh kiaN5 tai7-chi3, chi7-chui7 oe7 chou2-chi2 ah?
	14). Kiu3-siok8 lin2 e5 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5, an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 lin2 e5 ian5-kou3, Goa2 i2-keng chhe lang5 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, koh Goa2 beh hou7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 pai7-loh8, chhin-chhiuN7 to5-chau2 e5 peh-siN3, long2 che7 in hoa7-hoa7-hau2 e5 chun5.  15). Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Seng3--e5, si7 chhong3-cho7 I2-sek-liat8--e5, si7 lin2 e5 Kun-ong5.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 toa7-hai2-tiong khui-lou7, ti7 toa7-chui2-tiong khui-lou7;  17). hou7 chhia, be2, peng-teng, iong2-beng2 e5 lang5 long2 chhut-lai5; (in choe3 chit8-e7 to2--loh8-khi3, boe7 koh khi2--lai5; in biat8-bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 sit--khi3 e5 he2;)  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 m7-thang ki3-liam7 cheng5 e5 su7, iah8 m7-thang siuN7 cha2-si5 e5 tai7-chi3.  19). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh choe3 chit8-hang7 sin e5 su7, taN teh hoat-hian7, lin2 kiam2 m7-chai mah? Goa2 beh ti7 khong3-ia2 khui to7-lou7, ti7 soa-bou5 khui kang-ho5.  20). SoaN--nih e5 chau2-siu3 beh chun-tiong7 Goa2, soaN-kau2 kap to5-chiau2 iah8 beh an2-ni; in-ui7 Goa2 hou7 khong3-ia2 u7 chui2, hou7 soa-bou5 u7 ho5, thang hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 sou2-keng2--e5, lim.  21). Chit e5 peh-siN3 si7 Goa2 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 sou2 cho7--e5, beh po3-iong5 Goa2 e5 mia5-siaN.
	22). Nga2-kok ah, li2 bo5 u7 kiu5-kio3 Goa2; I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 hoan2-tng2 iam3-hoan5 Goa2.  23). Li2 bo5 toa3 li2 e5 iuN5 choe3 sio-che3 lai5 hou7 Goa2; iah8 bo5 u7 eng7 che3-mih8 chun-keng3 Goa2.  Goa2 bo5 in-ui7 sou2-hian3 e5 mih8 hou7 li2 tioh8-boa5, iah8 bo5 in-ui7 ju2-hiuN hou7 li2 ia3-sian7.  24). Li2 bo5 eng7 gun5 ui7 Goa2 boe2 chhiong-pou5, iah8 bo5 eng7 che3-mih8 e5 iu5 hou7 Goa2 pa2-chiok; hoan2-tng2 hou7 Goa2 in-ui7 li2 e5 choe7-ok tioh8-boa5, hou7 Goa2 in-ui7 li2 e5 choe7-koa3 ia3-sian7.  25). Chi2-u7 Goa2 in-ui7 ka-ki7 e5 ian5-kou3, chhat-biat8 li2 chiah e5 ke3-sit; Goa2 iah8 bo5 ki3-liam7 li2 chiah e5 choe7-ok.  26). Li2 tioh8 tiam2-chhiN2 Goa2; li2 Goa2 thang saN-kap pian7-lun7; li2 thang pai5-liat8 li2 e5 cheng5-li2, thang tit-tioh8 chheng-choe3-gi7.  27). Li2 khai-ki e5 chou2 hoan7-choe7, li2 e5 tiong-po2 poe7-gek8 Goa2.  28). Sou2-i2 Goa2 beh leng5-jiok8 seng3-sou2 e5 siu2-leng2, hou7 Nga2-kok siu7 chiu3-chou2, hou7 I2-sek-liat8 siu7 loe2-me7.

[44]	Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok, Goa2 sou2 keng2 e5 I2-sek-liat8 ah, taN li2 tioh8 thiaN.  2). Cho7-chiaN5 li2, koh tui3 thai--nih cho7-chiu7 li2, iah8 beh pang-chan7 li2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok, Goa2 sou2 keng2 e5 Ia5-su-lun5 ah, m7-bian2 kiaN.  3). In-ui7 Goa2 beh chiong chui2 piaN3 hou7 chhui3-ta e5 lang5, chiong ho5-chui2 koan3-ak ta-toe7; Goa2 beh chiong Goa2 e5 sin5 kang3-loh8 ti7 li2 e5 hou7-e3, chiong Goa2 e5 hok-khi3 kang3-loh8 ti7 li2 e5 kiaN2-sun.  4). In beh hoat-siN ti7 chhau2-tiong, chhin-chhiuN7 khoe-piN e5 liu2-chhiu7.  5). Chit-e5 beh kong2, Goa2 si7 siok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5; hit-e5 beh eng7 Nga2-kok e5 mia5 ka-ki7 chheng; koh chit-e5 beh chhin-chhiu2 sia2, kui ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5; iah8 beh eng7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 mia5 ka-ki7 chheng.
	6). Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 ong5, kiu3-siok8 e5 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 si7 khi2-thau5--e5, Goa2 si7 lou7-be2--e5; Goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 u7 Siong7-te3.  7). Tui3 Goa2 siat-lip8 kou2-cha2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 si5 chi7-chui7 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 kio3 i, kong2-beng5--i, ka7 Goa2 pai5-liat8 ah? hou7 in chiong be7-lai5 e5 su7 kap beh-chiaN5 e5 tai7-chi3 kong2-beng5.  8). Lin2 m7-bian2 lun2, iah8 m7-bian2 kiaN; Goa2 kiam2-m7-si7 tui3 kou2-cha2 chiu7 kong2-beng5, chi2-si7 li2 mah? koh lin2 si7 Goa2 e5 kan-cheng3, Goa2 i2-goa7 kiam2 u7 Siong7-te3 mah? sit8-chai7 bo5 u7 Chioh8-poaN5; Goa2 m7-bat u7 pat8-e5.
	9). Che3-cho7 tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7--e5 it-chin7 khang-hu; in sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5 long2 bo5 li7-ek; in e5 kan-cheng3 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 iah8 m7-chai, ti3-kau3 in kian3-siau3.  10). Chi7-chui7 che3-cho7 sin5-put8, chu3-cho7 bo5 li7-ek e5 ngou2-siong7?  11). KhoaN3 ah, i e5 tang5-phoaN7 long2 beh kian3-siau3; kang-chhiuN7 put-ko3 si7 lang5; chhut-chai7 in chu7-hoe7, chhut-chai7 in khia7--teh; long2 beh kiaN-hiaN5, saN-kap kian3-siau3.  12). Thih-chhiuN7 cho7 pou2-thau5, eng7 he2-thoaN3 thoan3-lian7, eng7 thui5 phah i, eng7 i u7-lat8 e5 chhiu2 lai5 tui5 i ti3-kau3 iau bo5 lat8; bo5 lim-chui2 lai5 ia3-sian7.  13). Bak8-chhiuN7 khan chin5-soaN3; eng7 pit ui7 i, eng7 lai7-to khek i, eng7 iN5-chhioh ui7-bou5, hong2 lang5 e5 heng5, choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 e5 sui2, tiam3 ti7 chhu3-lai7.  14). I chho3 pek-hiuN-chhiu7, koh chhu2 lek-chhiu7, kap siong7-chhiu7; ti7 chhiu7-na5-lai7 keng2 tiaN7-tioh8 chit8-chang5; i chai-cheng3 chheng5-chhiu7, tit-tioh8 hou7 ak toa7-chang5.  15). Chit-ho7 chhiu7 lang5 eng7 lai5 hiaN5-he2; eng7 i lai5 hang-sio; koh sio i lai5 pek-piaN2; iah8 koh chng sin5-put8 lai5 kui7-pai3; khek ngou2-siong7 lai5 khap8-thau5 pai3.  16). Eng7 chit8-hun7 sio ti7 he2--nih; eng7 chit8-hun7 chu2 bah lai5 chiah8; pek bah lai5 chiah8-pa2; ka-ki7 hang-sio kong2, A-ha7, goa2 hang-sio lah, goa2 kiN3-tioh8 he2 lah.  17). I eng7 chhun--e5 chng chit8-sian sin5-put8, chiu7-si7 tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7; i phak-loh8 pai3 i, ki5-to2 i kong2, Kiu5 li2 kiu3 goa2, in-ui7 li2 si7 goa2 e5 siong7-te3.  18). In m7-chai, iah8 boe7 siuN7, in-ui7 I kou5 in e5 bak8-chiu, hou7 in boe7 khoaN3-kiN3, that-bat8 in e5 sim, hou7 in boe7 beng5-pek8.  19). Bo5 lang5 hiau2-ngou7, bo5 ti3-sek, bo5 chhang-mia5, oe7 hiau2 kong2, Goa2 bat theh8 chit8-hun7 ti7 he2--nih sio, ti7 i he2-thoaN3-teng2 pek piaN2, sio-bah lai5 chiah8; chit e5 chhun--e5, goa2 kiam2 thang choe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 mih8 mah? goa2 kiam2 thang tui3 chha5-thau5 khap8-pai3 mah?  20). I eng7 he2-hu choe3 chiah8-mih8; i e5 sim hun-be5, hou7 i chha-biu7, i boe7-oe7 ka-ki7 kiu3, iah8 boe7-oe7 kong2, Goa2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2-lai7 kiam2 m7-si7 u7 peh8-chhat8 mah?
	21). Nga2-kok ah, I2-sek-liat8 ah, in-ui7 li2 si7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8, tioh8 ki3-tit chiah e5 su7; I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 si7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8, Goa2 cho7-chiu7 li2, tek-khak bo5 boe7-ki3-tit li2.  22). Goa2 chhat-biat8 li2 e5 ke3-sit, chhin-chhiuN7 bat8-hun5 siau-soaN3; Goa2 chhat-biat8 li2 e5 choe7-ok, chhin-chhiuN7 poh8-hun5 bo5--khi3; li2 tioh8 kui-ng3 Goa2; in-ui7 Goa2 kiu3-siok8 li2.  23). Chiah e5 thiN ah, eng-kai tioh8 chhiuN3-koa, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng choe3-chiaN5 i; toe7 e5 chhim e5 sou2-chai7 ah, eng-kai chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN; chiah e5 soaN eng-kai chhut-siaN chhiuN3-koa; chhiu7-na5 kap ki5-tiong sou2-u7 e5 chhiu7 long2 tioh8 an2-ni; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 kiu3-siok8 Nga2-kok, iah8 beh ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tit-tioh8 eng5-kng.
	24). Tui3 thai--nih cho7-chiu7 li2--e5, kiu3-siok8 li2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 cho7-chiaN5 ban7-mih8--e5, si7 ka-ki7 tian2-khui chiah e5 thiN, khui-khoah toa7-toe7--e5; (chi7-chui7 kap Goa2 ti7-teh ah?)  25). hou7 kong2 ke2-oe7 e5 tiau7-thau5 bo5 kong-hau7, hou7 chiam-pok e5 lang5 tian-kong5; hou7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 the3-au7, hou7 i e5 ti3-sek piN3-choe3 gu5-gong7;  26). hou7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 e5 oe7 eng3-giam7, Goa2 e5 su3-chia2 e5 ke3-ek8 tit-tioh8 chiaN5; lun7-kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kong2, Tek-khak u7 lang5 khia7-khi2; lun7-kau3 Iu5-tai7 e5 siaN5 kong2, Tek-khak siu7 khi2-cho7; i pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7 Goa2 beh hou7 i heng-khi2;  27). tui3 chhim-ian kong2, Li2 tioh8 ta--khi3, Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 li2 e5 kang-ho5 ta-la--khi3;  28). lun7 Kou2-liat8 kong2, I si7 Goa2 sou2-eng7 e5 bok8-chia2, beh chiaN5 Goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5; lun7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 i chiu7 kong2, I beh siu7 khi2-cho7, tian7-tng5 e5 toe7-ki iah8 beh kian3-lip8.

[45]	Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 boah-iu5 e5 Kou2-liat8, Goa2 khan i e5 chiaN3-chhiu2, hou7 liat8-kok hang5-hok8 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, Goa2 iah8 beh thau2 liat8-ong5 e5 io-toa3; hou7 siaN5-mng5 khui ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, koh chiah e5 mng5 tek-khak bo5 koaiN;  2). Goa2 tui3 i an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh kiaN5 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, siu-piN5 kham5-khiat8 e5 toe7; Goa2 beh phah-phoa3 tang5 e5 mng5, cham7-tng7 thih e5 chhoaN3.  3). Goa2 beh chiong am3-tiong e5 po2-mih8, kap un2-bat8 e5 chai5-po2 siuN2-su3 li2, hou7 li2 chai kio3-mia5 tiau3 li2--e5 chiu7-si7 Goa2, Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3.  4). In-ui7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok, Goa2 sou2 keng2 I2-sek-liat8 e5 ian5-kou3, Goa2 chiu7 kio3-mia5 tiau3--li2; li2 sui-jian5 m7-bat Goa2, Goa2 u7 chheng li2 e5 mia5.  5). Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ti7 Goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 u7 pat8-e5, tu5 Goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 u7 Siong7-te3; li2 sui-jian5 m7-bat Goa2, Goa2 beh ka7 li2 ha5-io;  6). tui3 jit8-chhut iah8 tui3 jit8-loh8 e5 sou2-chai7, hou7 lang5 long2 chai, tu5 Goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 u7 pat8-e5; Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ti7 Goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 u7 pat8-e5.  7). Goa2 cho7 kng, iah8 chhong3-cho7 am3; Goa2 cho7 peng5-an, iah8 chhong3-cho7 chai-e7; chiah-e5 long2 si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2-choe3--e5.
	8). Chiah e5 thiN ah, tui3 teng2-bin7 lai5 tih, kiong-chhong kang3-loh8 kong-gi7; toe7-bin7 lih8-khui, siN-chhut kiu3-un, hou7 kong-gi7 choe3 chit8-e7 hoat-siN; Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa bat chhong3-cho7 i.
	9). Chai-e7 ah, hit-e5 kap cho7 i e5 Chu2 ke3-kau3--e5, i put-ko3 si7 toe7-chiuN7 hia7-phiN3-tiong e5 chit8-te3 hia7-phiN3; thou5 kiam2 thang tui3 chhiau-i--e5 kong2, Li2 choe3 sim2-mih8? a2-si7 li2 sou2 choe3 e5 mih8 kiam2 thang kong2, I bo5 chhiu2 mah?  10). Chai-e7 ah, hit-e5 tui3 lau7-pe7 kong2, Li2 sou2-siN--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 ah? a2-si7 tui3 lau7-bu2 kong2, Li2 sou2-io--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 ah?  11). I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5, chiu7-si7 cho7 i e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chiong-lai5 e5 su7 lin2 thang mng7 Goa2; lun7-kau3 Goa2 chiah e5 kiaN2, i2-kip8 Goa2 e5 chhiu2 sou2-choe3--e5, lin2 thang kau-tai3 Goa2.  12). Goa2 cho7 toe7, iah8 chhong3-cho7 lang5 ti7 toe7-chiuN7; goa2 chhin-chhiu2 tian2-khui chiah e5 thiN, thiN-teng2 e5 ban7-siong7 iah8 si7 Goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7--e5.  13). Goa2 chiau3 kong-gi7 heng-khi2 Kou2-liat8, koh beh siu-tit8 i it-chhe3 e5 lou7; i beh khi2-cho7 Goa2 e5 siaN5, thau2-pang3 Goa2 siu7-liah8 e5 peh-siN3, m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 ke3-chiN5, iah8 m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 po3-siuN2; che si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.
	14). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Ai-kip8 tioh8-boa5 tit-tioh8--e5, Kou2-sit8 e5 chai5-li7, kap Se-pa e5 toa7-han3 lang5, long2 beh kui li2, siok8 li2, te3 li2; in beh koa3 thih-lian7 lai5 kui li2, phak-pai3 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, kiu5 lin2, kong2, Siong7-te3 chin-chiaN3 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan; chit-e5 i2-goa7 bo5 pat8-e5, koh bo5 pat8 e5 Siong7-te3.  15). Kiu3-chu2, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 sit8-chai7 si7 ka-ki7 un2-bat8 e5 Siong7-te3.  16). Hiah e5 chng ngou2-siong7--e5 long2 beh lau3-khui3 kian3-siau3, long2 choe3 chit8-e7 kian3-siau3.  17). chong2-si7 I2-sek-liat8 beh tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 eng2-oan2 e5 kiu3-un lai5 kiu3 in; lin2 tek-khak bo5 kian3-siau3, iah8 bo5 lau3-khui3, kau3 eng2 se3-tai7 bo5 soah.
	18). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhong3-cho7 chiah e5 thiN e5, I chiaN3-si7 Siong7-te3; I cho7 toe7 lai5 choe3-chiaN5 i; koh kian-kou3 i, m7-si7 khang-khang cho7, si7 chhong3-cho7 i hou7 lang5 khia7-khi2; I an2-ni kong2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, i2-goa7 bo5 pat8-e5.  19). Goa2 bo5 ti7 un2-bat8 a2-si7 ti7 ou-am3 toe7 e5 ui7 lai5 kong2; Goa2 m7-bat tui3 Nga2-kok e5 hou7-e3 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 khang-khang chhe7 Goa2; Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2-kong2--e5 si7 kong-gi7, sou2-thoan5--e5 si7 cheng3-tit8.
	20). Lin2 tui3 liat8-kok to5-thoat e5 lang5, lin2 tioh8 choe3-tin7 lai5, saN-kap oa2--lai5; hiah e5 kng tiau-khek ngou2-siong7 e5 chha5, ki5-to2 boe7-oe7 kiu3 lang5 e5 sin5-beng5--e5, long2 bo5 ti3-sek.  21). Lin2 tioh8 soan-thoan5, hou7 i chin3-cheng5 lai5, hou7 in tai7-ke chham-siong5; chi7-chui7 tui3 kou2-cha2 chi2-beng5 chit-e5? chi7-chui7 tui3 cha2-si5 soan-thoan5 chit-e5? kiam2-m7-si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa mah? Goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 koh u7 Siong7-te3; Goa2 si7 kong-gi7 e5 Siong7-te3, koh si7 Kiu3-chu2; Goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 pat8-e5.  22). Toe7-kek8 e5 lang5, long2 tioh8 giong2-bong7 Goa2 lai5 tit-tioh8 kiu3; in-ui7 Goa2 si7 Siong7-te3, bo5 koh u7 pat8-e5.  23). Goa2 ki2 ka-ki7 lai5 chiu3-choa7, Goa2 e5 chhui3 chiau3 kong-gi7 kong2-chhut chit e5 oe7, koat-toan3 bo5 siu to3-tng2, ban7 kha-thau5-u beh ng3 Goa2 lai5 kui7-pai3, ban7-chhui3 beh chi2 Goa2 lai5 chiu3-choa7.  24). U7 gi7-lun7 Goa2 kong2, Kong-gi7 leng5-lek8 tok8-tok8 chai7-ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lang5 long2 beh kui-oa2 I; hoan7-na7 siu7-khi3 I e5, tek-khak kian3-siau3.  25). I2-sek-liat8 e5 hou7-e3 long2 beh in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tit-tioh8 chheng-choe3-gi7, iah8 beh khoa-khau2.

[46]	Pi2-lek8 khut--loh8-khi3, Ni5-pho phak--loh8-khi3; in e5 ngou2-siong7 to5 ti7 siu3 kap cheng-siN e5 teng2-bin7; lin2 peng5-sou3 sou2 kng--e5, taN chiaN5-choe3 tang7-taN3, hou7 ia3-sian7 e5 cheng-siN chai3.  2). In long2 choe3 chit8-e7 phak--loh8-khi3, khut--loh8-khi3; boe7-oe7 kou3 in e5 tang7-taN3, pun2-sin iah8 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3.
	3). Nga2-kok ke, I2-sek-liat8 ke it-chhe3 iau2 chhun e5, tioh8 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7, lin2 tui3 chhut-si3 chiu7 hou7 Goa2 iang7 lin2, tui3 chhut-thai chiu7 hou7 Goa2 kui5-pho7.  4). Kau3 lin2 ni5-lau7, Goa2 iu5-goan5 si7 an2-ni, kau3 lin2 thau5-mng5 peh8, Goa2 iu5-goan5 kui5-pho7 lin2; Goa2 i2-keng cho7 lin2, iah8 beh iang7 lin2: Goa2 beh kui5-pho7 lin2, iah8 beh kiu3 lin2.  5). Lin2 beh chiong chi7-chui7 kap Goa2 saN-pi2, kap Goa2 tang5-teng2, thang kap Goa2 pi2-pheng7, hou7 goan2 saN-tang5 ah?  6). Tui3 te7-a2-lai7 piaN3-chhut kim, eng7 thian-pheng5 pheng5 gun5 e5 lang5, kou3 gun5-chhiuN7 che3-cho7 sin5-put8, in iah8 phak-loh8, iah8 kui7-pai3.  7). In chiu7 kng i ti7 keng-thau5-teng2, toa3 khi3 chhai7 ti7 i e5 sou2-chai7, i chiu7 tiaN7-tiaN7 khia7--teh; bo5 li7-khui i e5 pun2-ui7; lang5 kiu5-kio3 i, i boe7-oe7 in3, iah8 boe7 kiu3 lang5 thoat-li7 hoan7-lan7.  8). Lin2 tioh8 siau3-liam7 chit e5 su7, ka-ki7 choe3 tai7-tiong7-hu; poe7-gek8 e5 lang5 ah, tioh8 eng7 sim lai5 siuN7.  9). Lin2 tioh8 tui-liam7 te7-it kou2-cha2 e5 su7; in-ui7 Goa2 si7 Siong7-te3, i2-goa7 bo5 pat8-e5; Goa2 si7 Siong7-te3, koh bo5 pat8-e5 oe7 pi2-tit Goa2.  10). Goa2 tui3 khi2-thau5 chi2-beng5 lou7-be2 e5 su7, tui3 kou2-cha2 chi2-beng5 iau2-be7 chiaN5 e5 su7, kong2, Goa2 e5 ke3-ek8 tek-khak khia7-chai7, kiN3-na7 Goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5, Goa2 beh chiaN5 i.  11). Goa2 tiau3 eng-chiau2 tui3 tang-hng lai5, tiau3 hit-e5 chiaN5 Goa2 e5 ke3-ek8 e5 lang5 tui3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5, Goa2 i2-keng kong2-chhut tek-khak chiaN5--i; Goa2 i2-keng tiaN7-tioh8, iah8 tek-khak choe3 hou7 i chiaN5.  12). Lin2 chiah e5 ngi7-sim, li7-khui kong-gi7--e5, tioh8 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7.  13). Goa2 hou7 Goa2 e5 kong-gi7 kun7-oa2, tek-khak bo5 li7-khui hng7-hng7; Goa2 e5 kiu3-un tek-khak bo5 ian5-chhian5; Goa2 beh si kiu3-un ti7 Sek-an, kap Goa2 e5 eng5-kng ti7 I2-sek-liat8.

[47]	Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 chai7-sek-lu2 ah, loh8--lai5 che7 ti7 tin5-ai; Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 ah, bo5 cho7-ui7, tioh8 che7 ti7 thou5-kha; in-ui7 li2 bo5 koh chheng choe3 nng2-chiaN2 iu3-siu3 e5.  2). Tioh8 eng7 chioh8-bo7 bo7 beh8; tu5-khi3 li2 e5 phe3, thng3 li2 e5 tng5-saN, lou7-hian7 li2 e5 kha-thui2, liau5-ke3 khoe.  3). Li2 e5 e7-the2 beh lou7-hian7, li2 e5 kian3-siau3 beh hou7 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3; Goa2 beh po3-siu5, bo5 khoan-iong5 chit8-lang5.  4). Kiu3-siok8 goan2 e5 Chu2, I e5 mia5 si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3-e5.  5). Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 ah, li2 tioh8 cheng7-cheng7 che7, jip8 ti7 am3-tiong; in-ui7 li2 bo5 koh chheng choe3 liat8-kok e5 chu2-bu2.  6). Goa2 siu7-khi3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 hou7 Goa2 e5 san2-giap8 siu7 leng5-jiok8, chiong in kau ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2; li2 long2 bo5 lin5-bin2 in, chiong li2 kek8-tang7 e5 taN koa3 ti7 lau7-lang5 e5 sin-chiuN7.  7). Li2 ka-ki7 kong2, Goa2 beh eng2-eng2 choe3 chu2-bu2; sou2-i2 li2 bo5 chiong chiah e5 su7 khoa3 ti7 sim--nih, iah8 bo5 siuN7 i e5 kiat-kiok8.
	8). Li2 chit-e5 ian3-lok8, an-jian5 che7-e5, taN tioh8 thiaN chit e5 oe7, li2 sim-lai7 kong2, Chi2-u7 goa2, goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 pat8-e5; goa2 tek-khak bo5 ti3-kau3 chiu2-koaN2, iah8 bo5 tu2-tioh8 si2-kiaN2 e5 su7.  9). Chong2-si7 si2-kiaN2 chiu2-koaN2 chit nng7 kiaN7 su7, ti7 chit8-jit8 bak8-nih-ku2 e5 tiong-kan beh lim5-kau3 li2; ti7 li2 kiaN5 choe7-choe7 sia5-sut8, toa7-toa7 ui7-hu5 liam7-chiu3 e5 si5, chi2 nng7 hang7 su7 beh choan5-jian5 lim5-kau3 li2.  10). Li2 peng5-sou3 oa2-kho3 li2 e5 phaiN2, kong2, Bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2; li2 e5 ti3-hui7 chhang-mia5 be5-hek8 li2; koh li2 sim-lai7 kong2, Chi2-u7 goa2, goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 pat8-e5.  11). In-ui7 an2-ni chai-e7 beh lim5-kau3 li2; li2 m7-chai tui3 toh-loh8 lai5; chai-hai7 kau3-ti7 li2, li2 iah8 boe7-oe7 tu5--khi3; sou2-i2 m7-chai e5 hui2-biat8 iah8 beh hut-jian5 lim5-kau3 li2.  12). Tioh8 khi2-lai5 khia7, eng7 li2 e5 sia5-sut8 kap li2 choe7-choe7 e5 hu5-chiu3, chiu7-si7 tui3 li2 siau3-lian5 sou2 tioh8-boa5 hak8-sip8--e5, kiam2-chhai2 oe7 tit-tioh8 li7-ek, a2-si7 tit-tioh8 khah-iaN5.  13). Li2 e5 ke3-ek8 thai3-choe7, ti3-kau3 ia3-sian7; taN hou7 hiah-e5 koan thiN-siong7--e5, khoaN3 chhiN-sin5--e5, ti7 geh8-chhoe kong2 chham3-gu2 e5, long2 khi2-lai5, kiu3 li2 thoat-li7 sou2 beh lim5-kau3 li2 e5 su7.  14). KhoaN3 ah, in beh chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-a2 siu7 he2 sio; boe7-oe7 kiu3 ka-ki7 thoat-li7 he2-iam7 e5 lat8; iah8 bo5 he2-thoaN3 thang hang-sio, iah8 bo5 he2 thang che7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5.  15). Li2 sou2 tioh8-boa5 hak8-sip8 e5 su7 tui3-ti7 li2 long2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni; tui3 li2 siau3-lian5 e5 si5 kap li2 choe3 seng-li2--e5 iah8 tak8-lang5 to3-khi3 i e5 pun2 sou2-chai7, bo5 lang5 kiu3 li2.

[48]	Nga2-kok e5 ke, eng7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 mia5 lai5 chheng-hou--e5, tui3 Iu5-tai7 e5 chui2-goan5 chhut--lai5-e5, lin2 tioh8 thiaN ah; lin2 ki2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 lai5 chiu3-choa7, chheng-hou I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, chong2-si7 bo5 eng7 seng5-sit8, bo5 eng7 kong-gi7.  2). In-ui7 in ka-ki7 chheng-choe3 seng3-siaN5 e5 peh-siN3, oa2-kho3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3; mia5 choe3 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  3). I2-cheng5 e5 su7, Goa2 tui3 kou2-cha2 kong2-beng5; i2-keng chhut Goa2 e5 chhui3, iah8 si7 Goa2 sou2 chi2-si7--e5; Goa2 hut-jian5-kan choe3, tai7-chi3 chiu7 chiaN5.  4). In-ui7 Goa2 peng5-sou3 chai li2 si7 ngi7-sim--e5, li2 e5 am7-kun2 si7 thih--e5, li2 e5 thau5-hiah8 si7 tang5--e5.  5). Sou2-i2 Goa2 tui3 kou2-cha2 ka7 li2 kong2-beng5; ti7 iau2-be7 chiaN5 e5 tai7-seng chi2-si7 li2; bian2-tit li2 kong2, Chiah e5 su7 si7 goa2 e5 ngou2-siong7 sou2-kiaN5--e5, si7 goa2 tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7, kap goa2 chu3-cho7 e5 ngou2-siong7, sou2 beng7-leng7--e5.  6). Li2 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3; taN tioh8 long2-chong2 khoaN3 i; lin2 kiam2-m7-tioh8 po3-iong5 mah? tui3 taN i2-au7, Goa2 chiong sin e5 su7, chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 be7-chai un2-bat8 e5 su7, chi2-si7 li2.  7). Chiah e5 su7 si7 hian7-kim chhong3-cho7--e5, m7-si7 tui3 cha2 chiu7 u7; ti7 kin-a2-jit8 i2-cheng5, li2 iah8 be7-bat thiaN-kiN3, bian2-tit li2 kong2, Chiah e5 su7 goa2 i2-keng chai lah.  8). Li2 sit8-chai7 be7-bat thiaN-kiN3, li2 sit8-chai7 m7-chai; li2 e5 hi7-khang tui3 khi2-thau5 sit8-chai7 bo5 khui; Goa2 pun2 chai li2 kiaN5 tai7-chi3 kek8-ki5 khui2-cha3, li2 tui3 chhut-thai i2-lai5, chiu7 chheng-choe3 poe7-gek8--e5.  9). Goa2 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 mia5 ian5-chhian5 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3; ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 mia5-siaN khoan-iong5 li2, bo5 ka7 li2 chian2-tu5.  10). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 thoan3-lian7 li2 iah8 m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 gun5; li2 ti7 khou2-lan7 e5 he2-lou5-tiong Goa2 keng2 li2.  11). Goa2 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 ian5-kou3, ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 ian5-kou3, beh chiaN5 chit e5 tai7-chi3; Goa2 kiam2 thang hou7 Goa2 e5 mia5 siu7 leng5-jiok8? Goa2 bo5 beh chiong Goa2 e5 eng5-kng kui hou7 pat8-e5.
	12). Nga2-kok, Goa2 sou2 tiau3 e5 I2-sek-liat8 ah, tioh8 thiaN Goa2; Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; Goa2 si7 khi2-thau5--e5, iah8 si7 lou7-be2--e5.  13). Goa2 e5 chhiu2 kian3-lip8 toe7 e5 toe7-ki, Goa2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 tian2-khui chiah e5 thiN; Goa2 chit8-e7 kio3, chiu7 long2 khi2-lai5 khia7.  14). Lin2 long2 tioh8 chu7-chip8 lai5 thiaN; in tiong-kan chi7-chui7 bat kong2 chiah e5 su7? Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2-thiaN3--e5 beh ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 kiaN5 I sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5, I e5 chhiu2 beh kau3 ti7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5.  15). Tok8-tok8 Goa2, Goa2 i2-keng kong2, Goa2 iah8 keng2-tiau3 i, chhoa7 i lai5, i e5 lou7 beh heng-thong.  16). Lin2 tioh8 chiu7-kun7 Goa2 lai5 thiaN che; Goa2 tui3 khi2-thau5 be7-bat ti7 un2-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 kong2; tui3 u7 chit e5 su7, Goa2 chiu7 ti7-hia; taN Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe goa2 kap I e5 sin5 lai5.  17).
