Kiu3-siok8 li2 e5 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 an2-ni kong2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3; Goa2 ka3-si7 li2, hou7 li2 tit-tioh8 li7-ek, chhoa7 li2 ti7 eng-kai kiaN5 e5 lou7.  18). Hai7--ah, li2 be7 bat thiaN Goa2 e5 beng7-leng7; na7 thiaN, chiu7 li2 e5 peng5-an chhin-chhiuN7 ho5-chui2, li2 e5 kong-gi7 chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-eng2;  19). li2 e5 hou7-e3 choe7 chhin-chhiuN7 soa, li2 e5 pak-tou2-lai7 sou2-siN--e5 iah8 choe7, chhin-chhiuN7 soa-liap8; i e5 mia5 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tek-khak bo5 chian2-tu5, iah8 bo5 biat8-choat8.  20). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5 chhut-lai5, tui3 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 tiong-kan chau2-chhut; eng7 hoaN-hi2 toa7-siaN thoan5-po3 hou7 lang5 thiaN, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu3-siok8 I e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok; lin2 tioh8 chiong chit-e5 po3-iong5 kau3 toe7-kek8.  21). I in2-chhoa7 in keng-ke3 soa-bou5, in iah8 bo5 chhui3-ta; I ui7-tioh8 in hou7 chui2 tui3 chioh8-poaN5 lau5-chhut; chioh8-poaN5 lih8-khui, chui2 chiu7 chheng3-chhut.  Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, PhaiN2-lang5 tek-khak boe7 peng5-an.

[49]	Chiah e5 hai2-su7 ah, tioh8 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7; chiah e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 liu5-sim tui3 hng7-hng7 lai5 thiaN.  Tui3 goa2 ti7-thai--nih, Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 keng2-tiau3 goa2; tui3 goa2 ti7 lau7-bu2 e5 pak-tou2 I chiu7 kio3 goa2 e5 mia5.  2). I hou7 goa2 e5 chhui3 chhin-chhiuN7 lai7-to, chiong goa2 khng3 ti7 I e5 chhiu2 e5 ti3-im3-e7; koh hou7 goa2 chiaN5-choe3 boa5-kng e5 chiN3, chiong goa2 khng3 ti7 I e5 chiN3-te7.  3). Tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 si7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 I2-sek-liat8, Goa2 beh in-ui7 li2 tit-tioh8 eng5-kng.  4). Goa2 chiu7 kong2, Goa2 tioh8-boa5 si7 khang-khang, goa2 chin7-lat8 si7 bo5 li7-ek ia7 bo5 chhai2-kang; na7-si7 goa2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 chai7-ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goa2 e5 po3-siuN2 chai7-ti7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 thai--nih cho7-chiu7 goa2 choe3 I e5 lou5-pok8, beh hou7 Nga2-kok kui-ng3 I, hou7 I2-sek-liat8 chu7-chip8 ti7 I hia; (in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3 goa2 choe3 chun-kui3, goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ia7 chiaN5-choe3 goa2 e5 khui3-lat8;)  6). I u7 kong2, Li2 choe3 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 chin2-heng Nga2-kok e5 chi-phai3, hou7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong tit-tioh8 po2-choan5-e5 to3-tng2--lai5, che iau2 si7 sio2-khoa2 su7; Goa2 beh siat-lip8 li2 choe3 liat8-pang e5 kng, choe3 Goa2 e5 chin2-kiu3--e5, kau3 ti7 toe7-kek8.
	7). Kiu3-siok8 I2-sek-liat8 e5 seng3-chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, tui3 hit e5 hou7 lang5 sou2 khoaN3-khin, peh-siN3 sou2 iam3-ouN3, koaN-tiuN2 sou2 ap-che3 e5, an2-ni kong2, Kun-ong5 beh khoaN3-kiN3 li2, chiu7 khi2-lai5 khia7, siu2-leng2 ia7 beh kui7-pai3; che long2 si7 ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 chin-sit8 e5, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 u7 keng2 li2.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Ti7 tit-tioh8 chiap-lap8 e5 si5 Goa2 u7 thiaN li2, ti7 chin2-kiu3 e5 jit8 Goa2 u7 pang-chan7 li2; Goa2 beh po2-hou7 li2, hou7 li2 choe3 peh-siN3 e5 iok e5 tiong-po2, koh heng-khi2 thou2-toe7, hou7 lang5 seng5-chiap pha-hng e5 toe7 choe3 giap8;  9). ia7 tui3 siu7 khun2-pak8 e5 lang5 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 chhut--lai5; tui3 hiah e5 tiam3 ti7 ou-am3 e5 lang5 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 hian2-hian7.  In beh ti7 lou7--nih tit-tioh8 chiah8, ti7 it-chhe3 bo5 chhau2 e5 soaN tit-tioh8 niu5-chhau2.  10). In bo5 iau bo5 chhui3-ta; jiat8-khi3 kap iam7-jit8 bo5 beh siong-hai7 in; in-ui7 lin5-bin2 in--e5 beh chhoa7 in, khan in kau3 chui2-choaN5-piN.  11). Goa2 beh hou7 Goa2 e5 cheng3 soaN chiaN5-choe3 lou7, Goa2 e5 toa7-lou7 ia7 beh thun7-koaiN5.  12). KhoaN3 ah, chiah e5 lang5 beh tui3 hng7-hng7 lai5; khoaN3 ah, chiah e5 lang5 beh tui3 pak-hng sai-hng lai5; ia7 chiah e5 lang5 beh tui3 Chin5-kok lai5.  13). Chiah e5 thiN ah, eng-kai chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN; toe7 ah, eng-kai khoai3-lok8; cheng3-soaN eng-kai chhut-siaN chhiuN3-koa; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 an-ui3 I e5 peh-siN3, ia7 beh lin5-bin2 I hiah e5 khun3-khou2--e5.
	14). Sek-an kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 khi3-sak goa2, Chu2 i2-keng boe7-ki3-tit goa2.  15). Hu7-jin5-lang5 kiam2 oe7 boe7-ki3-tit i chiah8-lin e5 eN-a2, bo5 lin5-bin2 i sou2 siN e5 kiaN2? in kiam2-chhai2 u7 boe7-ki3-tit-e5, chong2-si7 Goa2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit li2.  16). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 chiong li2 khek ti7 Goa2 e5 chhiu2-chiuN2, li2 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5 siong5-siong5 ti7 Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5.  17). Li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 beh kin2-kin2 to3--lai5; hui2-hoai7 li2-e5 kap hou7 li2 pha-hng e5, beh li7-khui li2 chhut--khi3.  18). Li2 tioh8 kiah8-bak8 si3-koe3 khoaN3; in cheng3-lang5 long2 chu7-chip8 lai5 kui-oa2 li2.  Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 oah8-mia7 lai5 kong2, Li2 beh eng7 in it-chhe3 choe3 chng-thaN7 lai5 chheng7 i, koh eng7 in choe3 toa3 lai5 ha5-io, chhin-chhiuN7 sin-niu5 chit8-poaN-iuN7.  19). Lun7-kau3 li2 pha-hng leng2-cheng7 e5 sou2-chai7 kap li2 siu7 hui2-hoai7 e5 toe7, taN peh-siN3 choe7, khia7-khi2 siuN oeh8; thun-biat8 li2-e5 beh li7-khui li2 hng7-hng7.  20). Li2 sit-loh8 kiaN2 i2-au7 sou2 siN hiah e5 kiaN2 beh tui3 li2 kong2, Chit e5 sou2-chai7 goa2 khia7-khi2 siuN oeh8; kiu5 li2 hou7 goa2 u7 sou2-chai7 thang khia7-khi2.  21). Hit-si5 li2 sim-lai5 beh kong2, Goa2 i2-keng sit-loh8 kiaN2, ka-ki7 khia7-khi2, si7 siu7-liah8 e5, phiau-liu5 ti7 goa7-bin7, chi7-chui7 ka7 goa2 siN chiah-e5? chi7-chui7 chiong chiah-e5 iuN2-chhi7 kau3 toa7-han3? KhoaN3 ah, goa2 kou-toaN e5 si5, chiah-e5 ti7 toh-loh8?
	22). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh ng3 liat8-kok kiah8-chhiu2, ng3 ban7 peh-siN3 khia7 toa7-ki5; in beh chiong li2 e5 cheng3-kiaN2 pho7--lai5, chiong li2 e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 iang7--lai5.  23). Liat8-ong5 beh choe3 li2 e5 iuN2-pe7, ong5-hou7 beh choe3 li2 e5 lin-bu2; in beh chiong bin7 aN3-loh8 toe7, ng3 li2 kui7-pai3, koh chi7 li2 e5 kha e5 thou5-hun2; li2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; hoan7-na7 ng3-bang7 Goa2-e5 tek-khak bo5 kian3-siau3.  24). Beng2-lang5 chhiuN2--khi3 e5, kiam2 oe7 chhiuN2 to3-tng2? kiong5 e5 lang5 sou2 chhiuN2-liah8-e5, kiam2 oe7 kiu3 i mah?  25). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Beng2-lang5 sou2 chhiuN2-liah8--e5 beh chhiuN2 to3-tng2, kiong5 e5 lang5 sou2 chhiuN2--e5 beh tit-tioh8 kiu3; kap li2 saN-chiN--e5 Goa2 beh kap i saN-chiN, Goa2 ia7 beh kiu3 li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5.  26). Koh Goa2 beh hou7 hiah e5 ap-che3 li2-e5 chiah8 ka-ki7 e5 bah; in iah8 beh lim ka-ki7 e5 huih kau3-chui3, chhin-chhiuN7 lim tiN-chiu2 chit8-iuN7; kiN3-na7 u7 hiat-khi3 e5, beh long2 chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 li2 e5 kiu3-chu2, si7 kiu3-siok8 li2 e5 Chu2, si7 Nga2-kok e5 toa7 koan5-leng5--e5.

[50]	Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 li5-chhut lin2 e5 lau7-bu2, li5-su ti7 toh-loh8 ah? Goa2 chiong lin2 boe7 hou7 Goa2 toh-loh8 chit8 e5 che3-chu2 ah? KhoaN3 ah, lin2 siu7-boe7 si7 in-ui7 lin2 e5 choe7-koa3, lin2 e5 lau7-bu2 siu7 li5-chhut, si7 in-ui7 lin2 e5 ke3-sit.  2). Goa2 lai5 e5 si5, bo5 lang5 ti7-teh si7 chaiN2-iuN7? Goa2 kio3 e5 si5, bo5 lang5 in3 si7 chaiN2-iuN7? Goa2 e5 chhiu2 kiam2-si7 te2, boe7-oe7 kiu3-siok8 mah? Goa2 kiam2 bo5 chin2-kiu3 e5 lat8 mah? KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 chit8-e7 hoah, hai2 chiu7 ta--khi3; Goa2 hou7 kang-ho5 piN3-choe3 soa-bou5, ki5-tiong e5 hi5, in-ui7 bo5 chui2, chhau3-noa7, chhui3-ta chiu7 si2.  3). Goa2 hou7 chiah e5 thiN eng7 ou-am3 choe3 i-hok8, eng7 moa5-pou3 choe3 jia-kham3.
	4). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa siuN2-su3 goa2 siu7 ka3-si7--e5 e5 chih8, hou7 goa2 chai chaiN2-iuN7 eng7 gian5-gu2 hu5-chou7 ia3-sian7 e5 lang5; Chu2 tak8 cha2-khi2 kio3-chhiN2, kio3-chhiN2 goa2 e5 hi7-khang, hou7 goa2 oe7 thiaN, chhin-chhiuN7 siu7 ka3-si7 e5 lang5 chit8-iuN7.  5). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa khai-thong goa2 e5 hi7-khang, goa2 peng7-bo5 ui5-keh8, iah8 bo5 the3-au7.  6). Lang5 phah goa2 e5 ka-chiah-phiaN, goa2 chhut-chai7 i phah; lang5 chhoah goa2 chhui3-phoe2 e5 chhui3-chhiu, goa2 chhut-chai7 i chhoah; lang5 leng5-jiok8 goa2, ka7 goa2 phui3-noa7, goa2 iah8 bo5 ng-bin7.  7). In-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak pang-chan7 goa2, sou2-i2 goa2 bo5 kian3-siau3; ui7-tioh8 an2-ni, goa2 hou7 goa2 e5 bin7 ngi7 chhin-chhiuN7 teng7-chioh8; goa2 iah8 chai goa2 tek-khak bo5 ti3-kau3 lau3-khui3.  8). Chheng goa2 choe3 gi7--e5 kun7--lah; chi7-chui7 kap goa2 saN-chiN? i thang kap goa2 saN-kap khia7; chi7-chui7 choe3 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8? i thang chiu7-kun7 goa2.  9). KhoaN3 ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh pang-chan7 goa2, chi7-chui7 oe7 teng7 goa2 u7-choe7 ah? khoaN3 ah, in long2 chhin-chhiuN7 saN chiam7-chiam7 ku7, hou7 chiu3-thang5 sou2 chiah8.
	10). Lin2 tiong-kan chi7-chui7 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, thiaN-than3 I e5 lou5-pok8 e5 oe7 ah? kiaN5 ti7 ou-am3 bo5-u7 kng-beng5--e5, tioh8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, oa2-kho3 i e5 Siong7-te3.  11). KhoaN3 ah, hoan7-na7 lin2 tiam2-he2, eng7 he2-pe2 ui5 ka-ki7--e5, thang lai5 kiaN5 ti7 lin2 e5 he2-iam7 lai7, kap lin2 sou2 tiam2 e5 he2-pe2 tiong.  Che si7 Goa2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 ; lin2 beh to2 ti7 kan-khou2 e5 tiong-kan.

[51]	Lin2 chiah e5 tui-jip kong-gi7, chhe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5, tioh8 thiaN goa2; lin2 tioh8 siuN7-khoaN3 lin2 tui3 hia phah--chhut-lai5 e5 chioh8-poaN5, tui3 hia kut8--chhut-lai5 e5 thou5-khang.  2). Tioh8 siuN7-khoaN3 lin2 e5 chou2-kong A-pek-lah8-han2, kap siN lin2 e5 Sat-lah8, in-ui7 i kou-toaN chit8-lang5 e5 si5, Goa2 keng2-tiau3 i, su3-hok i, hou7 i ke-thiN choe7-choe7.  3). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng an-ui3 Sek-an, iah8 an-ui3 i it-chhe3 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7; hou7 i e5 khong3-ia2 chhin-chhiuN7 Ai-tian5, hou7 soa-bou5 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hng5; ti7 in tiong-kan beh u7 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, kam2-sia7 kap chhiuN3-koa e5 siaN.
	4). Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 chu3-i3 thiaN Goa2; Goa2 e5 kok-bin5 ah, tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN Goa2; in-ui7 hoat-lut8 beh tui3 Goa2 chhut, Goa2 beh lip8 Goa2 e5 kong-li2, lai5 choe3 liat8-pang e5 kng.  5). Goa2 e5 kong-gi7 kun7--lah, Goa2 e5 kiu3-un hoat-chhut; Goa2 e5 chhiu2 beh phoaN3-toan3 liat8-pang; hai2-su7 long2 beh theng3-hau7 Goa2, koh beh oa2-kho3 Goa2 e5 chhiu2.  6). Lin2 tioh8 kiah8-bak8 ng3 thiN, aN3-thau5 khoaN3 toe7; in-ui7 chiah e5 thiN beh chhin-chhiuN7 ian-hun5 siau-soaN3, toe7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 saN chiam7-chiam7 ku7, i e5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 iah8 beh chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni si2-bo5; chi2-u7 Goa2 e5 kiu3-un eng2-oan2 ti7-teh, Goa2 e5 kong-gi7 iah8 bo5 hoe3-bo5.  7). Chai-bat kong-gi7, chun5 Goa2 e5 ka3-si7 ti7 sim-lai7 e5 peh-siN3, tioh8 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7; boh8-tit kiaN lang5 e5 ki-chhi3, iah8 boh8-tit in-ui7 lang5 e5 hui2-pong3 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5.  8). In-ui7 chiu3-thang5 beh chiah8 in, chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8 i-chiuN5; chian2-thang5 beh chiah8 in, chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8 iuN5-mng5; chi2-u7 Goa2 e5 kong-gi7 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh, Goa2 e5 kiu3-un tit8-kau3 ban7-tai7.
	9). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 ah, khi2-lai5, khi2-lai5, si-chhut toa7 khui3-lat8; khi2-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-si5 e5 ni5-jit8, kou2-cha2 e5 se3-tai7 chit8-iuN7.  Chiong5-chian5 phah-chhui3 Lah8-hap-pek, chhak8-thau3 leng5--e5, kiam2-m7-si7 li2 mah?  10). Hou7 hai2 kap chhim-ian e5 chui2 ta--khi3, hou7 hai2 chhim e5 sou2-chai7 piN3 choe3 lou7, hou7 siu7-siok8 e5 peh-siN3 keng-ke3--e5, kiam2-m7-si7 li2 mah?  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu3-siok8 e5 peh-siN3 beh to3-tng2-lai5, beh chhiuN3-koa lai5 kau3 Sek-an, tit-tioh8 eng2-oan2 e5 hoaN-hi2 choe3 bian2-liu5; in beh hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, iu-bun7 thou2-khui3 long2 beh chau2--khi3.
	12). Goa2, Goa2 si7 an-ui3 lin2 e5; li2 si7 sim2-mih8 lang5, keng2-jian5 kiaN hit-e5 beh-si2 e5 lang5, kiaN hit-e5 beh piN3-choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2 e5 se3-kan lang5?  13). Iah8 boe7-ki3-tit thi2-khui chiah e5 thiN, an-tiaN7 toe7 e5 toe7-ki, chhong3-cho7 li2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, thong-jit8 in-ui7 po7-giok8-e5 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5, chiau3 i tou5-bou5 beh hui2-biat8 e5 cheng5-heng5? ki5-sit8 hit-e5 po7-giok8-e5 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 ti7 toh-loh8 ah?  14). Siu7 ap-pek-e5 beh kin2-kin2 tit-tioh8 thau2-pang3; tek-khak bo5 si2 lai5 loh8 hiat8, i e5 bi2-niu5 iah8 bo5 choat8.  15). Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, io5-tang7 toa7-hai2, hou7 i e5 eng2 hoa7-hoa7-hau2; ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 I e5 mia5.  16). Goa2 chiong Goa2 e5 oe7 he7 ti7 li2 e5 chhui3, eng7 Goa2 e5 chhiu2 e5 iaN2 jia-kham3 li2, ui7-tioh8 beh khai-thian pit8-toe7, koh tui3 Sek-an kong2, Li2 si7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3.
	17). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, khi2-lai5, khi2-lai5, khia7-teh, li2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2-tiong lim I toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 poe; lim hit-e5 hou7 lang5 tian-tian to2-to2 e5 poe-choaN2, lim kau3 ta-ta,  18). I sou2-siN chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 tiong-kan, bo5 chit8-e5 in2-chhoa7 i; i sou2 iuN2-chhi7 toa7-han3 chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 tiong-kan, bo5 chit8-e5 khan i e5 chhiu2.  19). Chi2 nng7-hang7 lim5-kau3 li2; chi7-chui7 oe7 thoe3 li2 ai-siong ah? chiu7-si7 u7 soe-pai7 kap biat8-bo5, ki-hng kap kiam3; Goa2 beh chaiN2-iuN7 an-ui3 li2?  20). Li2 chiah e5 kiaN2 hun7--khi3, to2 ti7 tak8 e5 koe-lou7-khau2, chhin-chhiuN7 lok8 ti7 lo5-bang7 e5 tiong-kan; siu7 Ia5-ho5-hoa moa2-moa2 e5 siu7-khi3, li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 chek-pi7.
	21). Sou2-i2 li2 chit e5 khun3-khou2 koh chui3-e5, khiok m7-si7 in-ui7 chiu2 lai5 chui3, li2 tioh8 thiaN.  22). Li2 e5 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 ui7-tioh8 I e5 peh-siN3 sin-oan e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 i2-keng chiong hit-e5 hou7 lang5 tian-tian to2-to2 e5 poe, chiu7-si7 Goa2 toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 poe-choaN2, tui3 li2 e5 chhiu2 theh8--chhut-lai5, li2 tek-khak m7-bian2 koh lim.  23). Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 poe he7 ti7 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 li2 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2-tiong; in bat tui3 li2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 aN3--loh8-khi3, chhut-chai7 goan2 tah8-ke3--khi3; li2 chiu7 eng7 ka-chiah-phiaN choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 toe7, chhin-chhiuN7 koe-lou7, chhut-chai7 lang5 keng-ke3.

[52]	Sek-an ah, khi2-lai5, khi2-lai5, chheng7 li2 e5 toa7 khui3-lat8; seng3-siaN5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, chheng7 li2 sui2 e5 i-hok8; in-ui7 tui3-taN i2-au7, bo5 siu7 kat-le2, bo5 chheng-khi3-e5, tek-khak bo5 koh jip8 li2 e5 tiong-kan.  2). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, tioh8 poaN7--khi3 tin5-ai; khi2-lai5 che7; Sek-an siu7-liah8 e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 thau2-khui li2 am7-kun2 e5 so2-lian7.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 siu7-boe7 bo5 theh8 lang5 chiN5, tit-tioh8 siok8-hoe5 iah8 bo5 eng7 gun5.  4). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Khi2-thau5 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8, ti7-hia kia3-kha; koh u7 A-sut8 lang5 bo5 ian5-kou3 ap-che3 in.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ki3-jian5 bo5 in-toaN hou7 lang5 liah8--khi3, taN Goa2 ti7-chia choe3 sim2-mih8 ah? Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Koan2-hat in e5 lang5 hoa7-hoa7-hau2 teh kio3, Goa2 e5 mia5 thong-jit8 siu7 siat-tok8.  6). Sou2-i2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 beh chai Goa2 e5 mia5; kau3 hit-jit8 in beh chai teh-kong2-e5 chiu7-si7 Goa2; khoaN3 ah, si7 Goa2.
	7). Po3 ho2 siau-sit, thoan5 ho5-peng5, po3 hok-khi3 e5 ho2 siau-sit, thoan5 kiu3-un-e5, tui3 Sek-an kong2, Li2 e5 Siong7-te3 choe3-ong5 lah, chit-lang5 e5 kha chiuN7 soaN-teng2, kau3 chiah sui2!  8). ThiaN ah, li2 siu2-bang7 e5 lang5 e5 siaN! in chhut toa7-siaN, saN-kap chhiuN3-koa; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa to3--lai5 Sek-an e5 si5, in beh tng-thau5 tui3-bin7 khoaN3-kiN3.  9). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7 ah, tioh8 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, saN-kap chhiuN3-koa; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an-ui3 I e5 peh-siN3, kiu3-siok8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 ban7-kok e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 lut8 I e5 seng3-chhiu2; toe7-kek8 e5 lang5 long2 khoaN3-kiN3 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 chin2-kiu3.
	11). Lin2 tioh8 li7-khui i, li7-khui i, tui3-hia chhut-lai5, boh8-tit bong bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 mih8; tui3 in tiong-kan chhut-lai5; lin2 kng Ia5-ho5-hoa khi3-ku7 e5 lang5 ah, tioh8 ka-ki7 chheng-khi3.  12). Lin2 chhut-lai5 m7-bian2 tioh8-kip, ia7 m7-bian2 to5-chau2; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak ti7 lin2 e5 thau5-cheng5 kiaN5, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 tek-khak choe3 lin2 au7-bin7 e5 po2-hou7.
	13). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 beh eng7 ti3-hui7 kiaN5 tai7-chi3, beh siu7 ku2-khi2 seng-koaiN5, koh beh chiaN5-choe3 chin koaiN5.  14). Choe7-choe7 lang5 ui7 li2 gong5-ngiah8, ( i e5 bin7-mau7 pi2 pat8-lang5 khah u7 sun2-siong, i e5 heng5-chong7 pi2 se3-kan lang5 khah u7 sun2-hai7;)  15). chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni i ia7 beh kek-tong7 choe7-choe7 kok e5 peh-siN3; liat8-ong5 beh tui3 i lai5 ng in e5 chhui3; in-ui7 sou2 be7-bat tui3 in kong2--e5, in beh khoaN3-kiN3; be7-bat thiaN-kiN3--e5, in beh beng5-pek8.

[53]	Lan2 sou2 thiaN-kiN3-e5, u7 chi7-chui7 sin3 ah? Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 ng3 chi7-chui7 hian2-beng5 ah?  2). In-ui7 i ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 seng-tiong2 chhin-chhiuN7 chiN2-chiN2 e5 iN2, iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 kun hoat ti7 ta-toe7; i bo5 ho2 heng5-chong7 bo5 ui-gi5; lan2 khoaN3-kiN3 i iah8 bo5 ho2 heng5-iong5, thang hou7 lan2 him-bou7 i.  3). I siu7 khoaN3-khin, hou7 lang5 pang3-sak, siu7 choe7-choe7 khou2-thang3, siong5-siong5 tu2-tioh8 iu-bun7; i siu7 khoaN3-khin, chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 lang5 ng-bin7 m7-khoaN3-e5 chit8-iuN7; lan2 iah8 bo5 chun-tiong7 i.
	4). I sit8-chai7 tam-tng lan2 e5 iu-bun7, pe7 lan2 e5 khou2-thang3; chong2-si7 lan2 liah8-choe3 i siu7 chek-hoat8, hou7 Siong7-te3 phah, koh siu7 khou2-chhou2.  5). Na7-si7 i ui7-tioh8 lan2 e5 ke3-sit siu7 siong, ui7-tioh8 lan2 e5 choe7-koa3 siu7-hai7; i tam-tng heng5-hoat8, lan2 tit-tioh8 peng5-an; i siu7 piN-phah, lan2 tit-tioh8 i-ho2.  6). Lan2 long2 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5 be5-lou7; tak8-lang5 kiaN5 ka-ki7 e5 phian-lou7; Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 lan2 cheng3-lang5 e5 choe7 long2 kui ti7 i sin-chiuN7.
	7). I siu7 ap-pek tu2-tioh8 kan-khou2, iau2-ku2 bo5 khui-chhui3; i chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-a2 khan kau3 siu7-thai5 e5 toe7; koh chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5 ti7 chian2-mng5 e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 bo5 chhut-siaN, i iah8 an2-ni bo5 khui-chhui3.  8). I tui3 ap-pek kap sim2-phoaN3 siu7 chhu2--khi3; ti7 i e5 se3-tai7, chi7-chui7 siuN7-tioh8 i tui3 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7 siu7 chian2-tu5? a2-si7 in-ui7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 choe7-koa3 siu7-phah ah?  9). I sui-jian5 bo5 kiaN5 kiong5-po7, chhui3 ia7 bo5 u7 khui2-cha3, iau2-ku2 ti7 i e5 si2 kap phaiN2-lang5 tang5-bong7, ia7 kap pu3-lang5 saN-kap.
	10). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoaN-hi2 sun2-hai7 i, hou7 i siu7 khou2-thang3; i e5 oah8-mia7 choe3 siok8-choe7 e5 che3, hit-si5 i beh khoaN3-kiN3 hou7-e3, koh ke-thiN he3-siu7, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 su7 beh ti7 i e5 chhiu2-tiong heng-thong.  11). I beh khoaN3-kiN3 pun2-sin lo5-khou2 e5 hau7-ko2, chiu7 sim-moa2 i3-chiok; Goa2 gi7 e5 lou5-pok8 beh eng7 i e5 chai-bat hou7 choe7-choe7 lang5 tit-tioh8 chheng-choe3-gi7; ia7 i beh tam-tng in e5 choe7-koa3.  12). Sou2-i2 Goa2 beh hou7 i kap che7 koaiN5-ui7--e5 pun hun7-giah8, kap kiong5-beng2--e5 pun sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8; in-ui7 i pang3-sak siN3-mia7 kau3-si2, i ia7 liat8 ti7 choe7-hoan7 e5 tiong-kan; chong2-si7 i tam-tng choe7-choe7 lang5 e5 choe7, koh thoe3 choe7-hoan7 ki5-to2.

[54]	Li2 bo5 hoai5-in7 bo5 siN-kiaN2 e5, tioh8 chhiuN3-koa; li2 be7-bat keng-ke3 siN-kiaN2 kan-khou2 e5, tioh8 chhut-siaN chhiuN3-koa, chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN; in-ui7 ka-ki7 tiam3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 pi2 u7 tiong7-hu--e5, siN-kiaN2 khah-choe7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.  2). Tioh8 khui-khoah li2 pou3-piN5 e5 toe7, pang3-toa7 li2 khia7-khi2 e5 tiuN3-pak; m7-thang han7-tiaN7; tioh8 khan-tng5 li2 e5 soh, kian-kou3 li2 e5 khit8-a2.  3). In-ui7 li2 beh ng3-cho2 ng3-iu7 lai5 khui-khoah; li2 e5 hou7-e3 tek-khak tit-tioh8 liat8-kok choe3-giap8; koh hou7 pha-hng e5 siaN5 u7 lang5 khia7-khi2.  4). Boh8-tit kiaN-hiaN5; in-ui7 li2 tek-khak bo5 ti3-kau3 kian3-siau3; iah8 boh8-tit ui3 siau2-jin5; in-ui7 li2 bo5 ti3-kau3 siu7 leng5-jiok8; li2 tek-khak boe7 ki3-tit siau3-lian5 e5 si5 e5 kian3-siau3; bo5 koh ki3-liam7 li2 chiu2-koaN2 e5 si5 e5 leng5-jiok8.  5). In-ui7 chhong3-cho7 li2-e5 si7 li2 e5 tiong7-hu; ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 I e5 mia5; kiu3-siok8 li2-e5, si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5; I tek-khak chheng-choe3 choan5-toe7 e5 Siong7-te3.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa tiau3--li2, chhin-chhiuN7 tiau3 siu7 khi3-sak sim-lai7 iu-siong e5 bou2, chiu7-si7 siau3-lian5 e5 si5 sou2 chhoa7, siu7 khi3-sak e5 bou2; che si7 li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 kong2 e5.  7). Goa2 pang3-li7 li2 put-ko3 tiap-a2-ku2, chong2-si7 beh eng7 toa7 chu5-pi siu li2 to3-tng2.  8). Goa2 hoat-chhut siu7-khi3, chiam7-si5 tui3 li2 ng-bin7; chong2-si7 beh eng7 eng2-oan2 e5 chu5-ai3 lin5-bin2 li2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kiu3-siok8 li2 e5 Chu2, kong2 e5.  9). In-ui7 che chai7 Goa2 khoaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 Na2-a e5 toa7-chui2; Goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 chiu3-choa7 bo5 koh hou7 Na2-a e5 toa7-chui2 hoan3-lam7 pian3-toe7, Goa2 iah8 chiau3 an2-ni chiu3-choa7, bo5 koh siu7-khi3 li2, chek-pi7 li2.  10). Toa7-soaN oe7 soa2-khui, sio2-soaN oe7 i5-soa2, tok8-tok8 Goa2 e5 chu5-ai3 tek-khak bo5 li7-khui li2, Goa2 peng5-an e5 iok iah8 bo5 i5-soa2; che si7 lin5-bin2 li2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.
	11). Li2 chit-e5 siu7 khun3-khou2, hou7 toa7-hong io5-tang7 boe7 tit-tioh8 an-ui3 e5 lang5--ah, Goa2 beh eng7 chhai2-sek an-ti3 li2 e5 chioh8-thau5, eng7 lam5-sek e5 po2-chioh8 he7 li2 e5 toe7-ki.  12). Koh eng7 ang5-po2-chioh8 cho7 li2 e5 siaN5-to2-chi2, eng7 ang5-gek8 cho7 li2 e5 siaN5-mng5, eng7 po2-chioh8 cho7 li2 si3-ui5 e5 pian-kai3.  13). Li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 long2 beh hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ka3-si7; li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 beh tit-tioh8 toa7 peng5-an.  14). Li2 beh in-ui7 kong-gi7 tit-tioh8 khia7-chai7, beh li7-khui che3-ap hng7-hng7, bo5 ti3-kau3 kiaN-hiaN5; li2 beh li7-khui chai-e7 hng7-hng7, in-ui7 i tek-khak bo5 kun7-oa2 li2.  15). Chiu7 kiam2-chhai2 u7 lang5 chu7-chip8, chong2-si7 m7-si7 tui3 Goa2; kiN3-na7 chu7-chip8 kong-kek li2 e5, beh in-ui7 li2 lai5 poah8-to2.  16). Thih-chhiuN7 pun5 he2-thoaN3, che3-cho7 hap8-eng7 e5 khi3-hai5--e5, si7 Goa2 sou2 chhong3-cho7; Goa2 ia7 chhong3-cho7 ham7-hai7 lang5 e5, hou7 i kiaN5 chau5-biat8.  17). KiN3-na7 ui7-tioh8 kong-kek li2 lai5 cho7 e5 khi3-hai5 tek-khak bo5 chiaN5 lou7-eng7; kiN3-na7 ti7 sim2-phoaN3 e5 si5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek li2 e5 chih8, li2 beh teng7 i e5 choe7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou5-pok8 e5 san2-giap8, ia7 si7 in tui3 Goa2 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 gi7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.

[55]	Eh, kiN3-na7 lin2 chhui3-ta-e5, tioh8 lai5 chiu7-kun7 chui2, ia7 bo5 chiN5-e5, lin2 tioh8 lai5; lai5 boe2 lai5 chiah8; lai5 ah, m7-bian2 gun5, m7-bian2 ke3-chiN5, lai5 boe2 chiu2 kap lin.  2). Lin2 siaN2-su7 khai-hui3 chiN5, boe2 hit-e5 boe7 chiah8-tit e5 mih8? siaN2-su7 tioh8-boa5, ti7 hit-e5 boe7 hou7 lang5 chiah8-pa2--e5 ah? lin2 tioh8 liu5-sim thiaN Goa2, chiu7 oe7 chiah8 hit e5 ho2-mih8, tit-tioh8 hiong2-siu7 iu5-ji7, hou7 sim hoaN-hi2.  3). Lin2 tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang chiu7-kun7 Goa2; tioh8 thiaN, chiu7 lin2 e5 sim-sin5 oe7 oah8; Goa2 beh kap lin2 lip8 eng2-oan2 e5 iok, chiu7-si7 sou2 eng3-un2 Tai7-pit8 kian-kou3 e5 un-hui7.  4). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 i2-keng siat-lip8 i choe3 liat8-pang e5 kan-cheng3, choe3 liat8-pang e5 kun-ong5 kap siu2-leng2.  5). KhoaN3 ah, li2 peng5-sou3 m7-bat e5 peh-siN3, li2 beh kio3 i lai5; peng5-sou3 m7-bat li2 e5 peh-siN3 iah8 beh chau2 lai5 oa2 li2; long2 si7 ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5; in-ui7 I i2-keng eng5-kng li2.
	6). Tioh8 than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa thang chhe7-tioh8 e5 si5, lai5 chhe7 I, ti7 I saN-kun7 e5 si5 kiu5-kio3 I.  7). PhaiN2-lang5 tioh8 li7-khui i e5 lou7, put-gi7 e5 lang5 tioh8 koe2-oaN7 i e5 liam7-thau5; kui-ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I beh lin5-bin2 i; kui-ng3 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3, in-ui7 I beh pian3-kiaN5 sia3-bian2.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 e5 liam7-thau5 m7-si7 lin2 e5 liam7-thau5, lin2 e5 lou7 m7-si7 Goa2 e5 lou7.  9). In-ui7 thiN chaiN2-iuN7 khah-koaiN5 toe7, an2-ni Goa2 e5 lou7 khah-koaiN5 lin2 e5 lou7, Goa2 e5 liam7-thau5 khah-koaiN5 lin2 e5 liam7-thau5.  10). In-ui7 chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 kap seh tui3 thiN kang3-loh8, iah8 bo5 koh to3-tng2, chiu7-si7 lun7-tek8 thou2-toe7, hou7 toe7-chiuN7 puh-ge5 kiat-sit8, hou7 ia7-cheng2--e5 u7 cheng2-chi2, hou7 chiah8--e5 u7 bi2-niu5;  11). Goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2-chhut e5 oe7 iah8 beh an2-ni; koat-toan3 bo5 khang-khang to3-tng2 lai5 Goa2 chia, si7 beh chiaN5 Goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5, beh hou7 Goa2 sou2 chhe i choe3 e5 su7 tit-tioh8 heng-thong.  12). Lin2 chhut-khi3 beh hoaN-hoaN hi2-hi2, tit-tioh8 in2-chhoa7 peng5-peng5 an-an: toa7-soaN sio2-soaN beh ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut-siaN chhiuN3-koa, tian5-ia2 e5 chhiu7-bak8 long2 beh tah-chhiu2.  13). Chheng5-peh hoat-siN lai5 thoe3 chhau2-chhi3, kong-liam-chhiu7 hoat-siN lai5 thoe3 chit8-le5; che si7 beh choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 e5 ki3-liam7, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 cheng3-ku3, boe7-oe7 chian2-tu5.

[56]	Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 siu2 kong-peng5, kiaN5 kong-gi7; in-ui7 Goa2 e5 kiu3-un i2-keng kun7, Goa2 e5 kong-gi7 beh hian2-beng5.  2). Lang5 an2-ni kiaN5, se3-kan lang5 an2-ni chhi5-siu2 i, siu2 an-hioh-jit8 bo5 kan-hoan7-tioh8, kim3-chi2 ka-ki7 e5 chhiu2 bo5 choe3 phaiN2; hit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.  3). Kap Ia5-ho5-hoa lian5-hap8 e5 goa7-pang lang5 boh8-tit kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak chiong goa2 kap I e5 peh-siN3 pun-li7; thai3-kam3 iah8 boh8-tit kong2, KhoaN3 ah, goa2 si7 kou-ta5 e5 chhiu7.  4). In-ui7 lun7-kau3 kiN3-na7 siu2 Goa2 chiah e5 an-hioh-jit8, keng2 Goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 su7, kap chhi5-siu2 Goa2 e5 iok e5 thai3-kam3, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2,  5). Chiah e5 lang5, Goa2 beh hou7 in ti7 Goa2 e5 chhu3, ti7 Goa2 e5 chhiuN5-ui5-lai7, u7 ki3-ho7 u7 mia5-ji7, pi2 u7 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 khah-ho2; Goa2 beh hou7 i eng2-oan2 e5 mia5 boe7-oe7 chian2-tu5.  6). Iau2-u7 hiah-e5 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa lian5-hap8 e5 goa7-pang lang5, beh hok8-sai7 I, beh thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, beh choe3 I e5 lou5-pok8, kiN3-na7 siu2 an-hioh-jit8 bo5 kan-hoan7, koh chhi5-siu2 Goa2 e5 iok e5 lang5;  7). Goa2 beh chhoa7 in kau3 Goa2 e5 seng3-soaN, hou7 in ti7 ki5-to2 Goa2 e5 chhu3 lai5 hoaN-hi2; in e5 sio-che3 kap le2-mih8, ti7 Goa2 e5 toaN5-teng2, tek-khak tit-tioh8 chiap-lap8; in-ui7 Goa2 e5 chhu3 beh chheng-choe3 ban7 peh-siN3 ki5-to2 e5 chhu3.  8). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 chio-chip8 I2-sek-liat8 siu7 koaN2-soaN3--e5, kong2, Hiah-e5 siu7 chio-chip8 e5 lang5 i2-goa7, Goa2 iau2 beh chio-chip8 pat8-lang5 lai5 kui-oa2 i.
9). SoaN-ia2 chiah e5 siu3 long2 tioh8 lai5 thun-chiah8, chhiu7-na5-lai7 chiah e5 siu3, iah8 tioh8 an2-ni.  10). I e5 siu2-bang7--e5 si7 chhiN-mi5, long2 bo5 ti3-sek, long2 si7 e2-kau2, boe7 pui7 e5 kau2, tok8-tok8 bin5-bang7, to2-teh, ai3 khun3.  11). Chiah e5 kau2 tham-chiah8, m7-chai pa2; chiah e5 bok8-chia2 boe7-oe7 beng5-pek8, tak8-lang5 kiaN5 ka-ki7 e5 phian-lou7, tak8-e5 tui3 kok hong-bian7 kiu5 ka-ki7 e5 li7-ek.  12). In kong2, Lai5 lah, goa2 khi3 phang5-chiu2, lan2 lim kau7-chiu2 kau3-pa2; bin5-a2-jit8 beh chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8, kek8-toa7 bo5-pi2.

[57]	Gi7-lang5 si2-bo5, bo5 lang5 khoa3 ti7 sim-thau5; khian5-seng5 e5 lang5 ke3-si3, bo5 lang5 siuN7-kau3 chit e5 gi7-lang5 ke3-si3 si7 thoat-li7 chiong-lai5 e5 chai-e7.  2). KiaN5 ti7 cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5, i beh chin3-jip8 peng5-an e5 sou2-chai7, an-jian5 hioh ti7 i e5 chhng5.
	3). Lin2 chiah e5 ang-i5 e5 kiaN2, kan-hu kap ki7-lu2 e5 cheng2-lui7, long2 tioh8 chin3-cheng5 lai5.  4). Lin2 tui3 chi7-chui7 hi3-lang7, tui3 chi7-chui7 khui-chhui3 thou2-chih8 ah? lin2 kiam2 m7-si7 poe7-gek8 e5 kiaN2-ji5, peh8-chhat8 e5 cheng2-lui7 mah?  5). Lin2 ti7 siong7-chhiu7 e5 tiong-kan, ti7 tak8 chang5 chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhiu7-kha, iok8-he2 kong-sim, ti7 soaN-kok--nih, ti7 chioh8-khang-lai7 thai5 gin2-na2.  6). Ti7 soaN-kok-lai7, kng-kut8 e5 chioh8-thau5 tiong, u7 li2 e5 hun7-giah8; chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 giap8; li2 iah8 tui3 i koan3-tian7, hian3 le2-mih8; in-ui7 chiah-e5, Goa2 kiam2 oe7 an-sim mah?  7). Li2 ti7 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 soaN-teng2 an-siat bin5-chhng5, iah8 chiuN7-khi3 hian3-che3.  8). Li2 ti7 mng5-au7, mng5-khia7-au7, khia7 li2 e5 ki3-liam7; tui3 pat8-lang5 lou7-hian7 sin-the2 lai5 chiuN7-khi3; khui-khoah li2 e5 bin5-chhng5, kap in lip8-iok; li2 ti7-hia khoaN3-kiN3 in e5 bin5-chhng5, chiu7 chin i3-ai3.  9). Li2 chiong iu5 toa3 kau3 ong5 hia, koh ke-thiN li2 e5 hiuN-liau7, chhe su3-chia2 khi3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7, ka-ki7 pi-chian7, tit8-kau3 im-kan.  10). Li2 in-ui7 lou7 hng7 ia3-sian7, chong2-si7 bo5 kong2, Che si7 khang-khang; li2 u7 koh tit-tioh8 khui3-lat8, sou2-i2 m7-chai loan2-jiok8.  11). Li2 in-ui7 chi7-chui7 lai5 lun2-neh kiaN-hiaN5, ti3-kau3 kong2 peh8-chhat8, bo5 ki3-liam7 Goa2, iah8 bo5 khoa3 ti7 li2 e5 sim-thau5? Goa2 kiam2-m7-si7 tui3 kou2-cha2 cheng7-cheng7, li2 chiah bo5 kiaN Goa2 mah?  12). Goa2 beh chi2-beng5 li2 e5 kong-gi7; lun7-kau3 li2 e5 sou2-kiaN5, long2 bo5 li7-ek li2.  13). Li2 au5-kio3 e5 si5, thang hou7 li2 sou2 chu7-chip8-e5 kiu3 li2; hong beh ka7 in chhe-soaN3; khi3 beh ka7 in pun5--khi3; chong2-si7 hit-e5 oa2-kho3 Goa2--e5 beh tit-tioh8 thou2-toe7, beh seng5-siu7 Goa2 e5 seng3-soaN choe3-giap8.  14). U7 siaN kong2, Thun7-koaiN5, thun7-koaiN5, pi7-pan7 lou7, tui3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 lou7-tiong tu5-khi3 that-gai7.  15). In-ui7 hit-e5 chi3-koaiN5 chi3-chun, eng2-oan2 ti7-teh, mia5 kio3-choe3 Seng3--e5, an2-ni kong2, Goa2 khia7-khi2 ti7 chi3-koaiN5 chi3-seng3 e5 sou2-chai7, iah8 kap sim-sin5 thong3-hoe2 khiam-pi e5 lang5 saN-kap khia7-khi2, beh hou7 khiam-pi e5 lang5 e5 sim-sin5 koh-oah8, iah8 hou7 thong3-hoe2 e5 lang5 e5 sim koh-oah8.  16). Goa2 tek-khak bo5 eng2-oan2 cheng-pian7, iah8 bo5 ku2-tng5 siu7-khi3; kiaN-liau2 Goa2 sou2 chhong3-cho7 e5 lang5, in e5 sim kap leng5-hun5 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 soe-lam2.  17). In-ui7 i tham-sim e5 choe7-koa3, Goa2 chiu7 siu7-khi3 phah i, Goa2 ng-bin7 siu7-khi3; i iu5-goan5 poe7-gek8, chiau3 i e5 sim-i3 khi3 kiaN5.  18). Goa2 khoaN3 i sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7, iah8 beh i-ho2 i; koh beh chhoa7 i, hou7 i kap hiah-e5 saN-kap siong-sim e5 lang5, koh tit-tioh8 an-ui3.  19). Goa2 cho7 beh hou7 in e5 chhui3 kong2-chhut o-lo2 e5 oe7, Peng5-an, peng5-an kui hou7 hng7 kap kun7 e5 lang5; koh Goa2 beh i-ho2 i; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.  20). Tok8-tok8 phaiN2-lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 gia5-eng2 e5 hai2, boe7-oe7 peng5-cheng7; i e5 chui2 chheng3-chhut u3-oe3 kap thou5-be5.  21). Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 kong2, PhaiN2-lang5 tek-khak boe7 peng5-an.

[58]	Li2 tioh8 toa7-siaN au5-kio3, m7-thang han7-chi2, chhut toa7-siaN chhin-chhiuN7 pun5 sau3-kak, tui3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 kong2-beng5 in e5 ke3-sit, tui3 Nga2-kok e5 ke kong2-beng5 in e5 choe7-ok.  2). In jit8-jit8 chhe7 Goa2, hoaN-hi2 chai Goa2 e5 to7-lou7, chhin-chhiuN7 kiaN5-gi7 e5 peh-siN3, bo5 li7-khui in e5 Siong7-te3 e5 hoat-lut8; in kiu5 Goa2 chiau3 kong-gi7 e5 sim2-phoaN3, hoaN-hi2 chhin-kun7 Siong7-te3.  3). In kong2, Goan2 kim3-chiah8, Li2 siaN2-su7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3? goan2 khek-khou2 goan2 e5 sim, Li2 siaN2-su7 m7-chai ah? KhoaN3 ah, lin2 kim3-chiah8 e5 jit8, iau2-ku2 ka-ki7 an-lok8, kiong5-pek lang5 ka7 lin2 choe3 khou2-kang.  4). KhoaN3 ah, lin2 kim3-chiah8 si7 beh saN-chiN, saN oan-ke, eng7 hiong-ok e5 kun5-thau5-bu2 phah--lang5; lin2 kin-a2-jit8 kim3-chiah8, boe7-oe7 hou7 lin2 e5 siaN thiaN kau3 teng2-bin7.  5). Chit-khoan2 e5 kim3-chiah8, kiam2-si7 Goa2 sou2 keng2, hou7 lang5 khek-khou2 i e5 sim e5 jit8 mah? Kiam2-si7 hou7 lang5 aN3-thau5 chhin-chhiuN7 lou5-tek, eng7 moa5-pou3 kap he2-hu phou ti7 i e5 seng-khu-e7 mah? che kiam2 thang chheng choe3 kim3-chiah8 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 jit8 mah?  6). Goa2 sou2 keng2 e5 kim3-chiah8, kiam2-m7-si7 thau2-khui hiong-ok e5 soh, thau2-pang3 pe7-taN e5 soh, hou7 siu7 che3-ap-e5 tit-tioh8 chu7-iu5, kong3-chih8 it-chhe3 e5 taN mah?  7). Kiam2-m7-si7 chiong li2 e5 bi2-niu5 pun hou7 iau-go7 e5 lang5, chiong si3-koe3 liu5 e5 song3-hiong lang5 chiap-lap8 ti7 li2 e5 ke? khoaN3-kiN3 thng3-pak-theh e5 lang5 hou7 i chheng7, tui3 ka-ki7 e5 kut-jiok8 iah8 bo5 siam2-khi3 bih mah?  8). An2-ni, li2 e5 kng beh hoat-chhut chhin-chhiuN7 thiN-kng-cha2 e5 kng, li2 e5 siong beh kin2-kin2 tit-tioh8 ho2; li2 e5 kong-gi7 beh kiaN5 ti7 li2 e5 thau5-cheng5; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng beh choe3 li2 au7-bin7 e5 po2-hou7.  9). Hit-si5 li2 kiu5-kio3, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh thiaN li2; li2 khun2-kiu5, I beh kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia. Li2 na7 tui3 li2 tiong-kan tu5--khi3 tang7 e5 taN, kap ki2-toh8-lang5 e5 chng2-thau5-a2, i2-kip8 lam7-sam2 kong2 e5 oe7;  10). li2 e5 sim na7 lin5-bin2 iau-go7 e5 lang5, hou7 khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 tit-tioh8 moa2-chiok, li2 e5 kng chiu7 beh ti7 ou-am3-tiong hoat-hian7, li2 e5 ou-am3 beh piN3 chhin-chhiuN7 jit8-tiong-tau3.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa iah8 beh siong5-siong5 in2-chhoa7 li2, ti7 khong3-han7 e5 toe7, hou7 li2 sim-moa2 i3-chiok, kut-thau5 iong2-chong3; li2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 koan3-ak e5 hng5, koh chhin-chhiuN7 lau5-boe7-ta e5 chui2-choaN5.  12). Hiah-e5 tui3 li2 chhut e5 lang5, beh khi2-cho7 ku2-ku2 i2-keng hong-hoe3 e5 sou2-chai7; li2 beh kian3-lip8 lek8-tai7 hui2-hoai7 e5 toe7-ki; li2 beh chheng-choe3 Pou2 phoa3-khiah--e5, kap Koh siu-li2 lou7, hou7 lang5 khia7-khi2--e5.  13). Li2 na7 tui3 an-hioh-jit8 kim3-chi2 li2 e5 kha, ti7 Goa2 e5 seng3-jit8 bo5 choe3 ka-ki7 sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5, chheng an-hioh-jit8 choe3 thang hoaN-hi2--e5, chheng Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 seng3-jit8 choe3 thang chun-tiong7--e5; iah8 koh chun-keng3 i, bo5 pan7 ka-ki7 e5 su-su7, bo5 than3 ka-ki7 e5 su-i3, bo5 kong2 su-khia oe7;  14). li2 chiu7 beh in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 hoaN-hi2; Goa2 beh hou7 li2 chiuN7 kau3 toe7-chiuN7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7; koh eng7 li2 e5 chou2 Nga2-kok e5 san2-giap8 iuN2-chhi7 li2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhin-chhui3 kong2 e5.

[59]	KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 m7-si7 te2, boe7-oe7 chin2-kiu3; hi7-khang m7-si7 tang7, boe7-oe7 thiaN.  2). Chiu7-si7 lin2 e5 choe7-koa3 hou7 lin2 kap Siong7-te3 keh-tng7, lin2 e5 choe7-ok hou7 I tui3 lin2 ng-bin7, bo5 thiaN.  3). In-ui7 lin2 e5 chhiu2 bak--tioh8 huih, lin2 e5 chng2-thau5-a2 bak-tioh8 choe7-ok, lin2 e5 chhui3-tun5 kong2 peh8-chhat8, lin2 e5 chih8 kong2-chhut phaiN2-oe7.  4). Bo5 lang5 eng7 kong-gi7 lai5 pin2-beng5, bo5 lang5 chiau3 seng5-sit8 lai5 pian7-hou7; long2 si7 oa2-kho3 hu-ke2, kong2 peh8-chhat8; sou2 hoai5-in7--e5 si7 chan5-hai7, sou2 siN--e5 si7 sia5-phiah.  5). In pu7 tok8-choa5 e5 nng7, kiN ti-tu bang7, lang5 chiah8 i e5 nng7 tek-khak si2, chit e5 nng7 na7 tah8-phoa3 tek-khak chhut ok-choa5.  6). In sou2 kiN e5 bang7 boe7-oe7 chiaN5-choe3 i-hok8, in sou2-choe3--e5 boe7-oe7 ka-ki7 jia-kham3; in sou2-kiaN5--e5 long2 si7 choe7-ok, in e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5 long2 si7 kiong5-po7.  7). In e5 kha chau2 lai5 kiaN5-phaiN2, in kin2-kin2 beh lau5 bo5-choe7 e5 lang5 e5 huih; in e5 liam7-thau5 long2 si7 sia5-phiah e5 liam7-thau5; sou2 keng-ke3 e5 toa7-lou7, long2 si7 pha-hng hui2-biat8.  8). Peng5-an e5 lou7 in m7-chai, sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7-keng3 bo5 u7 kong-peng5; in ui7-tioh8 pun2-sin cho7 oan-khiau e5 lou7, kiN3-na7 kiaN5-i--e5, long2 boe7 hiau2-tit peng5-an.
	9). In-ui7 an2-ni, kong-peng5 li7-khui goan2 hng7-hng7, kong-gi7 tui goan2 bo5-tioh8; goan2 ng3-bang7 kng-liang7, hoan2-tng2 si7 ou-am3; ng3-bang7 kng-beng5, hoan2-tng2 kiaN5 ti7 am3-tiong.  10). Goan2 bong chhiuN5, oa2 piah, chhin-chhiuN7 chhiN-mi5 lang5; goan2 si3-koe3 bong, chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 bak8-chiu e5 lang5; goan2 jit8-tiong-tau3 tian-tian to2-to2, chhin-chhiuN7 hong5-hun e5 si5 chit8-iuN7; goan2 ti7 iong2-chong3 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan; chhin-chhiuN7 si2-lang5 chit8-iuN7.  11). Goan2 hau2 chhin-chhiuN7 him5, ai-ai-chhan chhin-chhiuN7 ka-chui; ng3-bang7 kong-peng5, chong2-si7 long2 bo5; ng3-bang7 kiu3-un, chong2-si7 li7-khui goan2 hng7-hng7.  12). Goan2 e5 ke3-sit ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ke-thiN choe7-choe7, choe7-ok choe3 kan-cheng3 ko3 goan2; choe7-koa3 kap goan2 saN-kap ti7-teh, lun7-kau3 goan2 e5 choe7-koa3, goan2 long2 chai;  13). chiu7-si7 poe7-gek8 m7-jin7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, oat-to3-tng2 m7-te3 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3, kong2-chhut che3-ap kap poe7-gek8 e5 oe7, sim siuN7 peh8-chhat8 oe7, chiu7 soa3 kong2-chhut.  14). Koh kong-peng5 choan2-tng2 the3-au7, kong-gi7 khia7 ti7 hng7-hng7; seng5-sit8 poah8-to2 ti7 koe-lou7, cheng3-tit8 iah8 boe7 chin3 jip8.  15). Seng5-sit8 chio2-chio2; li7-khui phaiN2--e5 hoan2-tng2 chiaN5-choe3 siu7-chhiuN2 e5 mih8; hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3-kiN3, in-ui7 bo5 kong-gi7, chiu7 put-chi2 bo5 hoaN-hi2.  16). I khoaN3 bo5 lang5 chin2-kiu3, bo5 lang5 thoe3-kiu5, put-chi2 gong5-ngiah8; chiu7 eng7 ka-ki7 e5 chhiu2 lai5 kiu3 ka-ki7; eng7 I e5 kong-gi7 hu5-chhi5 pun2-sin.  17). I eng7 kong-gi7 choe3 khoe-kah lai5 chheng7, eng7 chin2-kiu3 choe3 thau5-khoe lai5 ti3; eng7 po3 kiu5-siu5 choe3 i-hok8 lai5 chheng7, eng7 jiat8-sim choe3 goa7-phau3 lai5 moa.  18). I beh chiau3 in e5 kiaN5-choe3 lai5 po3-eng3, siu7-khi3 I e5 tui3-tek8, po3-eng3 I e5 kiu5-siu5; tui3 cheng3 hai2-su7 kiaN5 po3-eng3.  19). An2-ni lang5 tui3 jit8-loh8 e5 sou2-chai7 beh keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5; tui3 jit8-chhut e5 toe7-hng, iah8 beh keng3-ui3 I e5 eng5-kng; in-ui7 I beh lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 kin2-lau5 e5 ho5-chui2, si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 khi3 sou2 chhui-pek--e5.  20). Beh u7 chit8-ui7 kiu3-siok8 e5 chu2 lai5 kau3 Sek-an, iah8 kau3 Nga2-kok chok8-tiong li7-khui ke3-sit e5 lang5 hia; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lun7-kau3 Goa2, Goa2 kap in sou2 lip8 e5 iok chiu7-si7 an2-ni; Goa2 e5 Sin5 ti7 li2 e5 teng2-bin7--e5, Goa2 e5 oe7, Goa2 sou2 he7 ti7 li2 e5 chhui3--e5, bo5 beh li7-khui li2 e5 chhui3, bo5 li7-khui li2 e5 kiaN2-sun e5 chhui3, iah8 bo5 li7-khui li2 e5 kiaN2-kiaN2 sun-sun e5 chhui3, tui3-taN kau3 eng2-oan2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[60]	Khi2-lai5 ah, hoat-chhut kng; in-ui7 li2 e5 kng i2-keng kau3, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng hoat-hian7, chio3 ti7 li2 e5 teng2-bin7.  2). KhoaN3 ah, ou-am3 beh kham3 choan5-toe7, ou-ou am3-am3 jia-kham3 liat8-kok; chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hoat-hian7 chio3 li2, I e5 eng5-kng beh chhut-hian7 ti7 li2 e5 sin-chiuN7.  3). Liat8-kok beh lai5 chiu7-kun7 li2 e5 kng, kun-ong5 beh lai5 chiu7-kun7 li2 hoat-hian7 e5 toa7-kng.
	4). Li2 kiah8-bak8 khoaN3 si3-hng, in long2 chu7-chip8 lai5 li2 chia; li2 e5 cheng3-kiaN2 tui3 hng7-hng7 lai5, li2 e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 iah8 beh hou7 lang5 pho7--lai5.  5). Hit-si5 li2 khoaN3-kiN3 chiu7 u7 eng5-kng, li2 e5 sim toa7 gong5-ngiah8, toa7 khui-khoah; in-ui7 toa7-hai2 hong-seng7 e5 chai5-but8 beh choan2-tng2 lai5 kui li2, liat8-kok e5 chai5-po2 iah8 beh lai5 kui li2.  6). Kui-tin7 e5 lok8-to5, kap Bi2-tian5 i2-kip8 I2-hoat toaN-nia7 e5 lok8-to5, beh pian3-moa2 li2 e5 keng2-lai7; Si7-pa e5 cheng3-lang5 long2 beh kau3; beh toa3 ng5-kim ju2-hiuN lai5, iah8 beh po3-thoan5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5-siaN.  7). Ki-tat8 e5 iuN5-kun5 long2 beh chu7-chip8 kau3 li2 chia, Ni5-pai5-iok kang e5 mi5-iuN5 beh choe3 li2 e5 lou7-eng7, ti7 Goa2 e5 toaN5-teng2 beh tit-tioh8 chiap-lap8; Goa2 eng5-kng e5 chhu3, Goa2 beh eng5-kng--i.  8). Hiah-e5 pe--lai5 chhin-chhiuN7 hun5, koh chhin-chhiuN7 kap pe--lai5 i e5 siu7--e5, si7 chi7-chui7 ah?  9). Chiah e5 hai2-su7 beh theng3-hau7 Goa2; Tha-si e5 chun5-chiah beh choe3-thau5, chiong li2 e5 cheng3-kiaN2, lian5 in e5 kim-gun5, tui3 hng7-hng7 choe3 chit8-e7 toa3--lai5, long2 ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5, koh ui7-tioh8 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5, in-ui7 I i2-keng eng5-kng li2.
	10). Goa7-pang lang5 beh khi2 li2 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5, in e5 ong5 beh hok8-sai7 li2; Goa2 bat siu7-khi3 phah li2, taN beh si-un lin5-bin2 li2.  11). Li2 e5 siaN5-mng5 beh siong5-siong5 khui, jit8-mi5 bo5 koaiN, hou7 lang5 chiong liat8-kok e5 chai5-po2 toa3 lai5 kui li2, iah8 chiong in e5 kun-ong5 khan--lai5.  12). In-ui7 kiN3-na7 peh-siN3 kap kok m7 hok8-sai7 li2--e5 beh biat8-bo5; hiah e5 peh-siN3 beh choan5-jian5 hong-hoe3.  13). Li7-pa-lun3 e5 eng5-kng, chiu7-si7 chheng5-chhiu7, sam-chhiu7, ng5-iong5-chhiu7, long2 beh saN-kap kui li2, ui7-tioh8 beh chng-thaN7 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2; Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 Goa2 kha-tah8 e5 sou2-chai7 tit-tioh8 eng5-kng.  14). Peng5-sou3 khou2-chhou2 li2--e5, in e5 kiaN2-sun long2 beh kau3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 aN3-io; khoaN3-khin li2--e5 long2 beh ti7 li2 e5 kha-e7 kui7-pai3; in beh chheng li2 choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN5, choe3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5 e5 Sek-an.  15). Li2 cheng5 siu7 pang3-sak, siu7 iam3-ouN3, sim7-chi3 bo5 lang5 keng-ke3, taN Goa2 beh hou7 li2 piN3-choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 eng5-hoa5, chiaN5-choe3 lek8-tai7 e5 hi2-lok8.  16). Li2 beh chiah8 ban7-kok e5 lin, koh suh chiah e5 kun-ong5 e5 lin-thau5; chiu7 chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 li2 e5 Kiu3-chu2, si7 kiu3-siok8 li2 e5 Chu2, Nga2-kok e5 toa7 koan5-leng5--e5.  17). Goa2 beh toa3 kim lai5 thoe3 tang5, toa3 gun5 lai5 thoe3 thih, tang5 lai5 thoe3 chha5, thih lai5 thoe3 chioh8; iah8 beh eng7 ho5-peng5 choe3 li2 e5 koaN-tiuN2, eng7 kong-gi7 choe3 li2 e5 kam-tok.  18). Li2 e5 toe7-hng bo5 koh thiaN-kiN3 kiong5-po7, keng2-lai7 bo5 koh thiaN-kiN3 pha-hng hui2-biat8 e5 su7; li2 beh chheng li2 e5 chhiuN5 choe3 Chin2-kiu3, chheng li2 e5 mng5 choe3 O-lo2.  19). Jit8-thau5 bo5 koh choe3 li2 jit8--si5 e5 kng, geh8 iah8 bo5 koh hoat-kng chio3 li2; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh choe3 li2 eng2-oan2 e5 kng, li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh choe3 li2 e5 eng5-iau7.  20). Li2 e5 jit8-thau5 bo5 koh loh8, li2 e5 geh8 iah8 bo5 kiu-bo5--khi3; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh choe3 li2 eng2-oan2 e5 kng, li2 pi-ai e5 jit8 iah8 beng5-pek8 lah.  21). Li2 e5 peh-siN3 long2 chiaN5-choe3 gi7-lang5, eng2-oan2 tit-tioh8 toe7 choe3-giap8; si7 Goa2 sou2 cheng3 e5 chhiu7-chai, Goa2 e5 chhiu2 sou2-choe3--e5, hou7 Goa2 tit-tioh8 eng5-kng.  22). Chi3-soe3--e5 beh chiaN5-choe3 chit8-chheng, kek8 pi-bi5--e5 beh chiaN5-choe3 kiong5 e5 kok; Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chiau3 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 ki5, kin2-kin2 chiaN5 i.

[61]	Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 Sin5 lim5-kau3 goa2; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 iu5 boah goa2, hou7 goa2 thoan5 hok-im hou7 song3-hiong e5 lang5; chhe goa2 i-ho2 siong-sim e5 lang5, po3-ko3 siu7-liah8-e5 tit-tioh8 thau2-pang3, siu7-koaiN-e5 chhut kaN-lo5;  2). po3-ko3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoaN-hi2 e5 ni5, kap lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 po3-siu5 e5 jit8; an-ui3 it-chhe3 pi-ai e5 lang5;  3). ti7 Sek-an pi-ai e5 lang5 eng7 hoe-bo7 siuN2-su3 i, lai5 thoe3 he2-hu, hoaN-hi2 e5 iu5 lai5 thoe3 pi-ai, o-lo2 e5 saN lai5 thoe3 iu-chhiu5 e5 sim, hou7 in chheng-choe3 kong-gi7 e5 chhiu7, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chai--e5, lai5 hian2-beng5 ka-ki7 e5 eng5-kng.  4). In beh khi2-cho7 kou2-cha2 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7, kian3-lip8 cha2-cheng5 leng2-cheng7 e5 ui7-chhu3, ia7 beh siu-li2 pha-hng e5 siaN5, chiu7-si7 tai7-tai7 leng2-cheng7 e5 ui7-chhu3.  5). Goa7-bin7 lang5 beh khi2-lai5 kou3 lin2 e5 iuN5-kun5, goa7-pang lang5 beh ka7 lin2 choh-chhan5, chiau3-kou3 lin2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5.  6). Chong2-si7 lin2 beh chheng-choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 che3-si; lang5 beh chheng lin2 choe3 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 chhe-eng7; lin2 beh chiah8-eng7 liat8-kok e5 chai5-but8, tit-tioh8 in e5 eng5-kng lai5 khoa-khau2.  7). Lin2 beh tit-tioh8 ka-pe7 e5 hok-khi3 lai5 thoe3 sou2 siu7 e5 kian3-siau3; in beh hoaN-hi2 ti7 in sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 hun7-giah8, lai5 thoe3 sou2 siu7 e5 leng5-jiok8; sou2-i2 ti7 keng2-lai7 beh tit-tioh8 ka-pe7 e5 san2-giap8, eng2-oan2 e5 khoai3-lok8 beh kui hou7 in.  8). In-ui7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ai3 kong-peng5, oan3-hun7 put-gi7 e5 chhiuN2-kiap; Goa2 beh chiau3 seng5-sit8 po3-eng3 in, ia7 beh kap in lip8 eng2-oan2 e5 iok.  9). In e5 hou7-e3 beh ti7 liat8-kok-tiong hou7 lang5 bat i, in e5 kiaN2-sun ti7 cheng3 peh-siN3-tiong ia7 si7 an2-ni; kiN3-na7 khoaN3-kiN3 in--e5 beh jin7 in, si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok e5 hou7-e3.
	10). Goa2 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa toa7-toa7 hoaN-hi2, goa2 e5 sim-sin5 in-ui7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiu7 khoai3-lok8; in-ui7 I eng7 chin2-kiu3 choe3 saN ka7 goa2 chheng7, eng7 kong-gi7 choe3 phau3 ka7 goa2 moa, chhin-chhiuN7 sin-kiaN2-sai3 ti3 sui2 e5 bo7, koh chhin-chhiuN7 sin-niu5 chng-thaN7 po2-mih8.  11). In-ui7 thou2-toe7 chaiN2-iuN7 hou7 pah-hang7 e5 gou7-kak puh-ge5, hng5 chaiN2-iuN7 hou7 sou2-cheng3--e5 hoat-siN, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 beh an2-ni hou7 kong-gi7 kap o-lo2 hoat-siN ti7 ban7-kok e5 bin7-cheng5.

[62]	Goa2 in-ui7 Sek-an e5 ian5-kou3 tek-khak bo5 cheng7-cheng7, in-ui7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 ian5-kou3 tek-khak bo5 hioh-khun3, tit8-kau3 i e5 kong-gi7 chhin-chhiuN7 kng teh hoat-chhut, i e5 chin2-kiu3 chhin-chhiuN7 teng teh toh8.  2). Liat8-kok beh khoaN3 li2 e5 kong-gi7, liat8-ong5 beh khoaN3 li2 e5 eng5-kng; li2 beh tit-tioh8 chheng-hou sin e5 mia5, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhin-chhui3 sou2 chheng-hou--e5.  3). Li2 beh ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2-tiong choe3 sui2 e5 ong5-bo7, ti7 li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 chhiu2-chiuN2 choe3 bian2-liu5.  4). Li2 bo5 koh chheng-choe3 Siu7-khi3-sak--e5, li2 e5 toe7 ia7 bo5 koh chheng-choe3 Pha-hng--e5; li2 beh chheng-choe3 Goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5, li2 e5 toe7 ia7 beh chheng-choe3 U7 tiong7-hu--e5; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoaN-hi2 li2, li2 e5 toe7 ia7 beh choe3 u7 tiong7-hu--e5.  5). In-ui7 chhin-chhiuN7 siau3-lian5 lang5 chhoa7 chai7-sek-lu2, li2 e5 peh-siN3 ia7 beh an2-ni chhoa7 li2; chhin-chhiuN7 sin-kiaN2-sai3 hoaN-hi2 sin-niu5, li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ia7 beh an2-ni hoaN-hi2 li2.
	6). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, Goa2 ti7 li2 e5 siaN5-teng2 siat-lip8 siu2-bang7-e5, in thong-jit8 thong-mi5 bo5 cheng7-cheng7; khun2-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5,  7). lin2 m7-thang hioh-khun3, ia7 m7-thang hou7 I hioh-khun3, tit8-kau3 I kian3-lip8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, hou7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 chiaN5-choe3 thang o-lo2--e5.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa ki2 ka-ki7 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 kap toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2-kut chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 tek-khak bo5 koh chiong li2 e5 gou7-kak hou7 li2 e5 tui3-tek8 choe3 chiah8-mih8, goa7-pang lang5 ia7 bo5 koh lim li2 sou2 tioh8-boa5 lai5 tit-tioh8 e5 sin-chiu2;  9). tok8-tok8 hiah e5 siu-koah--e5 beh chiah8 i, lai5 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa; hiah e5 siu-khioh--e5 beh ti7 Goa2 seng3-sou2 e5 iN7-lai7 lim i.
	10). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 siaN5-mng5 keng-ke3, pi7-pan7 peh-siN3 e5 lou7; thun7-koaiN5 thun7-koaiN5 toa7-lou7; tu5--khi3 chioh8-thau5; ui7-tioh8 liat8-kok khia7 toa7-ki5.  11). KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa bat thoan5-po3 kau3 toe7-kek8, lin2 tioh8 ka7 Sek-an e5 peh-siN3 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, li2 e5 chin2-kiu3 lai5 lah; khoaN3 ah, I e5 siuN2-su3 ti7 I hia, I e5 po3-tap ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5.  12). Lang5 beh chheng in choe3 Seng3 e5 peh-siN3, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 siok8-hoe5 e5; li2 ia7 beh chheng-choe3 Chhe7--tioh8--e5, Bo5 siu7-pang3-sak e5 siaN5.

[63]	Chit-e5 tui3 I2-tong lai5, tui3 Pho-su7-lah8 kau3, chheng7 ang5-saN, i-chiuN5 hang5-ngou2, u7 toa7 khui3-lat8 toa7-pou7 teh kiaN5 e5, si7 chi7-chui7 ah? chiu7-si7 Goa2, si7 chiau3 kong-gi7 kong2-oe7, u7 toa7 khui3-lat8 oe7 kiaN5 chin2-kiu3--e5.  2). Li2 e5 i-chiuN5 chaiN2-iuN7 u7 ang5-sek, Li2 e5 i-hok8 chaiN2-iuN7 chhin-chhiuN7 tah8 chiu2-khut--e5 ah?  3). Goa2 ka-ki7 chit8-e5 tah8 chiu2-khut; cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan bo5 chit8-lang5 kap Goa2 ti7-teh; Goa2 siu7-khi3 tah8 in, toa7 siu7-khi3 thun2-tah8 in; in e5 huih choaN7 ti7 Goa2 e5 saN, koh bak la5-sam5 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 i-chiuN5.  4). In-ui7 po3-siu5 e5 jit8 ti7 goa2 e5 sim-lai7, Goa2 kiu3-siok8 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 ni5 i2-keng kau3.  5). Goa2 khoaN3, ia7 bo5 pang-chan7--e5, Goa2 gong5-ngiah8 in-ui7 bo5 u7 hu5-chhi5--e5; sou2-i2 Goa2 ka-ki7 e5 chhiu2 ka7 Goa2 kiaN5 chin2-kiu3; Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 ka7 Goa2 hu5-chhi5.  6). Goa2 siu7-khi3 tah8 liat8-pang, toa7 siu7-khi3 hou7 in chui3-chui3; hou7 in e5 huih lau5 ti7 toe7--nih.
	7). Goa2 beh chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa it-chhe3 sou2 siuN2-su3 lan2--e5, kong2-khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chu5-ai3 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5-siaN, kap I ng3 I2-sek-liat8 ke sou2 si e5 toa7-un, chiu7-si7 chiau3 I e5 lin5-bin2 kap hong-seng7 e5 chu5-ai3 siuN2-su3 in--e5.  8). In-ui7 I kong2, In chin-chiaN3 si7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, bo5 kiaN5 hu-ke2 e5 kiaN2-ji5; an2-ni I chiu7 choe3 in e5 Kiu3-chu2.  9). Ti7 in it-chhe3 e5 khou2-lan7-tiong I ia7 tang5 siu7 khou2-lan7, koh I bin7-cheng5 e5 su3-chia2  chin2-kiu3 in; I eng7 chu5-ai3 kap lin5-bin2 kiu3-siok8 in; ti7 kou2-cha2 e5 jit8 siong5-siong5 pho7 in, kui5 in.  10). Chong2-si7 in poe7-gek8, hou7 I e5 Seng3-sin5 iu-bun7; I chiu7 hoan2-tng2 choe3 in e5 tui3-tek8, pun2-sin lai5 kong-kek in.  11). Peh-siN3 chiu7 ki3-tit kou2-cha2 Mou5-se e5 jit8, kong2, Chhoa7 in kap I choan5-kun5 e5 bok8-chia2 tui3 hai2--nih chhut--lai5 e5, ti7 toh-loh8 ah? chiong I seng3 e5 Sin5 he7 ti7 in tiong-kan--e5, ti7 toh-loh8 ah?  12). hou7 I eng5-kng e5 chhiu2 ti7 Mou5-se e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 kiaN5-tang7? ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 chiong chui2 pun-khui, beh ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 lip8 eng2-oan2 e5 mia5?  13). chhoa7 in keng-ke3 hai2-tiong chhin-chhiuN7 be2 kiaN5 ti7 khong3-ia2, hou7 in bo5 tioh8-tak--e5, ti7 toh-loh8 ah?  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 Sin5 hou7 in tit-tioh8 an-hioh, chhin-chhiuN7 cheng-siN loh8-kau3 soaN-kha; an2-ni Li2 iah8 chhoa7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3, ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 kian3-lip8 eng5-kng e5 mia5.  15). Kiu5 Li2 tui3 thiN aN3-loh8 khoaN3, tui3 Li2 seng3-kiat eng5-kng e5 sou2-chai7 khoaN3; Li2 e5 jiat8-sim kap Li2 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 sou2-choe3 ti7 toh-loh8 ah? Li2 thiaN3-thang3 e5 sim-tng5 kap lin5-bin2, tui3 goa2 theng5-chi2.  16). A-pek-lah8-han2 sui-jian5 m7-bat goan2, I2-sek-liat7 m7-jin7 goan2, chong2-si7 Li2 si7 goan2 e5 pe7; Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 si7 goan2 e5 pe7, tui3 ban7-kou2 i2-lai5, Li2 e5 mia5 chheng-choe3 kiu3-siok8 goan2 e5 Chu2.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 siaN2-su7 hou7 goan2 kiaN5 chho3, li7-khui Li2 e5 lou7, hou7 goan2 e5 sim ngi7, bo5 keng3-ui3 Li2 ah? Kiu5 Li2 ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, ui7 Li2 e5 san2-giap8 chi-chai3 e5 ian5-kou3, to3-tng2--lai5.  18). Li2 seng3 e5 peh-siN3 put-ko3 chiam7-si5 tit-tioh8 chit e5 san2-giap8; goan2 e5 tui3-tek8 i2-keng thun2-tah8 Li2 e5 seng3-sou2.  19). Goan2 chhin-chhiuN7 tui3 kou2-cha2 be7-bat hou7 Li2 ti7-li2 e5 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 be7-bat eng7 Li2 e5 mia5 lai5 chheng-hou--e5.

[64]	Goan7 Li2 lih8-khui thiN lai5 kang3-lim5, hou7 chiah e5 soaN tin2-tang7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5,  2). (chhin-chhiuN7 he2 sio ta-chha5, chhin-chhiuN7 he2 hou7 chui2 kun2), hou7 Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 chai Li2 e5 mia5, hou7 liat8-kok ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.  3). Li2 bat kiaN5 thang kiaN e5 su7, goan2 sou2 bo5 phah-sng3, hit-si5 Li2 kang3-lim5, chiah e5 soaN tin2-tang7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  4). Tui3 kou2-cha2 i2-lai5 lang5 be7-bat thiaN-kiN3, hi7-khang be7-bat thiaN-kiN3, bak8-chiu be7-bat khoaN3-kiN3, ti7 Li2 i2-goa7 u7 sim2-mih8 Siong7-te3, ui7-tioh8 theng3-hau7 i e5 lang5 kiaN5 tai7-chi3.  5). Li2 ngia5-chih hit-e5 hoaN-hi2 kiaN5-gi7, kap ki3-liam7 Li2 e5 to7-lou7 e5 lang5; khoaN3 ah, Li2 bat siu7-khi3, goan2 bat hoan7-choe7, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni i2-keng ku2, goan2 iau2 oe7 tit-tioh8 kiu3 mah?  6). Goan2 long2 chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5, sou2-u7 e5 gi7 long2 chhin-chhiuN7 u3-oe3 e5 saN; goan2 long2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-hioh8 chiam7-chiam7 ta--khi3; goan2 e5 choe7-koa3 chhin-chhiuN7 hong ka7 goan2 chhe--khi3.  7). Koh bo5 lang5 kiu5-kio3 Li2 e5 mia5, bo5 lang5 chhut-lat8 khiN5-tiau5 Li2; in-ui7 Li2 ng-bin7 m7-khoaN3 goan2, hou7 goan2 in-ui7 goan2 e5 choe7-koa3 ti3-kau3 siau-bo5.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, taN Li2 iu5-goan5 si7 goan2 e5 pe7; goan2 si7 thou5, Li2 si7 sio-hui5 sai-hu7, goan2 long2 si7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2-cho7--e5.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 m7-thang toa7 siu7-khi3, iah8 m7-thang eng2-oan2 ki3-liam7 choe7-koa3; kiu5 Li2 aN3-loh8 lai5 khoaN3, goan2 long2 si7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3.  10). Li2 chiah e5 seng3-siaN5 piN3-choe3 khong3-ia2, Sek-an piN3-choe3 khong3-ia2; Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiaN5-choe3 pha-hng.  11). Goan2 seng3 koh sui2 e5 chhu3, chiu7-si7 goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 o-lo2 Li2 e5 sou2-chai7, hou7 he2 sio-lio--khi3; goan2 sou2 him-bou7--e5 long2 hong-hoe3.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, u7 chiah e5 su7, Li2 iau2 jim2-oe7-tiau5 mah? Li2 iau2 cheng7-cheng7 hou7 goan2 chhim-chhim siu7 khou2-lan7 mah?

[65]	Peng5-sou3 be7 bat mng7 Goa2--e5, taN Goa2 hou7 in mng7; be7 u7 chhe7 Goa2--e5, taN Goa2 hou7 in tu2-tioh8; be7 u7 kiu5-kio3 Goa2 e5 mia5--e5, Goa2 tui3 in kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia, Goa2 ti7 chia.  2). Goa2 thong-jit8 chhun-chhiu2 ng3 hiah-e5 poe7-gek8 e5 peh-siN3; in chhut-chai7 ka-ki7 e5 i3-su3, kiaN5 m7-ho2 e5 lou7.  3). Chiah e5 peh-siN3 siong5-siong5 tng-bin7 jia2-tioh8 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3; ti7 hng5-tiong hian3-che3, ti7 chng-hia7-teng2 sio-hiuN;  4). khia7-khi2 ti7 bong7-lai7, hioh ti7 un2-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7, chiah8 ti-bah, in e5 khi3-ku7-lai7 u7 kho2-ouN3 e5 mih8 choe3 thng;  5). koh tui3 lang5 kong2, Li2 tioh8 khia7-khui, m7-thang oa2-kun7 goa2, in-ui7 goa2 pi2 li2 khah-seng3; chiah e5 lang5 si7 Goa2 phiN7-khang-tiong e5 he2-hun, si7 thong-jit8 teh-toh8 e5 he2.  6). KhoaN3 ah, che long2 sia2 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5; Goa2 bo5-beh cheng7-cheng7, tek-khak beh kiaN5 po3-eng3, po3-eng3 ti7 in e5 heng-cheng5.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, In-ui7 lin2 e5 choe7-ok, kap lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 choe7-ok, ti7 soaN--nih sio-hiuN, ti7 nia2-teng2 siat-tok8 Goa2; sou2-i2 Goa2 beh chiau3 in peng5-sou3 sou2-kiaN5--e5, po3-eng3 ti7 in e5 heng-cheng5.
	8). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 phu5-to5-pha-lai7 tu2-tioh8 u7 sin-chiu2, u7 lang5 kong2, M7-thang hui2-hoai7, in-ui7 u7 hok-khi3 ti7 hit lai7-bin7, Goa2 in-ui7 Goa2 chiah e5 lou5-pok8 e5 ian5-kou3, iah8 beh chiau3 an2-ni lai5 kiaN5, bo5 beh it-chin7 biat8 in.  9). Goa2 beh tui3 Nga2-kok e5 tiong-kan chhoa7-chhut hou7-e3, tui3 Iu5-tai7 e5 tiong-kan chhoa7-chhut seng5-chiap Goa2 e5 cheng3-soaN--e5; Goa2 keng2 e5 peh-siN3 beh seng5-chiap--i, Goa2 chiah e5 lou5-pok8 beh ti7-hia khia7-khi2.  10). Sa-lun5 beh chiaN5-choe3 chhi7-iuN5 e5 sou2-chai7, A-kat e5 soaN-kok beh chiaN5-choe3 gu5-kun5 to2 teh-khun3 e5 sou2-chai7; long2 si7 beh hou7 chhe7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 sou2 tit-tioh8.  11). Chong2-si7 lin2 chiah-e5 pang3-sak Ia5-ho5-hoa, boe7-ki3-tit Goa2 e5 seng3-soaN, ka7 Ka-tek pan7-toh, ka7 Bi2-ni5 koan3-tian7 tiau-ho5 e5 chiu2--e5;  12). Goa2 beh chu3-tiaN7 lin2 kui ti7 to-e7, long2 beh khut-sin siu7-thai5; in-ui7 Goa2 kio3, lin2 bo5 in3, Goa2 kong2-oe7, lin2 bo5 thiaN-than3; hoan2-tng2 kiaN5 Goa2 bak8-chiu-tiong khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2 e5, keng2 Goa2 sou2 bo5 hoaN-hi2--e5.
	13). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 beh chiah8, lin2 beh iau; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 beh lim, lin2 beh chhui3-ta; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 beh hoaN-hi2, lin2 beh kian3-siau3.  14). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8, in-ui7 sim khoai3-lok8, chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, lin2 beh in-ui7 sim iu-chhiu5 ai-khau3, koh in-ui7 sim-sin5 iu-siong ai-hau2.  15). Lin2 beh lau5 lin2 e5 mia5, hou7 Goa2 keng2 e5 peh-siN3 ki2 i lai5 chiu3-chou2; Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh thai5 lin2; leng7-goa7 eng7 sin e5 mia5 chheng I e5 lou5-pok8.  16). An2-ni ti7 toe7-chiuN7 ui7 ka-ki7 kiu5 hok-khi3-e5, beh ng3 chin-sit8 e5 Siong7-te3 kiu5 hok-khi3; ti7 toe7-chiuN7 lai5 chiu3-choa7--e5, beh ki2 chin-sit8 e5 Siong7-te3 lai5 chiu3-choa7; in-ui7 cha2-cheng5 e5 hoan7-lan7 i2-keng boe7-ki3-tit, iah8 tui3 Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 khng3-bat8.
	17). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 chhong3-cho7 sin-thiN sin-toe7, i2-cheng5 e5 su7 bo5 koh ki3-liam7, iah8 bo5 koh tui-siuN7.  18). Lin2 tioh8 in-ui7 Goa2 sou2 chhong3-cho7--e5 lai5 eng2-oan2 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8; in-ui7 Goa2 chhong3-cho7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 choe3 hoaN-hi2--e5, chhong3-cho7 i e5 peh-siN3 choe3 khoai3-lok8--e5.  19). Goa2 beh in-ui7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 lai5 hoaN-hi2, in-ui7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 lai5 khoai3-lok8; ki5-tiong tek-khak bo5 koh thiaN-kiN3 thi5-khau3 e5 siaN, kap ai-hau2 e5 siaN.  20). Ki5-tiong tek-khak bo5 u7 kui2-jit8-a2 si2-khi3 e5 eN-a2, iah8 bo5 u7 he3-siu7 bo5 moa2-chiok e5 lau7-lang5; in-ui7 chit8-pah he3 si2--e5, iau2-sng3 si7 gin2-na2, chit8-pah he3 si2 e5 choe7-jin5, iau2-ku2 si7 siu7 chiu3-chou2 e5.  21). In beh khi2-chhu3, ka-ki7 khia7-khi2; chai-cheng3 phu5-to5-hng5 lai5 chiah8 i e5 ke2-chi2.  22). In bo5 beh khi2-cho7, hou7 pat8-lang5 khia7 i; in bo5 beh chai-cheng3, hou7 pat8-lang5 chiah8 i; in-ui7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 jit8-chi2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7 e5 jit8-chi2; Goa2 keng2 e5 peh-siN3 chhin-chhiuN7 tioh8-boa5 tit-tioh8-e5 beh ku2-tng5 hiong2-siu7 i.  23). In tek-khak bo5 khang-khang tioh8-boa5, sou2-siN--e5 iah8 bo5 tu2-tioh8 chai-hai7; in-ui7 in long2 si7 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok--e5 e5 hou7-e3, in e5 kiaN2-sun iah8 beh kap i u7-hun7.  24). In iau2-be7 kiu5-kio3, Goa2 chiu7 in3 i, tu2-tu2 teh kong2 e5 si5, Goa2 chiu7 thiaN i.  25). Chhai5-long5 beh kap iuN5-ko saN-kap chiah8, sai beh chiah8 chhau2 chhin-chhiuN7 gu5; thou5-hun2 beh choe3 choa5 e5 chiah8-mih8.  Ti7 Goa2 e5 seng3-soaN pian3-toe7, long2 bo5 sun2-siong, bo5 chan5-hai7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[66]	Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, ThiN si7 Goa2 e5 cho7-ui7, toe7 si7 Goa2 e5 kha-tah8-i2; lin2 beh ka7 Goa2 khi2 sim2-mih8 ho7 e5 chhu3? sim2-mih8 ho7 e5 sou2-chai7, si7 choe3 Goa2 an-hioh e5 toe7-hng ah?  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Chiah-e5 long2 si7 Goa2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 chhong3-cho7 e5, sou2-i2 chiah-e5 chiu7 long2 u7; chong2-si7 Goa2 sou2 khoaN3-kou3--e5, chiu7-si7 khiam-hu sim thong3-hoe2, in-ui7 Goa2 e5 oe7 lai5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah e5 lang5.  3). Thai5-gu5 bo5 koh-iuN7 thai5-lang5; hian3 iuN5 bo5 koh-iuN7 kong3-chih8 kau2 am7-kun2; hian3 le2-mih8 bo5 koh-iuN7 hian3 ti-huih; sio ju2-hiuN bo5 koh-iuN7 o-lo2 ngou2-siong7; in keng2 ka-ki7 e5 to7-lou7, sim hoaN-hi2 in kho2-ouN3 e5 su7.  4). Goa2 iah8 keng2 be5-hek8 in e5 su7, hou7 in sou2 kiaN-hiaN5--e5 lim5-kau3 in; in-ui7 Goa2 kio3, bo5 lang5 in3; Goa2 kong2-oe7, in bo5 thiaN-than3; hoan2-tng2 kiaN5 Goa2 bak8-chiu-tiong khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2--e5, keng2 Goa2 sou2 bo5 hoaN-hi2--e5.
	5). Lin2 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lai5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah e5 lang5, tioh8 thiaN I e5 oe7; Lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7 oan3-hun7 lin2, in-ui7 Goa2 e5 mia5 kek-tiok8 lin2--e5, bat kong2, Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tit-tioh8 eng5-kng, hou7 goan2 tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3 lin2 e5 hoaN-hi2; chong2-si7 in beh tu2-tioh8 kian3-siau3.  6). U7 soan-hoa e5 siaN tui3 siaN5-lai7 chhut, u7 siaN tui3 tian7-lai7 chhut, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa po3-eng3 I e5 tui3-tek8 e5 siaN.  7). Sek-an iau2-be7 tu2-tioh8 siN-kiaN2 e5 kan-khou2, chiu7 seng-san2; iau2-be7 chai thang3-thiaN3, chiu7 siN ta-pou-kiaN2.  8). Chhin-chhiuN7 chit-ho7 su7, chi7-chui7 bat thiaN-kiN3? chiah e5 su7 chi7-chui7 bat khoaN3-kiN3 ah? kok kiam2-oe7 chit8-jit8 lai5 siN? peh-siN3 kiam2-oe7 tiap-a2-ku2 lai5 chhut-si3? in-ui7 Sek-an chit8-e7 tu2-tioh8 siN-kiaN2 e5 kan-khou2, chiu7 siN kiaN2-ji5.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 i2-keng hou7 i lim5-phun5, kiam2-bo5 hou7 i siN-chhut mah? Li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kong2, Goa2 hou7 lang5 siN-kiaN2--e5, kiam2 koaiN-bat8 i e5 thai mah?
	10). Lin2 chiah-e5 thiaN3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2--e5, tioh8 kap i tang5 khoai3-lok8, ui7 i hoaN-hi2; lin2 ui7-tioh8 i pi-ai--e5, taN tioh8 kap i hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8.  11). Ti3-kau3 lin2 thang suh i e5 an-ui3 e5 lin-thau5 lai5 tit-tioh8 pa2; hou7 lin2 tit-tioh8 i hong-seng7 e5 eng5-kng, chhin-chhiuN7 chhe7-tioh8 lin2, moa2-sim hoaN-hi2.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 peng5-an khui-khoah kau3 ti7 i, chhin-chhiuN7 kang-ho5; hou7 liat8-kok e5 eng5-kng kau3 ti7 i, chhin-chhiuN7 tiong3-moa2 e5 ho5; lin2 beh hiong2-siu7 i, lin2 beh tit-tioh8 pho7 ti7 sin-piN, io5 ti7 kha-thau5-u-teng2.  13). Chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 tit-tioh8 i e5 lau7-bu2 an-ui3--i, Goa2 iah8 beh an2-ni an-ui3 lin2; lin2 iah8 beh ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 tit-tioh8 an-ui3.  14). Lin2 khoaN3-kiN3, sim chiu7 khoai3-lok8; lin2 e5 kut beh tit-tioh8 lun7-tek8, chhin-chhiuN7 nng2-nng2 e5 chhau2 chit8-iuN7; koh Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 beh hian2-hian7 ti7 I e5 lou5-pok8; I iah8 beh siu7-khi3 I e5 tui3-tek8.  15). KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ti7 he2-tiong kang3-lim5, I e5 chhia chhin-chhiuN7 kng2-le5-hong, eng7 toa7 siu7-khi3 kiaN5 po3-eng3, eng7 he2-iam7 kiaN5 chek-hoat8.  16). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh eng7 he2 eng7 to kap it-chhe3 u7 hiat-khi3 e5 lang5 cheng-chian3, hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 thai5-si2-e5 choe7-choe7.  17). Hiah-e5 hun-piat choe3-seng3, chheng-khi3 ka-ki7--e5, chin3-jip8 ti7 hng5-lai7, kun-te3 hit tiong-kan chit8 e5 lang5 e5 au7-bin7, chiah8 ti-bah kap kho2-ouN3 e5 mih8 kap niau2-chhu2; in beh choe3 chit8-e7 biat8-bo5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	18). In-ui7 goa2 chai in e5 kiaN5-choe3 kap in e5 liam7-thau5; si5 kau3 Goa2 beh chu7-chip8 ban7 peh-siN3 ban7-chok8; in beh lai5, beh khoaN3 Goa2 e5 eng5-kng.  19). Goa2 beh siat ki3-ho7 ti7 in tiong-kan; to5-chau2--e5, Goa2 beh chhe in kau3 liat8-kok, chiu7-si7 kau3 Tha-si, Phou2-lek8, khui-keng e5 Lou7-tek, kap Thou2-pa, Nga2-oan5, kap peng5-sou3 be7 u7 thiaN-kiN3 Goa2 e5 mia5-siaN, be7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 e5 eng5-kng, hng7-hng7 e5 hai2-su7; in beh chiong Goa2 e5 eng5-kng thoan5-po3 ti7 liat8-kok-tiong.  20). In beh sang3 lin2 e5 cheng3 hiaN-ti7 tui3 liat8-kok-tiong to3--lai5, hou7 in u7-e5 khia5-be2, u7-e5 che7-chhia, che7-kio7, khia5-lo5, khia5 lok8-to5, kau3 Goa2 e5 seng3-soaN Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, choe3 le2-mih8 hian3-hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chhin-chhiuN7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 eng7 chheng-khi3 e5 khi3-ku7 toe2 le2-mih8, hian3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh tui3 in tiong-kan, chhu2 lang5 choe3 che3-si, choe3 Li7-bi7 lang5.  22). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, In-ui7 Goa2 sou2 cho7 e5 sin-thiN sin-toe7, ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tng5-tng5 ti7-teh; chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, lin2 e5 hou7-e3 kap lin2 e5 mia5-ji7, iah8 beh tng5-tng5 ti7-teh.  23). Tak8-pai2 tu2-tioh8 geh8 e5 chhoe-it, tak8-pai2 tu2-tioh8 an-hioh-jit8, kiN3-na7 u7 hiat-khi3--e5, beh kau3 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 kui7-pai3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  24). In beh chhut-khi3 khoaN3 hiah e5 poe7-gek8 Goa2 e5 lang5 e5 sin-si; in-ui7 in e5 thang5 boe7 si2, in e5 he2 boe7 hoa; kiN3-u7 hiat-khi3--e5 long2 beh iam3-ouN3 in.
